O vos, tres chiers filz, je vos ai acomplit cest livre qui est li derriens de la science de medicine ensamble l’emplissement de lui, et ai fait la fin per ses expositions et par ses declarations.	O you, dear sons, I have completed this book which is the last of medical science along with its explanation and concluded by its expositions and declarations.
Et m’est venu en vision que je le vos acomplisse avec cest traitier, qui est partie de l’uevre de mains, c’est a savoir «cyrurgie».	And it came to me in a vision that I should complete this treatise with this chapter, which is part of the work on hands, namely 'Surgery'.
Et por ceu que l’uevre de mains est fortraite en nostre region et est etraingie dou tout en tout, si est perie li science et decopee, et n’est riens demorez de li fuers que les petites descriptions en livres des anciens que les mains ont muees.	And because the work on hands is practiced in our region and carried out everywhere, it has been neglected except for a few details from ancient books that describe what the hands have done.
Et de ceu est venue li error et li vanitez, et sont closes les ententions et est aloignie li science.	And thus arises error and folly, and understanding is closed off, and wisdom has departed.
Or me semble que je la vuel vivifier ensamble l’ordination de cest traitier selonc la voie d’exposition et de declaration et de l’abreviation;	 Or it seems to me that I want to bring this treatise to life, along with the order of its content according to exposure and clarification, and abbreviation.
et venrai ensamble les formes des ferremens de cautere, et des autres estrumens de l’uevre avec l’ajostement de la declaration et de preparation de li, sicom il est mestier.	 And I shall bring together the forms of instruments for cautery, and other tools of surgery with preparation and explanation as necessary.
Et por la raison de ceu que nuls boins maistres de mains n’est trovez en nostre tens, est li ars de medicine eslongié.	And because there are no good masters at hand in our times, the art of medicine has been abandoned.
Et covient celui qui s’en entremet sormonter en la science d’anathomie, si com Galiens dit, tant qu’il saiche la juement des menbres, et les formes et les conjunctions et les separations d’aus, et aient connissance des osses et des nerf et des brais et le nombre d’ous, et le demenement et des voines movans et des reposans, et dou leu de lor issue.	It is necessary for those who undertake this to ascend in the knowledge of anatomy, as Galen says, understanding the judgment of bones, their shapes and connections and separations, having knowledge of the bones and nerves and blood vessels and number of veins, and their movement and active and resting states.
Et por ceu dist Ypocras que li nons avec le non est mout, et avec l’uevre est poc;	 And thus Hippocrates states that nothing without the art is much, and little without it.
et meismement en l’art de main.	 And especially in the art of hands.
Nos vos disons en l’introite de cest livre que qui n’est conissans des choses devant dites, si se gart qu’il ne chiece en error et qu’il n’ocie les homes;	 We tell you in the introduction to this book that those who are not mindful of the aforementioned things should be careful lest they err and kill people.
ensi que j’ai veut maintes fois plusors de ces qui s’entremettent de ceste science et si s’abandonent sen science et sens experiment.	 Thus, I have often thought of those who involve themselves in this knowledge but abandon the theory and lose their experience.
Car je vis un fol mire qui copa I apostume de scrophules ou col d’une femme, et copa les arteres dou col;	 For I saw a mad physician who cut an abscess of scrofulous glands or throat in a woman and severed the arteries near the neck.
por coi tant de sanc issit hors que li femme cheit morte entre ses mains.	 for this is why so much blood flowed out that the woman died in her hands.
Et vis I autre mire qui traït une piere d’un home d’eaige, et li piere estoit grans;	 And I saw another physician treating a stone from a man's eye, and the stone was large;
si emporta avec li une piece de la vessie, et fut mors li hons dedens III jors.	 if he took with him a part of the bladder, and he died within three days.
Et je i avoie ja esteit apelez por lou traire, et vis la disposition dou malaide et la grandor de la piere, et soi bien s’on lou tailloit il en morroit.	And I had already been called upon to treat it, and I saw the condition of the patient and the size of the stone, and if he was to be cut open, he would surely die from it.
Et vis I autre mire qui prist en cure I duc de nostre terre qui avoit la jambe brisie, et avec la briseure ot plaie;	 And I saw another physician who took care of a duke from our land who had a broken leg, and with the break there was an open wound;
et li mires plains d’ignorance estraint la brisure sus la plaie as esteles par fort lieure, et ne lassa a la plaie point de xalain, et le lassa ensi I termine;	 and the ignorant physician pushed the break onto the wound without proper alignment, and did not let it heal properly, leaving it that way for so long.
et li comanda qu’il ne la desliast mie;	 And he commands that it shall not be dislocated again;
et demora ensi que li jambe fut toute enflee et li piez et vint a perdition.	 and remain thus so the leg becomes completely paralyzed, and the fingers too, leading to loss.
Je fuis apelez por venir a lui, et me hastai por venir deslier la jambe;	 I come here called upon him, and hurried to dislocate his leg;
et quant je l’oi desloie si fut em pais et ne sentit point de dolor.	 and when I did dislocate it, he became at peace and felt no pain.
Mais toute voie li corruptions estoit ja confermee ou membre, et ne la poi saner;	 But in any case the contamination was already confirmed or limb, and could not be cured;
et ne cessa li corrution d’aler par le membre tant que li membres fut dou tout perdus.	 And the contamination ceased to spread through the member until the entire limb was lost.
Et vis .i. autre mire qui effondra .i. apostume enchancreit, et puis enflama per le malice de sa signorie.	And behold I see another physician who fells an encrusted abscess, which then inflames due to the spite of his lordship.
Car chancre, quant il est purs d’umor melancolique, ne covient mie qu’on i(l) touche de fer s’il n’est en teil leu c’on puisse toute oster ce que est corrumpus.	For cancer, when it is filled with melancholic humors, does not need to be touched with iron unless in part its location allows for the removal of what is corrupted.
Et por ceu, treschier filz, vos est besoig que vos sachiez que oevre de mains est devisee en II divisions:	 And therefore, dear son, you must know that the work of hands is divided into two parts:
c’est asavoir, huevre ou il a peril en plusors dispositions;	 namely, where there is danger in various conditions;
et je mostrerai en chescun leu de cest livre ou il a paour et peril.	 And I will show, at each place of this book, where there is fear and danger.
Por coi il est besoig que vos vos en gardez, si que li fol mire ne puissent mal parler de vos.	 For that's why you must guard yourselves well, so the foolish may not speak ill of you.
Si prenez vos armes en cusenson, et entreprenez vos malaides legierement et fermement, et usez de la millor voie si que per la graice de Deu vos venez a salut et soiez loez;	 If you take your arms in consideration and begin treating the illnesses easily yet firmly, using the best method for by God's grace to achieve health and be praised.
et lassiez les maladies espoantables de grief saniteit;	 and let the hopeful diseases bring about great health. (Note: This line may not make perfect sense in English as it was probably a general proverb or sentiment meant to encourage
et ostez vos armes de ceu que vos fait douter, et aiez foit en vos si que vos puissiez venir de cestui monde a l’autre de gloire.	 and take up your arms where you find doubt, and have faith within yourself that you may come from this world to the other of glory. (This line is also not perfectly translatable but gives an encouraging sentiment about having faith in oneself.)
Galiens dist en aucuns de ses amonestemens:	 Galien speaks in some of his warnings:
«Ne prenez mie en cure male maladie, que vos ne soiez apelez fol mire.	 "Do not treat illnesses poorly, lest you be called mad doctors.
» J’ai deviseit cest traitier selonc III chapitres.	 "I have devised this treatise according to three chapters.
Li premiers chapitres est des cauteres de feu et dé cauteres de medicine ague, et est li chapitres ordenez de lou chief jusques as piez;	 The first chapters are about fire and medical cauldrons of water, and the chapters are ordered from the head to the feet.
et des formes des estrumens, et des ferremens de cautere, et de tout ceu qui est necessaire en l’ueuvre.	 And of forms of tumors, and iron instruments for cauterization, and all that is necessary in the work.
Li secons chapitres si est de taillier et de percier, et des ventouses et des plaies, et des estractions des saiettes, et des semblans choses;	 The second chapter concerns cutting and piercing, and cupping and wounds, and arrow extraction, and such matters.
et est li chapitres ordenez et les formes des estrumens.	 And it is the ordered chapter on tumor forms.
Li tiers chapitres est de restorer les dislocations et des torcions, et des semblans choses;	 The third chapter is about restoring dislocations and twists, and such matters.
et est ordeneiz des lou chief jusc’as piez, et des formes des estrumens.	 And it is ordered from the head to the feet, and on tumor forms.
Ainsois que nos nos remembriens de l’uevre, il covient que je die la qualiteit de l’aide et dou nuisement de chescune complexion.	So we shall remember our work, it is necessary that I tell the quality of help and the harm of each composition.
Je dis que li qualiteis de l’aide, et dou nuisement, est li plus longe parole et subtilz science et li secrez reponus;	 I say that the quality of the aid, and its harm, is the longest word and subtle science and hidden remedy.
et de ceu parlerent li plusors des saiges, et s’acorderent a ceu;	 and what many wise men speak, they agree on this.
et me soffisent poc lor paroles, car je redous la longesce.	 And I am troubled by their few words, for I will regain strength.
Je dis que cautere aide universement a toute complexion ou il a matiere, fuer que II complexions:	 I say that cauterization helps with all constitutions or matters where it is applied, both of the humors.
c’est a savoir complexion chaude sens matere, et complexion seche sens matere.	 That is to say, hot temperament refers to matter, and dry temperament also refers to matter.
En complexion chaude et seche ensamble matiere, deviserent aucun et dirent que cautere i est grans aide;	 In the combined hot and dry temperaments with regard to matter, they converse and say that cauterization is of great help.
et li autre dirent le contraire:	 and the other says the opposite:
que cautere ne vaut a maladie que vient de chalor et de sechour.	 that cauterization does not help with diseases arising from heat and dryness.
Car li nature dou feu si est chaude, et ne doit mie estre cureiz de chaude maladie par chalor, ne per sechour;	 Because the nature of fire is hot, and it should not be treated with hot medicine due to heat, nor dryness alone.
et dist cil qui dist lou contraire que cautere fait grant aide a maladie chaude et seche que vient en cors des homes.	 And those who say the opposite assert that cauterebe greatly helps diseases of heat and dryness arising in men's bodies.
Car quant tu comperes le cors de l’ome et sa moistor a la complexion dou feu, tu trueves le cors froit.	When you examine the body of the person and their moisture with the fiery temperament, you find the body to be cold.
Et je m’acorde a ceste parole.	And I agree with this statement.
Car je l’ai troveit aucune fois per experiment.	For I have found it no time through experimentation.
Et toute voie, ne s’en entremette mie fuers que cil qui l’a esproveit, et qui conoit par lonc usaige le chapistre des cauteres, et la diversiteit des complexions des homes, et les dispositions et les causes de lor maladies, et les sorvenues et l’espaice dou tens;	 And in any case, it should only be attempted by those who have experience and know well the art of cauterization, the diversity of human constitutions, their dispositions and causes of diseases, as well as incidents and duration over time.
des autres complexions n’avons nos mie paour, meismement em maladies froides et moistes.	 We have no fear for other constitutions, especially those with cold and damp illnesses.
Et tuit li mire s’asemblerent et s’acorderent au cautere.	And all the healers gathered and agreed on the treatment.
Et sachiez, filz, que cautere ensamble feu si est des secrez des cures, et de plus grant bonteit que cautere de medicine ardant.	And know this, my child, that fire cautery is a secret of the cure, and even greater beneficence than burning medicinal cautery.
Car li feus est simples, et ne vient mie fuers que au membre qui est cuis, et ne nuit a autre membre se poc nom.	thed; Tap. ould that lesquilibtud: O.
Les medicines ardans vienent de membre a autre en aloignant, et font venir au membre maladies de grief sanation;	 Burning medicines move from one member to another by combining them, bringing severe healing diseases to the affected limb;
et par aventure ocit lou malaide.	 and sometimes it kills the patient.
Li feus por sa hautece et por la bonteit de sa substance ne fait mie ceu, s’il n’i a superfluiteit.	 The fire for its high temperature and the kindness of its nature does not do this, if there is no excess.
Et ceu vos ai je troveit par experiment et par la longesce dou servise et de l’estude que j’ai mis en l’art, et esteit sus la verteit des choses;	 And I have found this through experiment and the length of service and study that I have put into the art, regarding the truth of things.
et por ceu je m’escuse de la longesce de la parole, car il ne me plait mie que je vos oste le secreit qui est reponus ou feu, et la qualiteit de l’uevre, coment il deboute les maladies des cors, si com li philosophe le dit en demostrant;	 And so I excuse the length of my words, for it is not my desire to reveal to you the secrets contained within these pages and their explanations, as the philosopher demonstrates how they address diseases of the body.
or le recevez en vos pensees.	 Or receive them into your thoughts.
Et sachiez, fil, que il s’acorderent en quel tens doient estre faites les cauteres, et eslirent prientens.	And know, my son, when to perform the cauteries and praying lines.
Et je dis que cautere est covenable en tous tens, por ceu que li nuisemens sorvenans est desoz mis par l’aide dou cautere;	 And I say that caustery is suitable at all times, for the harm which occurs is removed by means of caustery.
et meismement se li cauteres est por dolors necessaires fors et hastans que ne puent atendre le tens que plus grans malice ne veigne au membre.	 and especially because caustery is necessary for sudden pains that cannot wait until the onset of greater illness in the limb.
Et n’i pensez onques, chier fil, si com font li fol mire;	 And never think as do fools, just as they are known to act.
car a la maladie qui est sanee par cautere n’a point de revenue;	 because the disease which is healed by caustery does not have a return.
et il le dient ensi;	 And he says thus;
mais il n’est mie si com il cuident, por ce que cauteres nen est que medicine qui mue la complexion, et seche les humors que sont cause de la dolor, et vaut mues que medicine por le hastement de sa valor, et por la vertut de son oevre et de sa signorie.	 But it is not as they think, because cautery is a remedy that changes the complexion and dries the humors causing pain, and it works more quickly than other medicines due to its potency and efficacy of its action and power.
Et possans chose est que li maladie viegne aucune fois selonc la complexion dou malaide et lou leu de la maladie et sa vertut;	 And some cause is that the disease comes at any time according to the disposition of the sick and their location and its nature.
et sont assemblees en lui les superfluitez par l’aquisition des viandes et des semblans choses, se ce n’est cauteres administrez em leu ou il ait poc de superfluitez et de moistor, si com cauteres de dens por la dolor, et les semblans choses, et teil dolor ne revient mie;	 And they are combined in him the excesses from acquiring meats and similar things, unless caustics are administered at the place where there is little excess and moisture, as with caustics for pain, and other such matters, so that the pain does not return.
mais ce avient poc.	 However, this happens rarely.
Et mout de gens n’entendent mie por coi cauteres est apelez li derriens de medecine, et c’est voir;	 And many people do not know why cauldrons are called the last of medicine, and that is true.
mais il ne croient mie que cauteres vaille aprés medicine, mais lor ententions est fause, et est cauteres li derriens de medicine por ceu que quant nos aministrons manieres de cures en aucune maladie et elles ne valent, adonc administrons nos le cautere, et il vaut.	 However, they do not believe that cauldrons are worth after medicines, but their understanding is false; cauldrons are the last of medicine because when we administer methods of treatment in any illness and they prove to be of no value, then we apply our cauldrons, which work.
Adonques apert bien que cauteres est li derriens de medicine, ne mie selonc l’entention des folz mires.	Then indeed cauterizations are the last of medicine, not according to the foolish beliefs of people.
Li ancien dirent que cauteres d’estrument d’or est muedres que de fer, et ne dirent ceu fuers que por la qualiteit de l’or et por la hautece de sa substance;	 The ancients said that a cauldron made of gold is more potent than one made of iron, and they claimed so not because it was a fork but due to the quality of the gold and its high value.
et dirent que li leus de cautere ne fait mie porriture, mais ceu n’est mie voir car je l’ai esprovei, et ai troveit que c’est voir en aucuns homes;	 and they said that the patient does not suffer deterioration from cauldrons, but this is indeed true as I have tested it myself, and found in some men.
et cauteres d’or vaut mues que de fer, si com il lou dirent.	 And gold cauteries are worth more than iron ones, as they have said.
Et toutevoie quant tu chaufes estrument d’or, tu ne seis mie quant il est chaus par la color de l’or, et s’est tantost refroidiez;	 Also when you heat a gold instrument, do not judge its temperature by the color of gold alone, as it cools quickly.
et s’on le chaufe trop;	 and if you overheat it;
si font au feu;	 If done with fire;
et ensi i a assez d’empechement.	 and thus there is enough obstruction.
Et por ce usons nos de cautere de feir que nos l’avons mues apparilliet a nostre oevre.	And therefore we use the iron cautery as we have found suitable for our work.
Or vos ai ordeneit cest chapitre des lou chief jusc’a piez, por ceu que li voie soit plus legiere a trover.	Or I have ordered this chapter from head to foot, so that the path may be easier to find.
dou cautere olivaire	Olive oil for anointing and healing purposes.
Cist cauteres vaut a moistor et a froidor sus lou cerveil, et en i a dous c’on fait par la cause d’une maladie qui est apelee «soda», et par la cause de maintes humors qui dessendent dou chief as eulz, et as oreilles, et por multitude de songes et dolor de dens et dolor de gorge, et meismement a toutes maladies qui vienent de froidor si com paralisie et sode et apoplexie et semblans maladies.	These cauteries are for moisture and cold on the brain; there are two that are done because of an illness called 'soda', and due to many humors descending from the head into the eyes, ears, causing a multitude of dreams and pain in the teeth and throat, as well as all diseases caused by cold such as paralysis, stroke, and similar afflictions.
Li forme de cest cautere si est que li malaides soit espurgiez par medicine solutive mondifiant le chief III nuis ou IIII, selonc ceu que li vertus et li eaige et li acostumance dou malaide le puet soffrir;	 The form of this cautery is such that the patient should be purged by a solutive medicine which modifies either III or IV chiefs, according to what the virtues and nature and customary tolerances of the patient can endure.
et puis fai rere lou chief dou malaide.	 and then address the head of the illness again.
Et puis le fai seoir croisiet entre tes mains, et mettre ses mains sor som peis;	 And then make it sit cross-legged between your hands and place its hands on some flat surface.
aprés met la racine de ta palme sus la racine de son neis entre ses II eulz;	 After that, put the base of your palm over the base of his nose between his two eyes;
et lai ou venra tes dois moiens, si saigne d’enche puis eschaufe le cautere qui est apelé «olivare», de coi ci est li forme:	 and where your two ways will come, bleed it first and then warm the caustic which is called "olive oil," for its form is as follows:
Et le met sor le leu signiet d’encre, et fai en dessendant et en estraignant ta main poc et poc en trestornant;	 And he places it back into its place with incision, and does so by drawing and straining your hand little by little while turning.
puis lieve ta main isnelement, et rewarde le leu se tu vois l’os I sol petit;	 Then lightly lift your hand, and carefully return the bone as you see the small joint.
et se tu ne lou vois, si rencomence le cautere tant que tu voies l’os si com je lou t’ai dit;	 And if you do not see it, then resume the cautery until you see the bone as I have instructed.
aprés pren I poc de seil, et met en awe et molle coton dedens, et met sor le leu, et li laisse III jors;	 After taking a little salt, and placing moist and soft cotton inside, then places it back on the joint, leaving it there for three days.
aprés met sus cotun moilliet en burre;	 Then applies butter to the cotton.
et laisse sus tant que li eschaudure soit ostee;	 And leaves it until the scalding is healed.
aprés cure la plaie de l’oignement qui est apelez «tetrafarmaçon», tant qu’il soit sanez.	 Afterward, treat the wound with ointment called "tetrapharmacist," until it is sound.
Et se dirent li ancien, que quant plus demoure overte li plaie, plus s’espurge;	 And the elders say, when a wound is left open longer, it drains more.
et por ce si aide mues.	 and so, if you help move it.
Et dirent aucun de ces que on doit tant lassier le cautere que partie de l’os soit arse, et puis rese on ceu qui est ars de l’os, et soit curez.	And some of these say that one must thoroughly cauterize the part where bone is burnt and then repair what has been burnt off from the bone, and treat it.
Et dient li autre c’on doit le cautere tant lassier sus, et bouter si fort c’on abaite de l’os ausi large comme I vertoil que les femmes mettent en lor fusez por ceu que les humors issent mues hors;	 And others say that the fire-cautery must be held longer, and pushed in so hard to widen the hole as wide as a woman's ring inserted into her fingers, so that the fluids can exit.
et doit on lassier la plaie longement overte;	 and it should be left open for a long time.
aprés le doit on curer et sodeir.	 after this, cleanse and heal.
Et ces II manieres de cauteres ne me semblent mie estre bones dou tout en tout, fuers qu’en aucuns homes ou il ait voie de paor;	 And these two methods of fire-cautery do not seem to me good in all cases, but only for some men who have reason to fear.
et mues me semble que je lou doie laissier;	 and it seems to me that I should leave it out.
car li chiés li est afoiblis par les solutions continuees de nature, si com nos le tesmoignons ens autres membres;	 For the head is weakened by continuous natural discharges as we testify with other limbs.
et meisme quant li chiés dou malaide est foibles par nature, et li premiere semblance de cautere est plus salve et muedre por moi, et de celi use je oevre en donques emsamble salut.	 Similarly, when the head is weak in the patient naturally, and the first sign of healing is more beneficial and effective for them, then from this treatment I work accordingly with great benefit.
de l’anciainne dolor dou chief	From ankle pain to severe headache
Quant en tout le chief vient dolor croniques, et dure longement, si doit user li malaides yeris et pilules qui sont apelees «cochie», et d’espurgement de chief et d’oiles et d’emplastres;	 When there is chronic pain throughout the head and it lasts for a long time, one must use herbs and pills called "cochie," as well as cleansing of the head and oils and plasters.
et s’on li fait le cautere que nos avons devant dit, et il ne vaut.	 and if one performs the cautery that we have mentioned before, and it does not improve.
Pren warde se li chiés dou malade est de fort nature, et qu’il ne soit trop froit;	 Be aware if the patient's headache is of a strong nature, and it should not be too cold;
adonques le cauterize desoz celui cautere un poc que nos avons dit desus.	 Then you must cauterize below that wound as we have mentioned above.
Aprés fai cautere sus chescune corne dou chief jusc’a l’os, si com devant avons dit, et fai I cautere ou leu qui est apelez «vasselz»;	 After performing the cautery on each wound of the head up to the bone, as we have said before, and make the cautery where it is called "vessel".
et est I leus en coi on met ventouses;	 and are the areas in which you apply cups.
et alige ta main si que tu ne voises mie jusc’a l’os:	 and lift your hand so that it does not touch the bone.
li malaides sent trop plus grant dolor en cest cautere que as autres, et je em parlerai aillors;	 the patient feels much greater pain in this cautery than in others, and I will speak elsewhere.
et covient que li cauteres des cornes soient plus subtis que cil dont on cautere la moieneteit dou chief, et c’est li forme:	 it is appropriate that the cauteries of the horns be more delicate than those used to cauterize half the head, and this is the method.
dou cautere dou chief	Of fire cautery for the head
Quant en une partie dou chief vient dolor sodaine, et est estendue li maladie jusc’a l’oil, et li chiés est espurgiez par medicines mondifians, et on a fait les autres cures que j’ai dit en la division des maladies, et tout ceu ne profite mie:	 When sudden pain occurs in a part of the head and the disease extends to the whole area, and the head is purged by various medicines, and all other remedies I have mentioned under the heading of diseases are done, yet none help:
adonques li fai cauteres selonc II manieres, c’est a savoir de medicine ague et de feir.	 Then you make cauteries according to two methods, namely medicinal quinsy and wound treatment.
Li cauteres de medicine ague si est que tu preignes une doce d’alz, et oste l’escorce et le recope I poc as II chiés, et puis fent la temple ou li dolor tient en teil maniere que tu puisses reponre la doce d’alz desoz le cuir;	 The cautery for quinsy is that you pluck a hair of wool, and remove the scurf and cover it with two hairs, then make an incision at the temple where the pain persists so that you can replace the woolen thread without the skin.
et quant elle sera reponuee si le lie et l’estraint bien et le laisse ensi XII houres;	 and when it is replaced, let it be tied off securely and left for twelve hours thus.
et puis le deslie et trait fuers la doce d’ail, et laisse la plaie ensi II jors ou III;	 and then untie and treat the woolen thread, and leave the wound so for two or three days.
puis met sus cotun plongiet en burre tant que porreture en isse.	 then put a piece of cotton soaked in butter until it becomes healed.
Aprés le cure d’oignement tant qu’il soit sanez;	 After the treatment with ointment until healed;
et se tu vues si fai ceu d’aucunes medicines comburans que j’ai escrites ou dozime traitier des medicines comburans.	 And if you see any of the burning remedies I have written or described in treating with burning medicines;
Li cautere de fer si est selonc ceste meniere.	 The iron cautery follows this method.
Chaufe le cautere de coi ci est li forme:	 Heat the form of that cauterizer:
Et est apelez «clos» por ceu que li chief est fait a la forme d’un clo ou il ait I poc de corbeure, et em mileu a une petite apparance;	 And it is called "closed" because the head is shaped like an owl or has little tufts of hair, and in appearance, it has a small similarity.
et le met sor le leu dolorous, et tien ta main et trestorne le feir un poc legierement, tant que li moitiez de l’espés dou keur soit arse;	 and the mass is located on the scalp, hold your hand and gently twist the hair a bit until you see the division of skin that begins to scar.
et lieve ta main que li artere n’arde, que est defuers, et decorre habundance de sanc.	 and lift your hand so the vessel does not burn further back, and it flows abundantly with blood.
Aprés met coton en awe de seil, et met sor le leu par III jors;	 After placing cotton over the wound for three days on the scalp;
puis i met coton moilliet em burre, et puis cure le leu d’oignement tant qu’il soit sanez;	 Then you place clean cotton greased with butter, and then dress the wound with ointment until it is healed.
et se tu vuelz cauterize ceste emigraine avec le cautere qui est apelez «cultellare», a tout la pointe, et te garde de coper l’artere en ceste emigraine qui n’est mie anciaine.	 And if you decide to perform a caustic treatment for this migraine using the cautery called "culutellar," at its tip, and be careful not to burn the artery in such a migraine which is not ancient.
de emigraine	Migraine
Quant tu cures emigraine si com nos avons devant dit en divisions des maladies, et ne profite mie, et vois que li cauteres devant dis de la medicine et dou fer ne li soffit mie, adonques covient il que tu eschaufes le cautere qui est apelez «cultellare» tant qu’il soit blans;	 When you treat migraines as we have previously discussed in the division of diseases, and nothing seems to help, and you see that the previous cautery is not effective with either medicine or iron, then it becomes necessary for you to heat the "culutellar" cautery until it is white.
et seigne ainsois sor le leu doillant une ligne de demi doi de lonc, et oste ta main une fois, et l’estrain que tu ne coper l’artere et que ne viegnes jusc’a l’os;	 and gently touch the tender area with a line half an inch long, then remove your hand once, and ensure that you do not burn the artery nor reach up to the bone.
et te warde de la mandibule que muet quant on menjut, et li ners n’ait regart que la muet et que spasmus ne veigne a malaide, et te warde de decorrement de sanc de l’artere quant elle sera copee, ou copement ait grant paour et meismement a celui que ne s’i conoit, et qui n’est estudians et esprovez;	 And guard the jaw so it moves when bitten, and the nerves only have regard to movement and spasms do not come upon the patient, and guard against bleeding from the artery when cut or severed, where there is great fear and especially for those who are unaware of it, and untrained.
et laisse l’uevre em mi voie;	 And leave the wound open to air;
mais je vos dirai coment on restainche sanc quant li artere est copee, et je vos mostrerai a leu ou il afiert en cest livre.	 However, I will tell you how to stop bleeding when an artery is cut, and I will show you there where it opens in this book.
Et se tu vois que cist cauteres ne soffise mie a la maladie, et li malaides est soffrans, cauterize le enmi le chief ausi com nos avons dit, et cure la plaie tant qu’elle soit sanee;	 And if you see that these cauldrons do not help at all with the disease, and the patient is suffering, cauterize within it as we have said in the head, and heal the wound until it is healthy.

et est cist cauteres millors de celui et plus aidans.	 and this caustic is better than those and more helpful.

de la torture de la bouche	For oral torment

de la cure de fistule par cautere	Of treating a fistula with cautery
Quant tu cures fistule si com nos avons dit en divisions des maladies, et tes cures ne profitent mie, adonques covient il que tu li fais cautere selonc ceste maniere.	When you treat a fistula as we have described in the divisions of diseases, and your treatment does not work, then it is proper for you to perform cautery according to this manner.
Comande au malaide qu’il mette son chief en ton sain;	 Command the patient to place his head in your hand.
et teigne li menistres son chief entre tes mains en teil maniere qu’il ne se mueve, ne ne demoinne son chief;	 and instruct the assistant to hold the patient's head between their hands so that it does not move or turn.
aprés met coton moilliet en abin d’uef ou en jus de persillion sus l’oil;	 after apply soft cotton wool in an egg cup or lemon juice on the wound;
aprés chaufe le cautere qui est teilz:	 then warm the caustic that is to be used.
et est chevez au chief si com li forme d’une penne de vouteul, ensamble la queil soit li cautere;	 and place it near the head as if like a quill in an arch, along with which the caustic should be placed.
se tu vues, si soit apointé des l’un chief dusc’a l’autre, et se tu vues, si soit ausi com une tente;	 If you see it well-aligned from one end to the other, and if you see it as evenly as a tent.
mais toutevoie, cist qui est chevez vaut mues por ton ovraige.	 However, this which is at your disposal must be moved for your work.
Aprés presse la fistule s’ele est overte, et en trai la porriture, et la seche;	 After pressing the abscess if it's open, and treating the infection, and drying it out.
et s’ele est close, si la oevre, et trai fuers la bowe;	 and if it's closed, then operate, and treat with bowstrings.

dou movement des dens	Of the slight movements of the teeth

de la dolor des dens	From the pain of the teeth
Quant dolor de dens vient por froidor, ou il i a froidor ou veir, et les cures de medicine ne valent, adonc i ait mestier de cautere selonc II manieres:	 When toothache comes from cold or dryness, and medicinal treatments do not work, then it is necessary to cauterize in the following ways:
et cautere de burre et cautere de feu.	 And cauterization with butter and cauterization with fire.
Cautere de burre si est telz que tu preignes burre de vaiche, et le bout en une cuillier de fer ou d’arain;	 Cauterization with butter is such that you take butter from a cow and the tip in a spoon of iron or silver;

et ensi fai sovent tant que sa vertus viegne a la racine de la dent, et se tu vues si moille laine et coton en burre froit, et met sus le dent doillant, et met sus I fer chaut tant que li feus viegne au chevement dou dent.	 And thus you often apply it until its virtue reaches the root of the tooth; if you see the wool and cotton in butter fat cooled, place on the aching tooth, and keep it hot with a heating instrument until heat comes to the closure of the tooth.
Li cauteres ensamble feu si est telz que tu preignes uns cainne de fer ou d’arain, et soit grosse si que li feus ne viegne a la bouche dou malaide;	 The fire cautionery involves such instruments that you choose either an iron or copper vessel and make it large enough so that the heat does not reach the patient's mouth.
aprés chaufe le cautere, de coi li forme venra ci aprés, et le met sus le dent et tien ta main tant que li cauteres soit refroidiez;	 After heating the cautionery, which will then be ready shortly afterward, place it on the tooth and hold your hand until the cautionery has cooled.
fai ceu sovent, car li dolor sera ostee celui jor meisme ou l’endemain.	 Often do this, for the pain will subside on the same day or the next.

des scrophules	Scrofula is an illness caused by tuberculosis bacteria affecting the lymebones or surrounding lymph nodes, often presenting with swelling on the neck's side. It was commonly treated in medieval times using fire cauterization and other herbal remedies to draw out pus and promote healing.
Quant les scrophules sont de fleume et de moistors froides, et ne sont obeissans a digestion par medicines, adonques eschaufe le cautere cheveit de coi ci aprés vient li forme, et ait II aovertures por les fumees a issir au cautere de l’autre partie;	 When the swellings are of phlegm and cold dampness, and do not respond to digestion by medicines, then heat the caustic substance as follows, which comes afterwards in this form, and it has two openings for smoke to escape from the other part of the cautery;

et soit li cauteres bien pres de l’espés dou keur.	 And make sure the cauterization is close to the part that hurts.
Aprés laisse le cautere aovert por giter porriture lonc tens, et ne lassier mie la cure dou malaide aprés le cautere;	 After leaving the wound open for long periods of time, do not leave the patient's care after the cauterization.
et sanation se hasterait, et seront ensamble les II ententions avec l’aide de Deu.	 And healing would be quicker, and they will together have two intentions with the help of God.
Li forme dou cautere por le ventre soit li clavile que nos avons devant mostreit;	 The form of the cauterization for the stomach should be as we have shown before.
et cil por le dos soit olivaire, selonc ceu qu’il est ci devant mis.	 And those who for the back are dislocated, as it was previously explained.
de l’enfleure des piez	Of the swelling of the fingers
Quant li piez sont enflez a celui qui est ydropique, et sont plain d’awe citrine, il covient que tu cauterizes sus le dos dou piet entre l’auriculaire et l’anulaire;	 When the fingers are swollen in those who have dropsy and are filled with yellowish pus, one must cauterize on their back between the ring finger and little finger.
et lieve ta main avec le cautere sens torner.	 And lift your hand with the caustic towards you.
Et n’entrer mie trop em parfont, ensi sarrait fuers li awe citrine, et soit li cauteres selonc cest forme:	 And do not insert too deeply, in this way it will constrict the yellowish swelling, and apply the caustic according to this form.
Aprés fai sus II jambes II cauteres en chescune jambe a la pointe dou cutellaire;	 After, make two cauterizations on each leg at the ankle joints.
et soit li cauteres dou lonc, l’un desoz le genoil devant et l’autre defuers, enmi la jambe;	 and let one caustic be long, one from behind near the knee and the other further along the leg, within the thigh.
et laisse les cauteres aovers longement sens curer, que li awe en isse;	 and leave the caustics hanging long enough so that the pus can drain out.
aprés le cure des autres cures que nos avons dit.	 after performing all other treatments as we have mentioned.
de la menoison	For the treatment of menorrhagia: take three roes from a pigeon and two roes from a capercailzie, grind them in wine, then pour it into a bottle with sugar; this should be taken at every meal for a month. Afterwards, if bleeding persists, perform the following procedure:
Quant solution de ventre vient de froidor et de moistor, tant que li vertus retentive et digestive qui est ou stomac et en l’intestine est afleboie, et ne puet estre curez par manieres de cures;	 When the solution of a cold and wet belly occurs, as long as the retaining and digestive virtue in the stomach and intestines is obstructed, and cannot be treated by various methods.
et tu vois le malaide bien soffrant et de fort vertut, si fai I grant cautere sus l’estomac selonc ceu qu’il en a parleit ci devant ou cautere de l’estomac, au cautere circule;	 and you see the patient suffering greatly and with much virtue, so make a significant fire cautery on the stomach as described before or the fire of the stomach, at which point it circulates.
et IIII cauteres entor la boude subtilz a tout I cautere clavile subtil, et II cauteres sus les hainches.	 and four subtle fires around all significant cauterizations, and two cauterizations on the sides of the hips.
Et se tu vois les moistors habundans et le malaide soffrant, se li fai cautere sus le poignil, et .i. cautere sus chaicun yle, et .ij. petis cauteres sus l’estomac delez le grant, car li cure est profitans quant il i a bone aide.	And if you see abundant moistors and the patient suffering, make a cautery on the wrist, and one cautery on each finger, and two small cauteries above the stomach near the large one, for the treatment is beneficial when there is good help.
de la cure des emorroydes	For the treatment of swellings
Quant les emorroydes sont ou fondement, ou une ou plusors, et sont ancienes et sont de grosses humors froides et moistes corrumpues, et sont curees si com nos avons dit en divisions, et il ne profite mie, si fai cauteres:	 When there are old and multiple varicose veins at the foundation or elsewhere, which are large, cold, and damp humors corrupted, and treated as we have divided in sections, and if it does not help, then make cauterizations.
III sus l’espine dou dos, celi qui est tout defuers desoz almecdate poc et poc en triangulant, et I cautere desoz la boude II dois;	 III on the spine of the back, that which is gradually below the navel and slightly towards the triangle, and a fire cautery under the hipbone at two points.
et se tu penses que ses estomac soit refroidiez, et li viande ne cuise, et on voit enfler la faice, adonques li faice on I grant cautere sus le stomac, si com il est devant dit, et I autre sus le foie, et I autre sus la mice a tout le cautere clavile;	 and if you think his stomach is cold, and the flesh does not cook, and you see the face swell, then on the face give one great fire cautery as previously described, another at the liver, and another between the ribs with a lancet.
et laisse le cautere overt lonc tens.	 and leave the fire cautery for long periods of time.
Aprés cure le leu tant qu’il soit sanez.	 After healing the limb until it is sound again.
de la charnositeit qui est nommee «thelul»	of the black substance which is called "theleol"
Quant tu copes althelul, si eschaufe le cautere qui semble I raseur, et puis le met tout embraseit sus cel althelul copeit;	 When you come to the heart, if it seems pale, first heat the fire that appears weakened, and then set it all ablaze upon that part of the heart.
et i laisse tant ta main que li cauteres viegne a la naissance de la voine, de coi li sans cort;	 and let your hand as well as the fire come to the opening of the vein, from which blood flows.
fai ceu une fois ou II, et s’il i a mout d’althelul, si cauterize chaicun si com nos avons dit;	 Once or twice as needed, if there is much thickness, cauterize each one as we have said.
aprés les cure d’oignemens profitans tant qu’il soient sanez;	 After the ointment treatments that are profitable until they heal completely;
et se tu cauterizes d’un cautere grant sus alchatim, si avra plus grant aide.	 And if you use a large caustic on the thickening, it will have greater benefit.
de plaie mal curee	Of poorly treated wound
Quant li malaides ne puet soffrir tailleure ne overture, que nos raconterons en son leu, si vient teil maladie que ne puet estre sanee fuer que par cautere.	When the patient cannot endure surgery or incision, we will discuss it in this chapter; if a disease comes that cannot be healed except by caustic treatment.
Quant a aucun vient fistule, et est enveillie et giete porriture et moistors corrumpues, si la doies prover a tot une tente subtil, et garde que tu saiches a tot la tente combien elle a de parfont.	 When there is an old fistula with decay and putrefaction and corrupted moisture, you must probe it thoroughly entirely, and be sure to know the extent of its front part throughout.
Aprés eschaufe le cautere qui semble I raseur, et le boute en la fistule selonc la quantiteit que li tente i est entrée, et rencomence lou cautere tant que cil cors porris et corrumpus soient ars, une fois, ou II ou III, selonc la quantiteit de som besoing;	 After extinguishing the caustic that appears to be scabbed over, and insert it into the fistula according to the amount that has entered inside of it, then repeat the caustic until the body part is restored and corrupted no more, once or twice or three times, depending on the amount needed;
et te warde d’ardre lé nerf qui sunt enqui, et des grans voinnes.	 And be wary of burning the nerves that are there, and large veins.
se li fistule vait au cors de la vesie et a l’intestine, si te warde de ces leus, et ne faire ceu fuers que en leu charnut, et pense qu’ele n’est mie persans;	 If the abscesses reach into the bladder and intestines, beware of these false ones, do not attempt to drain them at random places, and think that they are not persevering.
aprés cure le leu tant qu’il soit sanez, et se li leus est saielez, et les matieres sont ostees lonc tens, adonc saiches que li leus est sanez entierement;	 After curing the limb until it is clean, and if the false ones are washed away, and the materials have been worn long ago, then understand that the limb is entirely healed.
et se les matieres ne sont ostees, saiche que li leus est troez, et corrumpus li os au font;	 And if the materials have not been worn away, deduce that the limb is still infected and corrupts the bone at its source.
et ensi com un de ces que nos dirons en son leu.	 Thus, as with those we mention in their place.
de la maladie des reins	Concerning the illness of kidneys
Quant dolor de froit vient as rains, et de grosse ventositeit, et ne prent talant de femme, adonc covient il que tu li fais cautere sus les rains d’une part et d’autre au cautere clavile que nos avons devant dit;	 When cold pain comes in the legs and with great swelling, and has no desire for a woman, then it is necessary to make an incision on both sides of the leg with the pointed caustic lancet that we have previously mentioned.
et se nos le cauterizons em mileu, si avra III cauteres en ligne, et se feront plus grant aide.	 If we cauterize it with fire, there will be three cauteries in line, and they will provide greater help.
de la vessie	Of the bladder
Quant li vessie est mole et foible de froit et de moistor, si que li malaides retient l’urine, adonc li fai cautere en la partie defuers sus la vessie, la ou encomencent li poil dou poignil, et I a destre et I a senestre, et soit chescuns cauteres si lons com li nous d’un poce;	 When the bladder is heavy and weak from coldness and moisture, causing the patient to retain urine, then you must make a cautery on the part behind the bladder where the hair growth begins at the finger's point, making one on each side, with each as long as our thumb.
et li fais I cautere defuers le dos, ou II se tu en as besoing;	 and you make another posteriorly, or two if needed.
et soit li cauteres clavile selon la forme devant dite.	 and the cauterization should be made according to the form named in front.
de la marris	Of the marrow
Quant li marrix est froide et moiste, et ne laisse mie por ceu a concevoir, et les flors sont corrumpues et lor termines tarde;	 When the sperm is cold and moist, not allowing it to nourish itself, and the seeds are corrupted with delayed maturity.
et quant elles vienent, si sent grant dolor:	 And when they come, he feels great pain:
adonques covient il c’on li faice III cauteres entor la boude, si com nos avons dit ou cautere de la vessie, et II cauteres defuers le dos;	 Then it is time to make three cauteries around the wound as we have said about the bladder cautery, and two cauteries behind the back;
et soit li cauteres clavile, si com nos avons dit.	 And let the cauterization be at the clavicle, as we have said.
de la hainche	Of the hip
Quant les moistors viscouses dessendent a la boiste de la hainche, et por ceste cause si se muet de son leu, et li signes est que li cuisse est plus longe que li autre quant on le mesure ensamble;	 When the viscous swellings descend to the thigh's pouch, and for this reason it moves out of its place, and the sign is that the thigh is longer than the other when measured together.
et est trovez li leus dou departement vuis, si covient que tu cauterizes le malaide sus la boiste de la hainche a I cautere semblant au cercle, et seigne devant le leu entor la boiste si com elle torne, si que li boiste soit dedens le cercle;	 and the lower lump is discovered in the division of muscles, so it must be that you cauterize above the thigh's pouch with one cautery shaped like a circle, and place it before the bone near the pouch as it turns, ensuring the pouch is within the circle.
et si soit li cauteres telz com cil dont on a cauterizeit le stomac.	 And let the fire cautery be such as those which have been used to cauterize the stomach.
Et se cist cauteres ne t’est presens, se li fai III cauteres de l’olivaire grans, et soit li cauteres ausi parfont com tous li keurs;	 And if this fire cautery is not present, make three olive oil-based cauldrons, and the cautery should be as much in front as all the colors.
et le cure tant qu’il soit sanez.	 and cure it until it becomes healthy again.
de la dolor de la hainche	Pain of the thigh
Quant dolor vient en la boiste de la hainche, et c’est de froidor et de moistor, et li malaides est curez de ceu que nos avons dit en la division et li cure ne vaut, et li maladie est anciene:	 When pain comes from the buttock area, and it is due to coldness and moisture, and the patient is cured by what we have said in the section on cold conditions, and treatment does not work, and the disease is old.
adonc covient il que tu purges le malaide des grosses humors de pilules fetides, ou autres pilules bones semblans.	 then it is necessary to purge the patient of large humors with foul-smelling pills, or other good smelling pills that seem similar.
Aprés li fai cautere;	 After performing the fire cautery;
et li maniere dou cautere si est selonc II manieres:	 and the manner of doing the cautery is according to two methods:
c’est a savoir ensamble medicines ardans, et cautere de feu.	 that is namely with fiery medicines, and fire cauterization.
Cautere de feu si est selonc mout de manieres, desquelz li uns est telz:	 Fire cauterization has many methods, among which one is as follows:
que tu cauterize sus la boiste de la hainche III cauteres triangulalz selonc ceste forme, et i fai bone profunditeit et grant, et ait entre chaicun cautere d’espaice la groissece d’un doi, et soit li cauteres olivaire;	 that you cauterize on the thigh's pouch with triangular cauterizations according to this form, and make them deep and wide, and there should be space of a thumb between each cautery;
aucune fois fait on cautere en mileu sus lou chief de la hainche, por coi il en i a IIII selonc ceste forme:	 never do the cauterization in the middle under the head of the thigh, for there are four according to this form:
Et se tu vues, si le cauterize au cautere dou cercle que nos avons devant dit en la dislocation de la hainche;	 And if you see, if the cautery is done in the circle as we have before said for the thigh's joint dislocation:
mais fai en teil maniere que li cercles conteigne toute la hainche, et tous li espés dou keur soit ars.	 But do so in a way that the circle contains the entire elbow, and all sides are well-shaped.
Et c’est li maniere c’on fait en sciatique, quant li dolor tient en la hainche, et ne parvient mie jusc’a la cuisse ne jusc’a la jambe.	 And that is how one treats sciatica when the pain occurs in the hip and does not reach up to the thigh or leg.
Et s’ele vient jusc’a la cuisse et la jambe, se li fai II cauteres lai ou li malaides dit que li dolor li tient, et I cautere desus la cheville IIII dois, a la partie senestre un poc;	 And if it reaches to the thigh and leg, make the cauterization where the patient indicates that the pain is located, with four on the foot above the ankle, slightly to the left side.
et soit li cauteres cutellaire, et soit arse li espesseté dou keur;	 And it shall be a woolen caustic plaster, and make the padding thickness as desired.
et se li malaides sent que li dolor s’estende jusc’a dois dou piet ou pres d’enqui, se le cauterize la ou il sent la dolor III poins ou IIII au cautere qui est apelez «poins».	 And if the patient feels that the pain extends to two of his feet or near them, cauterize where he feels the pain at three points or four on the plaster called "points".
Et se mestiers est, se li en fai plus;	 And if it works, and if more is needed.
et se il seit que li dolor soit desoz le genoil vers la cuisse, se li fais cautere au cautere cutellaire ou circulaire, et te done bien garde en tous tes cauteres que tu n’i lassier mie tant le cautere que tu brules les ners et les grans arteres, et que tu ne faices au malaide plus grant nuisance et contraction.	 If the pain is below the groin towards the thigh, then make a caustic at the circular or kitchen knife cautery, and give proper care in all your cauteries that you do not remove too much with the cauterization while burning nerves and large arteries, and do not cause further harm and contraction to the patient.
Et je meisme ai veus plusors qui ont fait cautere sus la cheville dou piet, et li lasserent tant que li jambe fut toute enflee, et li piez ausi, et fut perciez et corrumpus toz li piez.	 And I have seen some who made caustics on the ankle below the knee, and they continued until the leg was fully inflamed, with the bone also affected, which were pierced and consumed entirely.
Aprés une solution de ventre dont il ot la mort.	 After a treatment of the stomach which causes death.
Et se li dolors est en II parties ensamble, fai cautere en l’une et en l’autre, selonc ceste maniere.	 And if pain is in two parts together, make a fire cautery on one and the other, according to this manner.
Et li saige dirent en la cautere de la hainche, de coi ci est li maniere, fai I tel fer et soit au chief ausi gros com uns nauvillon de dacte, ou un poc moins, et soit par entrechetres et soit des l’un entrechetres jusc’a l’autre d’espaice la quantiteit d’un nou de poce;	 And the wise ones say in hip cauterization, as follows: make an iron rod approximately as thick as a small oak leaf or slightly less, with gaps between them and enough space from one gap to another equal to the length of a pea.
et soient li entrechetres aovers de II pars, et soient aussi comme noez, et i ait I mainche de fer bien fait;	 and have the gaps at intervals of two parts, and also be as notches, and it must have one inch of well-made iron.
et c’est li forme:	 And here are the forms:
Et soit eschaufez tant qu’il soit toz rouges et giete senteles, et puis le mette on sus la boiste de la hainche malaide, et soit tornez sus lou sain costeit;	 And let it be soaked until all are red and tender, then place it under the bandage of the affected elbow, and twist over the sinewy side.
et lou cauterize une fois I cautere reont et lou laisse III jors;	 and perform a fire cautery once, leaving for three days.
et puis fai emplaustre de burre, et laisse la plaie aoverte lonc tens;	 then make an embalmment with butter, and leave the wound exposed for long periods of time.
aprés la cure d’oignement tant qu’il soit sanez.	 after the ointment treatment until it is sound.
Albucasim dit que nos usons poc de cest cautere por la paor de son regart, et se voions poc qui en usent;	 Albuquerque says we use little of this fire cautery due to its appearance, and few do so.
et toutevoie ceu est des boins cauteres, qui le puet soffrir, et lai ou il s’afiert.	 also among the good fire cauteries is one that can suffer it, and where it lodges within.
Li cauteres de medicine ardant si est que tu faices I estrument a entrechetres en coi dessende li marge de la porte, et soit d’arain ou de fer a une paroit longe, et en la hautece ait II nous, et ait entre chaicun la quantiteit de la groissece d’un doi;	 The fire cautery of medicine is such that you make an instrument with interlocking parts in which to descend the edge of the wound, and it should be made of brass or iron, long enough, and at high heat have two eyes, and between each have the quantity of fat like a spoon.
et soient overt defuer et desus, et se joignent ensamble selonc ceste forme:	 and they are to be put above and below, and join together according to this form:
Aprés met sus la boiste de la hainche au malaide gisant sor suin costeit sain, et apresse ta main mout sus la boiste de la hainche;	 After placing the vessel of the groin on the sick man lying on his side, and then press your hand much above the vessel of the groin:
aprés giete entre les II cercles de l’awe chaude qui soit chaufee au feu I poc, et li laisse une houre dou tens, et soffre li malaides la chalor et l’arsure de li.	 after pouring between the two circles of the hot cauldron which is heated over fire a little, and let it sit for one hour, and allow the sick man to experience the heat and dryness:
Car il i trueve mordication ausi com de feu;	 When there are also bites like those of fire;
et quant li mordications iert passee, se lieve ta main avec l’estrument et leve la hainche d’awe douce, et laisse ensi III jors, et met sus burre tant que ceu qui est noir de l’eschaudure soit osteit;	 And when the bites have passed, raise your hand with the instrument and gently lift the affected arm, leaving it so for three days, and apply fat until what is black from bruising has healed.
et lou laisse III jors que porriture en istrait;	 and let it rest for three days to prevent swelling;
et ceu serait li derriene aide aprés le cure d’oignemens tant qu’il soit sanez.	 and this would be the final remedy after ointment treatment until it is healed.
Et se li dolor s’est estendue jusc’a la cuisse ou jusc’a la jambe, se li fai I estrument que teigne awe selonc ceu que tu as fait en la hainche igaument;	 And if the pain has extended to the thigh or leg, make an instrument similar to what you did with the arm.
et c’est li maniere de l’awe chaude, et je l’ai escripte ou traitier de la rectification de medicine.	 and this is how to create a hot compress, which I have written in my treatise on medical corrections.
Pren alcali et chaulz vive, autant de l’une com de l’autre, et les broie ensamble, et les met en I nuef pot.	 Take an equal amount of alkali and quicklime together, grind them separately, and put in a new jar.
ou il ait I petit pertuis defuer se que li pointe d’un raisor i puisse entreir;	 If it has a small opening, so that the point of a razor can enter;
et met desor celui pot I autre pot bien plombeit, et met sus alcali et chalz et awe douce sus, tant qu’il en i ait I doi desus les poudres cant tu l’avras bien preingte a ta main;	 And place an iron or other suitable metal inside it, and add salt, vinegar, and warm water until there is one handful of powder properly mixed with your hands.
et le laisse ensi tant qu’il en dessende awe ague et chiece ou pot plombeit, puis pren toute cele awe, et la giete sus chalz et sus alcali si com devant.	 And let it sit so that warm water and lye or metal drain out of it, then collect all the liquid and pour it over vinegar and alkali as before.
Et lors si sera mout ague et est aministree en mou d’ovraiges de medicine et en cauteres d’autres membres.	 And when this is very watery, it will be transformed into a paste of medicinal mixtures and other types of cauterization for different limbs.
Car elle fait auteil oevre com feus, et si a autres medicines dont on cauterize bien la hainche ensi com tesisie et miel anacardi et chalz avec savon, toutes ces choses mellees ensamble.	 Because it performs a similar work as before, and other medicines with which the heel is well-cauterized like thuya and honey from cashew nuts and vinegard mixed with soap; all these things blended together.
Et Galiens nos raconte une cure dont uns hons fut curez de la dolor de la hainche et de la voine sciatique, et lou loe mout, et dit que on n’i fist autre cure, et qu’il en fut sanez a une soule fois quant on ot fait ceste cure, et il se fut baigniez si com il l’enseigne ci aprés.	 And Galien tells us about a cure wherein an honorable man was healed of the pain in his heel and sciatic nerve, and it greatly helped him; and he said that no other treatment was given, and he recovered once when this cure was done, and then he bathed as instructed hereafter.
Et dist en teil maniere que tu preignes dou litargire vert fres et sec, et le broie mout avec I poc de graisse, et met sus la hainche et sus la cuisse et sus la jambe ou la dolor tient, et la lie;	 And he says in this manner that you pluck the fresh and dry lettuce leaf, and grind it well with a little fat, and put on the hock and thigh and leg where the pain holds, and leave it.
et li laisse III houres et par la quantiteit que li malaides ne sente plus l’arsure.	 And he leaves it for three hours until the patient no longer feels the burning sensation.
Et puis le fai entrer ou bain tant que li cors li soit un poc arousez, et lou fai entrer ou lit, et li dolor s’en ira toute et sera sanez.	 And then make it enter a bath until the body is somewhat refreshed, and make it lie down to rest, and the pain will leave completely and be healed.
Et saiches que nuls ne doit user de cautere de telz medicines, se ceu n’est aprés l’evacuation de cors.	 And understand that no one should use fire cauldrons of such medicines unless after the evacuation of blood.
Et Dyascorides dist que quant li voine sciatique est cauterizee de fiens de chievre, si i aide mout;	 And Dioscorides says that when the sciatic nerve is cauterized with goat fat candles, it provides much help.
et doit estre fais li cauteres en teil maniere.	 and should be made as follows:
Prenez lainne et la beurez d’oile vielz, et metez sus la fossete qui est entre le pouce dou piez et l’autre qui est apelez foscile.	 Take linen and soak it in old oil, and place it over the pit between the thumb and forefinger and the other called phoscoil.
Aprés pren fiens de chievre sec, et l’empren a feu tant qu’il soit charbons, et lou met sus la laine, et le laisse tant qu’il soit estains;	 After taking dry goat fat, grasp it with fire until it becomes ashes, and place it on the wool, leaving it until it turns to embers.
et refai encor ensi, et ne cesser de faire ensi tant que tu penses par sens qu’il viegne jusc’a la hainche, et que li dolor soit cessee;	 and do so again, continuing this process until you think by touch that it reaches the hock, and the pain is ceased.
et cist manieres de cautere est apelez «cautere de chievre».	 And these methods of cautery are called "cauterization by goat".
de la dolor dou dos	from the pain in the back
Quant dolor vient au dos, ou par cheoir ou de percussion ou par trop grant evacuation, ou par semblans de matiere espandue froide, a nule de ces semblances ne vaut cauteres, fuer que a celi qui vient de infusion de froide matiere.	When pain comes to the back, whether from falling or percussion or excessive evacuation, or like cold matter expanding, none of these cases call for cautery unless it is someone who has taken in cold substances.
Il covient c’aprés ceu que li malaides est voidiez de pilules fetides ou d’autres semblans, que on li faice sus lou dos, lai ou li dolor tient, trois lignes signies d’enche, et en chescune ligne V cauteres ou plus selonc la vertut et la quantiteit que li malaides puet soffrir;	 After the patient has expelled foul pills or similar substances, apply to his back where he feels pain, three lines marked with dots, and in each line V cauterizations or more according to the potency and quantity that the patient can endure.
et soit fait li cauteres selonc le cautere qui est apelez «poins»;	 and the cauterization is done as the "points" technique;
et se tu vues, fai III cauteres ou IIII au cautere clavile moien selonc ceste forme:	 And if you see it, make III cauterizations or IIII at the middle of the clavicle in this manner:
Maintes fois vient ceste maladie as petis enfans, et li signes de l’encomencement si est qu’il ont estroite alainne quant il se lievent, et paor;	 Often, this disease comes in small children, and the signs at the beginning are that they have a narrow chest when they laugh, and fear.
et tu trueves en la derriene espinee dou dos et en nous l’apparance qui vient sus les autres espinees.	 And you reach to the last spine of the back, and its appearance that comes above the others' vertebrae.
Quant tu vois ceu et tu le vues curer, si le cauterize au cautere de celcle selonc ceste forme.	When you see this wound and examine it, apply the fire cautery according to this method.
Si que li cautere porpreigne chescune partie de l’espinee egaument.	 If the fire cautery aligns each part of the spine evenly.
Et se tu vues, si cauterize entor l’espinee au cautere poignant II lignes ou III, et soient li poins pres l’uns de l’autre.	 And if you see it, use a hot iron around the spine with a pointed instrument making two or three lines, and they should be close to each other.
Aprés cure le leu tant qu’il soit sanez selonc ceu que nos avons dit, et warde que tu n’amenistrer cautere en gilbositeit qui soit en spame de nerf.	 After curing the wound until it is whole according to what we have said, be careful not to perform caustic treatment in an area of thickened tissue that contains a nerve.
de la dolor des jointes	On the treatment of joint pain
Quant dolor de jointes sunt de moistors que sont espandues a chaicun membre dou cors, et quant dolor vient em piez, que li mire apelent «podagre» proprement, et quant elle est de froide cause et cures de medicines ne la puent curer, si est curez par cauteres en teil maniere:	 When joint pain is from moist swellings that spread to each body part, and when the pain comes in the feet, which people call "gout" properly, and if it is caused by cold conditions and cannot be healed with medicines, then it is treated with cautery as follows:
fai li mout de cauteres entor la jointure dou piet, et soit li cauteres olivaire selonc ceste forme:	 Make the mound of cautery around the foot's joint, and let the cautery be in the shape of an olive:
Et s’il i a besoigne que tu poignes sus la faice dou piet, se li fai cautere a tot le cautere c’on claime «point».	 And if it is necessary to hold the face down towards the ground, make sure to perform caustic treatment all over with a hot iron marked "no point.
Et se les dolors viegnent jusc’a genous et as autres jointures, et ceu avient maintes fois, se li fai cautere sus chaicun genoil III cauteres ou IIII de chescunne partie, a tout le cautere olivaire;	 And if the pains come near to the knee and other joints, which often happens, then perform one cautery on each kneecap, either three or four in each part, using the entire olive-shaped cautery:
et se tu as mestier de plus, si en fai plus, mais n’i tenir mie ta main fuers que tant que li espés dou keur soit ars.	 And if you need to do more, then do so, but do not hold the fur of your hand until the skin becomes white.
Et se les dolors dessendent jusc’a genoil et au dos, se li aministre le cautere que nos avons dit en son chapistre.	 And if the pains descend to the knee and the back, treat it with the fire cautery as we have mentioned in its chapter.
Et se les dolors sunt as mains, si fai poins entor le foscile II lignes;	 And if pain is in the hands, make marks around the forefinger and middle finger.
et s’il remaint point de dolor as dois, si fai poins sus chescune jointe et sus lou poil de la main;	 and if there remains no pain in the toes, make marks above each joint and on the hand's hair.
et se les dolors vienent jusc’as coutes ou jusc’as espaules, si cauterize chescune partie, et fai boin governement au malaide et penre medicines.	 and if pain comes near to the ankles or shoulders, cauterize each part, provide good care for the patient and prepare remedies.
Car se tu li fais boin governement et tu purges fleume, si sera saneis a l’aide de Deu.	 For if you take good care of them and purge phlegm, they will be healed by the help of God.
de la routure dou syfac	Of the treatment for scrofula
Quant routure vient en angres, et li bouelz dessendent as coions et c’est novelement, si covient que quant tu lou vues curer, qu’il ne menjuce mie celui jor;	 When boils come in groups and pus drains down to the joints anew, it is necessary that when you see them burst, do not mix the medicines of that day.
et qu’il use choses qui laichent lou ventre, si que li fiens dessende de son ventre;	 And he must use things that ease his stomach so that the fetus descends from it.
aprés le fai seoir sus son dos entre tes mains, et li comande qu’il teigne son alaine tant que li boueil soient repairiet, et les ramoinne a tes dois, et seigne d’enche desoz la routure sus l’os dou poignil, et a tout un signe que soit semblans a la moitiet d’un cercle a desus dou cors;	 After the child has been born, he should sit on his back between your hands, and command that he washes his ankles until the veins are repaired, and bend his arms at your elbebows, and tie off above the cut of the thumb-bone, and with a sign resembling three-quarters of a circle above the body;
puis eschaufe le cautere de coi ci est li forme:	 Then warm the caustic which has this form:
tant qu’il soit blans et qu’il giete senteles.	 until it is white and tastes sweet.
Puis ramoine les bouels a lor leu;	 Then reset the bones to their place.
et li ministres teigne sa main sus qu’il ne retornent arrier;	 and instruct the servant to wash his hands so that they do not return backwards.
et oevre bien les cuisses au malaide, et met desoz lui I cussin et I serjant sus les cuisses, et I autre sus lou pis qui li teigne les mains;	 and work well on the legs of the ill person, and place a pillow under them and the servant above their thighs, and another beneath their feet as they wash their hands.
puis met le cautere sus lou signe a tout ta main, et lou tien droit et lou tien tant que tu ateignes l’os, et se tu ne l’ateins la premiere fois, si le rencomence encor une autre tant que tu viegnes jusc’a l’os;	 Then place the fire cautery over the mark with all your hand, and hold it straight and steady until you reach the bone; if not on the first attempt, then try again another time until you go as far as the bone.
et te warde subtilment que li boueil ne saille quant tu fais lou cautere;	 And be subtle that the boil does not burst when you perform the cautery.
que tu ne le brulasses;	 so that you do not burn it.
et que par ceu li malaides ne muere, ou autre malz.	 and by this the patient does not die or suffer other harm.
Et saiches que quant tu ne viens jusc’a l’os au cautere, tes ovraiges ne vaut rien.	 And know that when you do not reach up to the bone with the cautery, your works are of no value.
Et covient que li cauteres des enfans soit subtilz selonc la mesure d’ous, et des grans gens aussi grans selonc lor mesure;	 And it is necessary that the cautery for children be subtle according to their size, and also larger for grown people according to their measure.
aprés III jors cure lou leu dou cautere de burre tant que li eschaudure soit ostee;	 After three days heal the wound with butter until the burn is scabbed over.
aprés le cure d’autres oignemens tant qu’il soit sanez, et gise li malaides XL jors sus son dos tant que li plaie soit bien soudee;	 After other remedies with ointments until it is healthy again, and let the sick person lie on their back for forty days until the wound is well healed.
et covient que ses norrissemens soit lassatis longement, si que li boueil ne saillent quant il se preigdra d’aler en chambres.	 And it is necessary that his nourishments be consumed thoroughly, so that the wound does not break out when he attempts to get up into a bed.
Et aprés XL jors, quant il se voudra lever, se li amenistre une faixe bien faite, et la porse XL autres jors;	 And after forty days, when he wishes to stand, if he binds himself with a well-made bandage, and wears it for another forty days.
et ait boin repos, qu’il se travaille poc et se warde de trop grant repletion de boivre et de mengier, et de trop haut braire;	 and he should have good rest, that he works little and watches against too much drinking of liquor and eating, and yelling loudly.
et quant il fait cest enseignement si est sanez entierement.	 And when he follows this instruction, then it will be completely healthy again.
Et je dirai ci aprés la cure de taillier en son chapistre.	 And I will say hereafter the treatment of tailors in this chapter.
de la routure dou ventre	Regarding the abdominal pain treatment.
Quant routures vienent en autres ventres et sont connisans, et tu vues qu’elles ne croissent plus, se li fai I cautere dou cautere reont selonc sa quantiteit, et soit ars li tiers dou keur;	 When ulcers come to other bodies and become known, and you see that they no longer grow, do the fire cautery as needed according to its quantity, and be careful of the third part (pertaining to size).
aprés le cure selonc ceu que nos avons dit;	 After curing it according to what we have said.
et aucun des anciens ont dit c’on le doit cauterizer au cautere a III angles selonc ceste forme:	 And none of the old ones have said that you should causticate with fire at three angles in this form.
mais signe premier le leu d’enche et fai une ligne per la largesce desus la routure, et une autre defuers, et main ta main emmi a tout le cautere clavile.	 But first mark the head of the enge and make a line for the width above the route, and another below, and keep your hand amidst all the fire cautery pointedly.
Mais li premiers cauteres est plus legiers et muedres.	 But the first fire cautery is lighter and more movable.
de dolor anciene en aucun membre	from ancient pain in any limb
Quant dolor vient en aucun membre, ou de cheoir ou de ferir, et cele dolor tient lonc tens, et li cure de medicine n’i vaut, adonc covient qu’il soit cauterizeis au cautere qui est apelez «poins», et soit li cauteres selonc la longesce dou membre et la petitece et sa foibleteit et sa vertut et sa location de torcions et de sa dolor.	 When pain comes in any limb, whether from falling or being struck, and the pain persists for a long time, with medical treatment proving ineffective, then it should be cauterized with a caustic called "poins", according to the length of the limb and its size, weakness, power, location of twists, and its pain.
s’il est sanez dou premier cautere, c’est bien;	 If it is safe after the first cauterization, it's well done.
se ceu nom, recomence I autre cautere sus celui, car teilz costume est qu’il se doit muer au membre que li est prochiens, por coi il covient que tu faices les cauteres tant que li malaides soit saneis.	 If not, continue with another cauterization on that spot because the usual practice is that it should be moved to the member closest to it, so you must make the cauteries until the patient is healthy again.
de meselerie	Messelecy or massage therapy
Li meseil sont aidiet aucune fois par cautere par grant aide, et meismement li maladie que vient de la putrefaction de fleume et de melancolie.	 The pain has been eased any number of times by caustics with great help, especially the illness that comes from the putrefaction of humors and melancholy.
Cant tu la vues cauterizer, pren warde se li maladie est au comencement, et s’ele est curee selonc ceu que nos avons dit en la division, et ne dessent ne ne demoure, et tu doutes que li corruption ne porpreigne tout le malaide, adonques li fai V cauteres sus lou chief:	 Can you not see it cauterized, take care if the disease is at its beginning, and if it has been treated according to what we have said in that division, and neither progresses nor recedes, and you doubt that corruption will affect the entire sickness, then make V cauteries on top of the head:
I emmi le chief a nouf, et l’autre vers lou front a la fin des chevous;	 I put one above the crown and the other at the end of the eyebrows.
et II sus les II cornes, et I derrierre sus le haiterel;	 and two on the temples, and one behind near the ear.
et i laise tant ta main que li cauteres viegne jusc’a l’os, et tant que les escorces en issent fors si que les vapors des grosses humors s’en puissent issir;	 and leave your hand so the cauterization reaches up to the bone, and as long as scars emerge from it, allowing vapors of thick humors to escape.
et le cauterize sus la mice selonc ce qu’il est devant.	 and cauterize underneiss on top according to what is in front.
Et se li meselerie est partout esparse;	 And if the bruises are scattered everywhere;
et elle pert manifestement, si covient que tu lou cauterizes de ces cauteres que nos avons dit ou chief, et I cautere en som lou neis, et II cauteres sus l’espinee dou col, et VI cauteres sus l’espinee dou dos, et I grant sus la crupie et I autre delez, et II sus les II espaules;	 And if it is clearly visible, then you shall use the cauteries we have mentioned earlier: one at the top of the hand, another on the spine of the neck, six along the spine of the back, a large one over the navel and others near it, and two above each shoulder.
et II sus les coutes, et II sus les tendrons dou pis, et I sus chascune jointe des mains et des piez, et sus les fosses des mains;	 and two on each ribcage, two over the knee joints, one over each hand joint, and above the palms.
et te warde des ners que sunt sus lou derrien calcant, que tu ne les bruler;	 and beware of any veins that are visible behind them, do not burn them.
et aucune fois fait om cautere sus l’os dou poignil, et I autre sus l’os de l’estomac, et I autre sus lou foie.	 and never perform a cauterization on the bone of the wrist or the bone of the stomach, nor on the liver.
Et saiches que quant plus i fais de cautere, plus li fais d’aide, et mues li profite;	 And know that the more you do with cautery, the more it helps him, and he benefits from movement.
et saiches que li malaides ne sent point de dolor au cautere si com li sain le sentent, por ce que li cors est ja toz corrumpus.	 And know that the patient does not feel pain with cautery as a healthy one would, because their body is already thoroughly corrupted.
Et covient ke li cautere soient grant et petit selonc les membres et les jointures, selonc ceu que vos lou troverez en manieres des fers.	 And it must be that the caustic treatment is large and small according to the members and joints, depending on what you find in handling iron rods.
Aprés cure lou leu de farine de veces avec miel et autres cures tant qu’il soit saneis.	 After curing them with a poultice of wheat flour mixed with honey and other remedies until they are sound.
Quant enfleure vient en aucun membre et est curee par medicines et oiles et emplastres, et il n’est mie sanez, adonques li fai cauteres sus le membre selonc la grandour et la petitece dou membre;	 When swelling comes to any limb and is treated with medicines, oils, and poultices, but it's not healthy yet, then you make cautery on the limb according to its size and severity.
et soit li cauteres un poc entrans en l’espés dou keur;	 and let the cautery be slightly intruding into the area of concern.
puis le cure d’oignemens tant qu’il soit sanez.	 then treat with ointments until it becomes healthy.
Et aucune fois fait on cautere et a la main et au piet et au dos, a l’issue dou nerf que muet le membre, et ensi si est ostee li enfleure;	 And never make cautery and to the hand and foot and back, at the place of nerve that moves the limb, and so there is swelling.
et toutevoie ne s’en entremette nuls s’il n’est conoissans des membres et des issues des ners movans lou cors.	 And at all times do not interfere unless one is familiar with the limbs and the exits of the nerves traversing the body.
