adonques se tu la vues coper, li ovraiges est telz que tu boutes une aguille en la racine des la partie desoz jusc’a celi desus, puis boute une autre aguille ou il ait I fil double des la partie dou larmier;	 Then if you see it heal, the operations are such that you insert a needle at the root of the part from below up to above, then insert another needle or there be two threads on the upper edge.
et la fai percier, et laisse la premiere aguille selonc la disposition;	 and pierce it further, leaving the first needle according to its arrangement.
puis cope lou leu dou fil double et lie une partie de l’uve entor, et l’estraint bien, puis estrai l’aguille et met sus l’oil lainne moillie en abun d’uef;	 then cut the second thread and tie a part of the eyelid around it, stretching well, then remove the needle and place oiled cloth abundantly over the eye.
et le laisse tant que li filz chiece avec l’uve, puis cure l’oil de choses confortans tant que li plaie soit sanee;	 and leave until the threads fall off with the eyelid, then treat with comforting ointments until the wound is healed.
et aucune fois li plaie est restrainte par l’uve chescune part d’un cercle de drap, tant qu’elle soit sanee.	 And at no time is the wound constrained by a veil from each side of a circle of cloth, until it is healed.
Et se li eulz done grant apparance, si le perce au spatumile subtil qui viegne em parfont de l’oil, et corre la moistor albuginé et dessende li eulz, et entre ens tantost;	 And if the eyes give a large appearance, when through a subtle stab at the bottom of the eye appears, and it passes through the white matter and descends into the eye, and enters almost immediately.
puis l’estrai tant qu’il soit sanez.	 Then extract until healed.
de la bowe de l’oil	Regarding the bowels of the wound
Ceste maladie qui est apelee «alcunnati» nen est fuers que bowe qui est assemblee en l’oil, semblant a aigue dessendant, et ce n’est mie aigue;	 This disease known as "alcunati" is not merely bowing that appears in the eye resembling water descending, and it is not actually water.
et li maniere de l’apparance de l’ovraige si est que tu faices seoir lou malaide sus I siege appareilliet et droit, puis prent le chief entre tes mains de II pars, et lou muef tant que tu voies la bowe venir au desus a tes eulz;	 and the way it appears is that you make the patient sit on a specially prepared chair and straighten up, then take his head between your hands from both sides, until you see the bow coming above their eyes.
puis soit ens fichie, et ne dessende et soit descombree li lumiere, et voie li malaides les choses si com il soloit;	 Then it is fixed firmly, and does not descend or become dislodged, allowing the patient to see properly as usual.
et s’elle ne dessent desoz, saiches que c’est aigue, et se li dessendemens de la bowe n’est appareilliez si com nos avons dit.	 And if it does not descend again, you should believe that it is healed, and the displacement of the bowstring has been corrected as we have stated.
si fai seoir lou malaide entre tes mains, puis prent le spatumile subtil et fent sus la toile cornee I poc par la continuation de la conjunctive avec la toile cornee et la corone, tant que li bowe isse;	 If you make the patient sit between your hands, then take a fine styptic and apply it under the sclerosed cornea slightly by the continuous use of the ointment on the sclerosed cornea and the crown, until the bowstring heals.
et quant elle ert issue, si distille en l’oil aigue chaude mellee a miel, ou aigue ou fenugreic est boillis et miel, puis soit curee d’autre cure tant qu’elle soit sanee.	 And when it is healed, then apply the warm oily mixture with honey or water and fenugreek that has been boiled, followed by another remedy until it becomes healthy again.
des aigues de l’oil	from eye waters
Nos avons jai les semblances des aigues en la division, et ceu qu’il covient por percier;	 We have found similarities to water in its separation, and what must be done for cutting.
si en oevre selonc la santeit.	 If in the work according to one's health.
Il covient que tu faices seoir lou malaide entre tes mains croisiet, fuers de la lumiere por le soleil, et li lie l’oil sain et estreint mout fort;	 It is necessary that you make the patient sit between your hands crosswise, away from sunlight and oil anoint his body, firmly gripping.
puis met la papiere de l’oil a ta main senestre se li eulz est senestres, ou a ta main destre se li eulz est destres;	 Then place the oil paper on your left hand if the eyes are left-oriented or on your right hand if the eyes are right-oriented.
puis prent en ta main destre, se li eulz est senestres, l’estrument qui est apelez «almagda», ou a ta main senestre, se li eulz est destre;	 Then take in your right hand, if the eyes are left-oriented, the instrument called "almandine," or with your left hand if the eyes are right-oriented.
puis met la pointe de l’estrument delez la corone par la groissece d’un rait en celle blenchor de l’oil a la partie dou menor larmier, puis boute l’estrument qui est apelez «almagda» vertuousement, et trestorne ta main tant qu’il perce en la blenchor de l’oil, et sente que almagda viegne a la chose vuide;	 Then place the tip of the instrument near the crown by moving it like a ray into that corner of the oil on the lower part of the eye socket, and insert the instrument called "almandine" firmly, and twist your hand until it pierces through to the other corner of the oil, feeling as almandine enters the hollow.
et covient que li mesure de la voie almagda soit au parfont de la mesure des l’espaice qui est des la prunele jusc’a la fin de la noirour;	 It is proper that the measure of the Almadad way be at the forefront of the space from the plum to the end of the elbow.
et c’est li corone de l’oil;	 and it is the bend of the arm;
si verras l’os en celle papiere por la clarteit de la toile cornee, et pues met l’estrument jusc’a leu ou li aigue est, puis l’espresse desoz une voie aprés autre.	 If you see the bone on that paper due to the whiteness of the tissue, then place the instrument up to it or where the vein is, and squeeze out another way afterward.
se li aigue dessent maintenant, si voit li malaides devant lui et l’estrument en son oil.	 If they go numb now, look at the patient's face and the instrument against his palm.
Aprés repose I petit, et se li aigue remonte la seconde voie, met la fuer avec l’estrument, et quant elle est ens fichie et ele ne monte, si estrai almagda legierement en tornoiant ta main poc et poc;	 Afterward rest for a while, and when the vein rises again in the second way, apply force with the instrument, and once it is firmly inserted and does not rise further, gently remove Almadad by slightly twisting your hand back and forth.
et puis remette en aigue un poc de seil gemme, et leive de ceu l’oil dedens.	 And then introduce a little bit of tying thread, and let the arm inside out.
Puis met par defuer l’oil estoupes ou lainne moillie en oile roset et en abun d’uef, et lie avec l’oil sain.	 Then insert the stopper or softened linen in oil and wax abundantly, and seal with clean flesh.
Nos, et cil qui sont de nostre tens, mettons sus comin broiet avec abun d’uef.	 And those of our time, apply a poultice with plenty of wax.
Et se almagda n’i puet entrer en l’oil par sa duresce, car il i a de teilz homes qui ont trop durs les eulz, si covient que tu preignes l’estrument qui est apelez «alberit», de coi ci est li forme:	And if the splinter cannot enter through the bone due to its hardness, as some people have overly hard nails, it is necessary that you use an instrument called 'alberit', of which this shape exists:
Et perce donques la conjunctive soulement, et n’aler mie trop em parfont, mais fai I leu subtil, puis i boute almagda, si com nos avons dit;	 And pierce then the joint solely, and do not go too far in depth, but make it subtle, then apply medicinal plaster, as we have said.
et au complissement de l’uevre appareille au malaide I dorteur avenant, en coi il dorme sus son dos en I leu tenebrous;	 And for the completion of the work, prepare an appropriate cushioning for the patient to lie on their back in a dark place.
et soit deveez de toz movemens, et preigne legieres viandes, et ne mueve son chief ne a destre ne a senestre, et soit liiez selonc sa disposition jusc’a tier jor;	 And keep them from all movement, and provide light foods, and do not move their head to the right or left, and bind them securely according to their position until the third day.
puis le deslie en cele maison meisme tenebrouse, et esprueve sa veue, et lou fai veoir aucunes choses, et puis li remet lou lien jusc’a septime jor;	 Then remove them to the same dark house and test their vision, allow them to see things, and then reapply the bandages until the seventh day.
et ne covient mie que tu faices ceu en l’oure de la cure ou aprés l’incision maintenant, mais il covient que tu aliges ceu, por ceu que li aigue monte hastanment.	 And it is not necessary to do so during the treatment or immediately after incision now, but you must elevate their head because of rapid fluid buildup.
se apostemes chaus vient, que tu desliies l’oil devant le septime jor, et l’adrece de ceu qui assouaige aposteme;	 If an abscess comes, release the oil three days before incision, and apply soothing ointment to the affected area.
et quant il est apaisiez, si deslie la veue et met sus sa faice I orilliet por covrir aucun jor, et soit adés en celle maison tenebrouse.	 And when it is calmed, remove any dressing and place a bandage on the face to cover for one day, keeping in that darkened house.
Et puis isse de la maison poc et poc, et se convertisse en ses cas;	 Then gradually leave the darkened house little by little, and return to normal activities as you are able.
et saiches que nulz deciples ne se doit entremettre en cest cas.	 And believe that no interference should occur in this case.
Et uns vint a nos qui estoit de la Yrach, qui nos dist que en som pais faisoit om almagda perciet, a coi on succe l’aigue, mais toutevoie je n’en vis onques nul en nostre terre, ne je ne lou lis onques en livres des anciens;	 And one day to us from Yrach came saying that in our land there were om almagda perciets causing water to flow, but I have never seen any here in our lands or read about them in ancient books.
et par aventure c’est une novele chose.	 And sometimes it is a new thing.
Et ce sont les semblances des formes de almagda, por ceu que cil qui ne les conoit les voie;	 These are the similarities to forms of elephants because those who do not know them see them this way.
et soient d’arain proprement:	 and they truly are:
Et soient li chief d’aus de ceste meisme subtiliteit, et li derriene en .iij. angles ague.	The head of those from this same subtlety lies flat on three corners sharp.
de la char sor le neis	they p s, et w with l’s ount cite of arment:
Aucune fois naissent ou neis chars ajostees diverses, de coi il i a aucunes qui semblent scorpions a mout de piez;	 At no time do they give birth or have various dislocations, from which some appear like scorpions stinging their limbs.
et si i a de telz ou il ait char enchancree de fuxe color, et si a char souef de bone color.	 and if there are such that they have sharp dislocations of fiery colors, and those with softness in the color of bones.
En celle donques de ces chars qui est souef, et ne mie enchancree, covient que tu faices seoir lou malaide entre tes mains encontre lou soleil;	 In cases like these where there is softness and not sharp dislocations, you should make the patient sit between your hands facing the sun.
et oevre ses narines, et giete l’oncine a celles chars, et les trai fuers;	 and open his nostrils, and pour onion extract onto those with softness, and apply force to them.
pues cope ceu que tu em pues sostenir au spatumile subtil agut d’une part, tant que tu saiches que celle char est toute ostee.	 thus continue what you have started holding the tender tip of a subtle blade on one side until you know that dislocation is completely bone-like.
Et s’il en remaint aucune chose c’on ne puisse coper, si l’ovrez a tout I des estrumens subtil legierement, si qu’il n’i demoure rien;	 And if there remains anything that cannot be handled, try operating on it with all subtle ointments lightly applied, so nothing remains.
et se sans te sormonte, ou aposteme chaus, si lou secort si com il covient;	 And if there is an inflammation or abscess, treat it as necessary.
et se c’est apostemes malignes, si te haste et lou cauterize tant que li sans soit estainchiez et soient ostees toutes les chars, puis giete ou neis aisil et aigue ou vin.	 And if it is a malignant abscess, quickly cauterize until the pus dries and all wounds are closed, then pour oil or wine to cool and disinfect them.
Se li neis oevre, et moistors en vient jusc’a palais, saiches qu’il est sanez;	 If healers do not work, and moisture reaches the throat, ensure they are safe;
et se moistors ne perce si com il covient, saiches qu’il i a char nee en l’os desus, a coi li estrumens ne vient mie por taillier:	 And if moisture does not penetrate as it should, make sure there is no swelling in the bone above, where pus cannot come out for dressing.
adonques covient il que tu i boutes I fil de lin un poc gros, et soit noez de mains nous, et ait entre chescun nout d’espaice I doit ou moins;	 Then it is necessary to tie a piece of flaxen thread slightly thickened, and keep it clean with hands, ensuring space between each knot or less.
et mette li malaides lou chiés dou fil en son neif a som pooir, et traie en odorant tant qu’il viegne par lou neif dedens la bouche;	 And place the patient's head back through its neck as much as possible, and pull gently until it enters comfortably into the mouth.
et maintes fois font ensi li enfant as escoles, et c’est legiere chose a celui qui le vuet faire;	 And many times they do so with children at schools, and it is an easy task for those who want to do it.
puis tien le chief qui vient par lou neif a une main, et l’autre chief qui vient par la bouche a l’autre main, et saiche l’un aprés l’autre en soiant as nous qui sont ou fil.	 Then hold the head coming through the neck with one hand, and the other head coming from the mouth with the other hand, and support one after another as we who are fil (children) do.
Fai ceu tant que tu saiches que li nout ont corrompue celle char, puis trai lou filz, essue le sanc, et moille lou fil en oignement egiptien, et le remet derechief au neis si com devant;	 Do this as long as you know that they have contaminated the wound. Then guide the child, drain the blood, and wash their hair with Egyptian balm, and return it to its place as before in the neck.
fai ceu III jors ou plus, tant que li oignemens corrode tout ceu qui est demorez de char;	 Do this for three days or more, until the anointments have consumed everything that remains of the wax.
et puis met ou neis une caine de plonc aucuns jors tant qu’il soit sanez, et s’il a mestier de medicines sechans, si en use;	 Then afterward apply a bandage for several days until it heals, and if drying remedies are needed, then use them.
et c’est li forme de l’estrument por purgier lou chief, a coi on distille les oiles et les medicines ou neis:	 This is the form of the instrument used to purge by pouring in oils and remedies at its top.
Et soit d’argent ou d’arain, semblant a une lampe overte, si com une cainne, et li conduis ausi;	 And it should be of silver or copper, resembling an open lamp, as in a container, and this leads them similarly.
et se tu vues, si fai une cainne close, et soit li estrumens plains por espurgier lou chief;	 And if you see it, then make a closed vessel, and let the effluvia be plain to purge the head.
et ait I mainche au chief por lou tenir quant on chaufe l’oile ou aucune liquor.	 There should be a handle at the top to hold when heating the oil or any liquid.
de la char sor le neis	they p s, et w with l’s ount cite of arment:
Maintes fois naist au chief dou neis une maladie qui est apelee «telul», et croist et devient grans adés, tant qu’il est vis chose au regarder;	 Many times appears on the head of the nose a disease called "telul," and it grows and becomes large until it is visible upon looking.
et por ceu covient que tu lou copes au comencement, et l’oste tout fuer, puis met sor leu lou cautere ou la medicine ardant;	 And therefore, one must initially make an incision, then stitch it firmly, and subsequently place the fire cautery or hot medication on it.
et s’on le tarde a coper tant qu’il soit grans, si pren warde s’il est durs, de fuxe color, de povre sens:	 And if it is not operated upon while still small, one should take care to observe if it becomes hardened, of furious color, and with weakened sensation.
si ne lou touchier mie de fer car c’est uns apostemes enchancrez, car quant on le cope aucune fois, si en vient grant malice au malaide;	 if not touched by iron, for it is an incurable boil, because whenever one operates upon it, great harm befalls the patient.
et se li apostemes est de soef touchement, non mie de fuxe color, et tu vois c’on le puisse tout coper, si vuide le malaide et lou cope sens paor, et cure le leu de choses sechans et restraignans.	 and if the boil is of soft touching, not furious color, and one sees that it can be entirely incised, relieve the patient from fear and perform the operation without hesitation, curing dry and constrictive things.
quant li neis est copez et cosus	When the neck is cut off and removed
Saiches que quant solutions de continuation vient en une de ces cartillagines ovraiges, i profite poc, fuer que en aucuns homes.	 Believes that when continuous supply comes to one of these cartilaginous works, it benefits little, even in some people.

et adonques ajoste les II levres a une costure, puis le cure tant qu’il soit sanez;	 And then bring together both edges of the wound into a seam, and then heal it until it is sound.
et se les levres sont ja desevrees d’une part et d’autre, si covient que tu escorches toutes les parties de lor keur tant qu’elles sainent, puis assemble les II levres a une costure, et l’estraint, et poudre sus poudre de sanc de dragon, et encens broiet;	 And if the edges are torn apart on both sides, it is necessary that you scrape all parts of their flesh until they heal, then bring together both edges into a seam, bind them up, and powder with powdered blood of a dragon, and burn incense.

ou par aguilles, si com nos avons dit en la costure dou ventre;	 or with needles, as we have said in the abdominal stitching.

des apostemes des levres	For abscesses on the lips
A mains homes avient dedens les levres aposteme dur, semblans a grains de veces, et menor et plus grant;	 Sometimes abscesses occur within the thickened vein ends, appearing like grains of pepper, and small and larger ones;
adonques couvient que tu tornes les levres, et fendes sus chescun nout, et le prent as pinceures et le cope en chescune partie;	 Then it is necessary to return the vein ends, cut above each one, and grasp them with forceps and place them in separate parts.

de la char des gencives	From the edge of the gums
Maintes fois naist sus les gencives char ajostee, que li ancien apelent «albulus»;	 Often emerges under the gums that the ancients called "albulus";

si ne revient mie aprés le cautere;	 if it does not return after cauterization;

des sordens	For ulcers
Aucunes fois sont assemblees au chief des dens, dedens la bouche entre les gencives, escorces qui sont laides et aspres;	 Never gathered at the top of the teeth between the gums, scales that are unattractive and sharp;
et aucune fois sont li dent noir et citrin et vers, tant que li corruption vient a la gencive, et sont li dent puant;	 At times they are black and yellowish-green and wormy, as long as decay reaches the gums, and the teeth become foul.
si covient que tu faices seoir lou malaide entre tes mains, et ses chiés soit en ton saint, et reis les dens ou les escorces aperent, tant qu’il n’i demore rien;	 If it becomes necessary to make the patient sit between your hands, and his head be in your holy one, and remove any teeth or scraps that are found, until there is nothing left.

et s’on oste ceu que i est a la premiere rasion, c’est boin;	 And if you extract what is at the root, it is good.

et saiches que li dent ont mestier de diverses formes d’estrumens por reire, selonc ceu que li oevre lou demoustre, por ceu que li raseur dont on reit defuer les dens ont autres formes que cil dont on reit entre les dens;	 Know that the teeth require various forms of treatments to heal, according to what the work shows, because the razors from which one removes teeth have different shapes than those found between the teeth.
et cestes formes et autres soient avec toi appareillies.	 And these forms and other similar things are with you arranged accordingly.
Il covient quant tu cures lou dent de sa dolor que tu tardes dou traire tant com tu pues, car ce ne doit om mie faire;	 It is necessary when treating the tooth of pain that you delay the extraction as much as possible, for it should not be done hastily.
car c’est une substance mout haute jusc’a donc c’on n’ait point d’excusation dou raier.	 because it is a matter so important up to that one has no excuse for the extraction.
Adonques quant li malaides est constrains dou traire, si covient que tu soies certains dou dent doillant.	 Then when the patient is straining to urinate, it is necessary that you are certain about the condition of their teeth.
Maintes fois desoit li dolor lou malaide, et cuide qu’elle soit ou dent saint, et fait traire le boin dent;	 Often the pain troubles the patient, and he thinks it is a healthy tooth, and pulls out the bad tooth.
et toutevoie ne se depart mie li dolor per ceu, tant que li malvais estrais, car nos l’avons ja veut faire a ces sainors;	 And indeed, do not leave the pain at all because of this, as long as the evil persists, for we have already tried it with these healers.
et quant tu es bien certains dou dent doillant, si covient que tu escorches entor lou dent a tout i. spatumile fort por warder la gencive de toutes pars;	 And when you are certain of the toothache, if it is necessary, scrape around the tooth completely and thoroughly in order to protect the gum on all sides.
puis le mues a tes dois ou as tenailles subtilz au premier poc et poc, tant qu’il soit bien eslochiés, puis i afferme bien les tenailles;	 Then move it with your fingers or delicate tweezers slowly and gradually until it is properly aligned, then firmly fix the tweezers.
et soit li chiés dou malaide en ton saint entre tes genous, et lou tien bien si qu’il ne se mueve.	 And place the head of the malady in your holy hands between your thumbs and index fingers so that it does not move.
Aprés estrai lou dent droitement sens brisier, et s’il ne saut fuer, si prent aucun de ces estrumens et le boute dedens de chescune part legierement, et lou remuef si com tu as fait premier.	 After extracting the tooth straight without breaking it, and if it does not come out easily, take one of these ointments and apply it inside from every side gently, then move it as you did initially.
Et se li dens est perciez et mengiez, si covient que tu l’emplisses de drapelz, lai ou li pertus sont;	 And if the tooth is pierced or mangled, if necessary, fill it with thread gauze at the sites of the holes.

Et te done bien en warde que tu ne le brises, et en remaigne une partie, et reveigne au malaide par la malice de la racine plus grans dolors de la premiere.	 And make sure not to break it, and leave a part behind; causing greater pain from the root for the patient initially.
Et te warde que tu ne faices mie ensi com font li ignorant sainor, qui par lor haste et par lor hardiesce brisent aucune fois le charreit, et n’i amenistrent mie ceu que nos avons conteit;	 And be sure not to do as the ignorant surgeon does, who through their hastiness and boldness break the instrument every time, without applying what we have explained.
mais font venir aucune fois par l’oquison de ceu grant maladie por les racines que i demorent, ou por lou charreit qu’il brisent, si com nos avons sovent veut;	 but they bring about great disease through this condition to the roots that remain there or from breaking the instrument as we have often seen.

et se decorremens de sanc i vient, que sovent avient, si emple lou leu de vitriole broiet;	 and if bleeding occurs, which often happens, apply the paste of antimony to the area.

Les formes des estrumens, a coi om muet les dens premier, soient a longes pointes et a gros mainches, qu’il ne doublent mie quant tu trairas le dent;	 The forms of the strangulations, where one cannot move the teeth first, have sharp points and large loops that do not overlap when pulled through the hole.
et ce sont les formes:	 and these are the shapes:
Et soient de gros membres si qu’il ne ploient mie au traire, et soient de fer inde bien fait, et soient dentez por mues tenir.	And they have large limbs that do not bend easily when grasped, and are made of well-crafted iron, and have teeth to hold them securely.
de la racine des dens	From the roots of the teeth.
Quant li racine demoure au traire, si covient que tu mettes sor le leu coton moilliet em burre I jor ou II, tant que li leus soit amolis, pues i boute les tenailles qui sont apelees «algefri», de coi li chiés semblet bec de soigne;	 When the root cannot be pulled through, it is necessary to place cotton or wool in butter for one or two days until the gums are softened, then insert the pincers called "algefri", making the head appear like a bird's beak.
et soient dedens faites ausi com une lime et c’est li forme:	 and they should be made similar to files in shape:
Et se les racines ne vuellent issir a tout ces tenailles, si covient que tu descuevre la char tot entor la racine, et i met l’estrument qui est apelez «althali», c’est a savoir palainche, de coi ci est li forme:	the le Mort; 1.
Et soit fors et gros si qu’il ne brise mie, et se li racine saut par ceu, c’est boin;	 And it is long and thick so that it does not break easily, and if the root comes out through this, it is good.
se ceu non, si t’aide de toz les estrumens, de coi les formes vienent ci aprés:	 If not, use all instruments, through which forms come hereafter:
Et si s’aide on de cest estrument qui ait .ij. rains, de coi ci est li forme:	And if you use the instrument that has two prongs, thus is the form as follows:
et d’autres ferremens qui sont devant en la rasion des dens, et de cest estrument qui semble unes grans tenailles, dont ci est li forme:	and other instruments placed in front on the density, and of this instrument which appears like large pincers, thus is the form as follows:
Et soit cist estrumens fors qu’il ne puisse brisier, et saiches que mout d’estrumens de dens sont;	 And these tools are such that they may not break, and know there are many of the same kind.
et ausi d’autres estrumens, qui ne sont mie contez;	 and likewise other instruments, which are not counted.
et li saiges maistres subtilz trueve par soi meisme son estrument, selonc ceu que ses ovraiges et li maladie li demoustre, car il i a de teilz maladies ou li ancien n’enseignerent point d’estrument por la diversiteit d’au;s et s’om brise point dou charreit ou des autres os, ou il porrit, si i cerche as estrumens qu’il i covient, que je t’ai dit, et t’aide des gestes, de coi ci est li forme:	 and the wise master is subtle in using his instrument by himself accordingly to his procedures and illnesses that show themselves, for there are some diseases where ancient teachers did not provide an instrument due to their variety, or if it breaks on the cart or other bones, seek the instruments I mentioned earlier and use gestures as follows:
Et soient gros et bien tenant por tenir l’os, qu’il n’eschaipe, mais le puisse tenir et oster;	 And let them be large and firmly held to grasp the bone without slipping but can hold and extract.
et puis restoure lou leu de medicines convenant a ceu, et s’il ait en l’os porriture, et elle est petite, si la reis a tout cest estrument:	 And then restore it to its original position with appropriate medicines for this, and if there is decay in the bone, and it is small, bring all of this instrument.
Quant li dent apperent ne mie selonc lou cors natureil, et li forme est laide, et meismement en femmes puceles, si covient que tu saiches se li dens est neis aprés lou dent, et n’est mie en droit leu, et on ne lou puet soier ne limer:	 When the tooth appears not in accordance with natural form and is ugly, especially in maiden women, one must ascertain if the root is still present after the tooth, and it is neither in its proper place nor can be saved or filed down.
adonques lou raie;	 Then proceed with cutting.
et s’il est aers avec lou dent, si prent cest estrument dont ci est li forme, et est semblans a I petit bec, et soit de fer inde agut en som:	 And if it is hardened along with the tooth, take this instrument of which there are images below, and it appears as though having a small beak, and made of iron well sharpened at its tip.
Et lou cope poc et poc em mains jors por la duresce dou dent, et por ceu que tu ne mueves les autres, et s’il est apparans c’on le puisse limer, si lou lime d’une teil lime com ci est li forme:	And the wax is taken little by little over many days due to dental hardness, and because you do not move the others; if it appears that one can be filed down, then file in a manner consistent with its shape.
et est ausi com li lime de coi on fait les aguilles;	 And it is similar to the file from which needles are made;
et en lime lou dent poc et poc em mains jors legierement, si qu’il ne se mueve tant qu’il chiece;	 And with a file the teeth are touched lightly, little by little over time, so that they do not move until they loosen.
puis la plaine en la fin a tout aucun raseur, et se li dens est trop trenchans et il blece la lengue, si covient limer l’aspreteit tant qu’il soit igalz, si qu’il ne blece la lengue ne ne corrompe la parole.	 Then at the end it shall be smoothed without any roughness, and if his teeth are too sharp they will nick the tongue; thus one must file the sharp edges until they are even, so that he does not nick the tongue nor damage speech.
quant li dent lochent	When a tooth becomes loose.
Quant li dent devant lochent, ou par percussion ou par cheoir, et li malaides ne puet presser sus ceu qu’il menjue qu’il ne chient, et tu les as curez de medicines restrignans, et ceu ne vaut;	 When the teeth are loose or have fallen out by impact or decay, and the patient cannot hold what they chew without it falling apart, and you have treated them with constricting medications, but that is not effective.
si les covient restraindre d’un fil d’or, car li filz d’argent devient vert et porrit, mais li ors ne se mue onques;	 if they require being bound by a thread of gold, because silver threads turn green and rot, but gold does not move.
et soit li filz moiens ne trop gros ne trop menus, selonc la quantiteit de l’espaice entre les dens;	 And let the child's stitch not be too large or too small, according to the quantity of space between the bones.
et se tu vues adrecier les dens, si pren lou fil et lou boute double entre les II dens sains, puis met les chiés entre les dens meus, s’il en i a I ou plusors, tant que tu veignes saigement jusc’au dent sain d’autre part;	 And if you see the bones aligning correctly, take the thread and pass it twice between both healthy teeth, then place the needle among the affected teeth, until you reach another healthy tooth on the opposite side.
puis rencomence la coverture jusc’a la partie ou tu encomensas, et estrains ta main subtilment et saigement, tant qu’il ne se mueve point;	 Then resume wrapping up to the part where you began, and gently yet firmly pull your hand backward until it does not move.
et soit ta lieeure a la racine dou dent si qu’il ne puist eschaper.	 And ensure the ligature is close to the base of the tooth so that it cannot escape.
Puis cope les chiés dou fil a unes tenailles, et les assemble, et les repont entre le dent sain, et le met ensi qu’il ne blece la lengue;	 Then cut the thread with pliers, tie them together, and place them so that they do not touch the tongue.
et puis le laisse ensi estroit tant com il puet demorer, et s’il deslie, ou li filz ront, si l’estraint d’un autre fil;	 And then let it lie so narrow as long as it can remain there, and if it dislocates again, or the children return, they must be strained with another bandage.
si demorrait et servira ensi tout son tens, et c’est li forme des dens et li figure de l’adrecement des II dens sains, et des II meus, si com tu vois:	 If it remains and serves thus for its entire duration, and it is the shape of two bones and the alignment of two healthy joints, as you see.
Et quant li dent chiet, si lou remet on en son leu, de fres en fres, si com nos avons dit;	 And when the tooth falls out, then reset it back in its place, freshly each time, as we have said.
et ne s’en entremette mie qui n’est saiges et soffrans, et aucune fois fait on la forme d’un dent d’os de vaiche, et lou met on au leu ou li defaute est, et l’estraint on si com nos avons dit, et demore et sert ensi lonc tens.	 And let no one who is not wise and patient interfere, nor at any time make the shape of a wolf's tooth, but place it where it is missing, and strain it as we have said, and it remains and serves thus for long durations.
de coper lou liien de la lengue	tions. I2 Confit.
Aucune fois est cist liiens qui vient desoz la lengue ou naturez, que on naist ensi;	 Never is this bandage which comes from under the tongue or its natural form found to be like that.
ou par accident de plaie soudee;	 Or by accident of a burn wound;
et li ovraiges est telz que tu oevre la bouche dou malaide, et ait sa teste en ton sain, et li lieve la lengue;	 And the procedures are such that you treat the mouth of the sick person, keeping their head in health, and lift their tongue.
puis cope lou liien nervous dou large, tant que li lengue soit desloie de son tenement, et se il i a duresce ou nout, et c’est de soudement de plaie, si i boute l’uncine et cope dou large celui liement;	 Then treat the sick person's tongue, until it is dislocated from its place, and if there is hardness or swelling, and it is a severe wound, apply an incision and sever the ligaments.
et garde que li fendure ne soit mie trop em parfont, por l’artere qui est desoz;	 And ensure that the incision is not made too wide, for the artery which lies beneath.
et quant tu as fait, si leve le leu d’aigue rose et d’aisil, ou d’aigue froide, puis met desoz la lengue une tente de lin;	 And after you have done so, lift up a piece of pink silk or cold water cloth, then place it under the tongue with a linen tent.
et la teigne li malaides chescune nuit, que li leus ne puisse soder.	 And each night wash away any tartar from the patient's teeth so they cannot close.
Et se decorremens de sanc vient, si met sor le leu vitriole broiet;	 If bleeding continues to occur, then apply a poultice of potassium iodide on it.
et se li sans te vaint, si le cauterize au cautere lentiginout, qui est boin a ceu;	 And if the wound does not heal, then use a slow-burning caustic which is beneficial for this.
puis le cure d’autre cure tant qu’il soit sanez,	 Then pursue another treatment until it becomes healthy again.
et se tu lou vois de fusse color ou noir ou dur, si que li malaides ne lou sent, si n’i touchier point, car c’est chancre;	 And if you see the wound is colored or black or hardened, and the patient does not feel it, do not touch it, for it is a chancre.
et s’il est declinans a blenchor, et il i a moistor, si i giete l’oncine, et lou fent d’un spatumile subtil, et lou delivre d’une part et d’autre;	 And if it is approaching gangrene, and there is moisture present, then apply an unguent with onion extract, which softens the area gently, and release it from both sides.
et se li sans te vaint a ton ovraige, si met sus vitriole broiet tant qu’il soit estainchiez, puis revien a ton ovraige tant que tu traies tout fuer;	 And if the wound does not heal at your hands, apply potassium ipsenate until it becomes impervious, then return to your treatment as long as you have exhausted all means.
puis leve lou leu d’aisil et de seil, et le cure d’autres cures tant qu’il soit sanez.	 Then lift it carefully and gently, and treat other injuries until it is healthy again.

se c’est apostemes dur de petit sens et de fusse color, si ne lou touchier mie de fer.	 If it is an abscess of mild pain and size with a pale color, do not treat them without iron.

et trai aucune chose des toiles avec, puis la cope a l’estrument, de coi ci est li forme, que semble unes forces;	 And train any thing with threads, then grip the instrument of it, which is its form, that seems like some force.
et toutevoie li chief sont corbé, et l’un endroit l’autre, et sont molt agut, et est fait de fer inde ou d’andainne:	 In all ways, the head is curved, one place to another, and it is very painful, made of iron or copper.

et aucune fois naissent en la gorge autres apostemes que les II amandres, si les cope donques ensi com les II amandres igament.	 And at no time does an abscess arise in the throat other than two large ones, then treat them as you would with these two large abscesses.
Et je medicinai une femme d’un aposteme que li estoit neis dedens la gorge, c’est a savoir I aposteme de petit sens;	 And I treated a woman for an abscess that was inside her throat, which is to say one small abscess.
et avoit jai bien pres close toute la gorge, si que li femme ne pooit expirer por le conduit qui estoit estoupez, et ne pooit ne mengier ne boivre, et fust morte s’elle demorast ensi I jor ou II.	 and the abscess was so tightly closed that it nearly choked her throat passage which was blocked, and she could not breathe or eat or drink, and would have died if she remained like this for a day or two.
Et li apostemes estoit jai si montez qu’il avoit fuer mis II rains par les II pertuis dou neis.	 And the abscess was so swollen that there were two heads through its two openings on each side of the neck.
Je hastai donques tantost, et fichai en l’un I oncine, puis lou traï fuers, et en traï grant porcion de bowe;	 So I acted immediately, and inserted one needle therein, then the wound was turned, resulting in a large portion of pus.
puis refis autreteil en l’autre pertus dou neis, et li ovrai la bouche et li pressai la lengue;	 Then reset it on the other side, by pulling the nose, and open the mouth and press the tongue.
aprés fichai l’oncine en ces apostemes, et en copai une partie, et n’en issit fuers que un poc de sanc;	 After extracting the splinter from this abscess, and biting off part of it, did not result in much blood.
et ensi fut destoupez li conduis de la gorge la femme, et comensa maintenant a boivre aigue et puis vin, et ne cessai de taillier de cel aposteme par lonc tens;	 And thus was cleared the path of the throat for the woman, and now began to drink water and then wine, and did not cease tearing at that abscess for long times.
et li apostemes recroissoit adés, et remplissoit lou leu que je avoie vuidiet, tant qu’il refut mout gros;	 And the abscesses reappeared again, and filled up the space that I had emptied, becoming quite large.
adonques je l’engignai et lou cauterizai dedens la gorge:	 Then I deceived it and performed a cautery within the throat.
ensi demora sens croistre;	 Thus, he stayed without growing.

et en emple le chevement de cest estrument, de coi ci est li forme:	 And for using this instrument, here is its form:

s’elle est curee de fumigation selonc ceste maniere, pren calament et ysope et origanum et rue et camomille et avronne et semblans herbes, et les assemble toutes ou aucunes d’eles en I pot, et i met aisil, et fai bullir;	 If it is treated with fumigation in this manner, take expectorants and yarrow, hyssop, rue, chamomile, elecampane, and similar herbs, and put them all together or some of them into an earthenware pot, then set to boil.

car li craiffe d’uef ne lait mie la vapor grever la bouche, et c’est bone cure ensamble salut.	 For the cracked tooth does not much burden the mouth, and it is a good remedy together with health.

si covient donc que tu traies ceu que tu pues veoir, et li presse la lengue au soleil a tout l’estrument, si que tu voies mues la chose;	 Therefore you must treat what you can see, and press the tongue to the sun with all your instrument, so that you may move the thing.
et ceu que ne t’apert mie et est reponus en la gorge, covient que tu faices vomir le malaide ainsois que li viande soit cuite en l’estomac;	 And what does not appear and is resituated in the throat, it must be made to induce vomiting so that the meat may cook in the stomach.
par aventure si istra li chose aerse par le vomissement;	 Perhaps if you eject the thing through vomiting;
ou li malaides englutisse une piece d’esponge, ou une piece de navel, ou une racine de laitue, ou I morceil de pain sec;	 Or the patient swallows a piece of sponge or a piece of cotton, or a lettuce root, or crust from dry bread.

et s’elle ne vient fuer de ceu que nos avons dit, si pren I estrument de plonc selonc ceste forme:	 And if it does not move as we have said, take the instrument of tongs in this manner:

li chapistres des apostemes	The instrument used for treating sinuses; and it looks like has texture similar to surgical procedure as the beak of a surgeon's tool, thus:
Mout de semblances d’aposteme sont, selonc ceu que li remembrance vient ci aprés d’un et d’autre en cest livre, et sont diver en perforation et en taille;	 Many types of abscesses are, as recollection comes after one and another in this book, and they differ between puncturing and cutting.
et c’est en II manieres dont l’une est en sa semblance meisme, et de ceu qu’il tient moistor.	 And it is in two ways alike, one from its own nature itself, and because of moisture.
Et li seconde maniere si est por les leus ou il sont au cors.	 And the second way is for boils that occur within the body.
car li apostemes dou chief est autres que cil dou fondement, et li apostemes dou leu charnut est autres que cil qui vient en jointures, et chescuns ait son jugement en l’uevre.	 because an abscess at the top is different from one at the base, and an abscess in the thighs is different from those that occur in joints, and each has its judgment in practice.
Et si a apostemes c’on ne doit mie percier, tant que li bowe est meure selonc son acomplissement;	 If with an abscess that should not be pierced, until the bowel is completely healed according to its course;
et si a de telz qu’il covient percier quant il sont crut, et ne meurent mie selonc lor acomplissement, si com aposteme qui sont delez jointures.	 and if of those that should be pierced when they are ripe, do not heal as is their course, like an abscess near joints.
Car quant apostemes vient delez jointures, et on le laisse tant qu’il est porris entor, par aventure si sont corrumput li liien et li nerf de la jointure, par coi ce est cause de contraction en celui membre.	 When abscesses occur near joints and are left to become ripe, by chance they may corrupt the ligament and nerve of the joint, causing contraction in that limb.
Ou li aposteme est delez lou membre principel, et se tu tardes la perforation tant qu’il soit meurez, si nuira au membre principeil;	 Or the abscess is near a major limb, and if you delay the piercing until it has healed, it will harm the main limb;
ou il est delez lou fondement, si le perce on ainsois qu’il soit meurs;	 or it is near the foundation, if you pierce then not when it is fully healed.
et ne covient mie que tu perces aposteme crut sens digestion acomplie, fuers que celui qui est delez lou fondement, qu’il ne porrisse em parfont, et soit alongiez dedens, et i viegne fistule;	 and it does not bode well to pierce an abscess when digestion is incomplete, especially one near the foundation, that it may rupture entirely, extend internally, and cause a fistula.
et ne puisse saner en grant termine.	 And cannot heal completely.

et covient que tu faices seoir la perforation ou plus dependant leu de l’aposteme, et la ou il apert mues;	 And it is necessary to keep the incision in place unless further moved from the abscess site, and wherever healed.

et je vos dirai ceu que je vis.	 And I will tell you what I have seen.
Je vis que une damoisele prist I coutel, et le ficha en sa gorge, et copa partie des chenelz dou pormon;	 I saw a maiden take a knife and thrust it into her throat, cutting part of the windpipe.
et je fui apelez por li curer, et la trovai ausi com morte.	 And I went to try to cure her, but found her as dead.
Je descovris la plaie, et trovai le sanc qui en estoit issus, et soi bien qu’elle n’avoit mie copeit voine ne conduit fuer que la gorge, et li vens issoit fuer par la plaie.	I discovered the wound, and found blood issuing from it; and I saw that she had not bled from her veins or any other passage except through her throat, and the bleeding was strong from the injury.
Je me hastai, et cousi la plaie, et la curai tant qu’elle fut sanee;	 I hurried, stitched the wound, and treated it until she was healed.
et n’avint a la damoisele fuer qu’elle fut roge de voix, et revint aprés a sa disposition;	 and there was no harm to the maiden except for her being hoarse in voice, and afterwards returned to her usual state.
por ceu di je que en la tailleure de l’epiglote n’ait mie paour.	 Therefore I say that in treating the epiglottis there is no need for fear.
de la grosse gorge	of the large throat
Cist apostemes est apelez «hernie de gorge», et est uns grans apostemes en color d’une jaisse, et est molt en femmes;	 These abscesses are called "throat hernias," and they are large abscesses the color of jet, and occur mostly in women.
et est selonc II manieres:	 There are two methods as follows:
naturez, et accidens;	 natured, and accidental.
ou natureil n’a point d’engien.	 or natural does not have a remedy.
Et li accidens est selonc II manieres, de coi l’une est semblans a gras nous, et li autre maniere est semblans a aposteme qui vient de nous d’artere;	 And such occurrences are in two ways, one resembling fatigue to us, and the other way is like an abscess that comes from our artery.
et il i ait paour, et ne covient mie ovrer de feir fuers que en celi qui est petite, et le prueve et cerche a tout l’intromissoire:	 And there may be fear, and it does not require working on large wounds except in that which is small, and try and search for everything related to it.
se tu le trueves ausi com I nout gras, et ne pent a nulle voine, si le cope, si com on cope les nous, et le trai a tout sa coife, s’il en i a point;	 If you find it as we have found fatigue, and not directed to any vein, then bandage like we bandage ours, and treat the area completely, if there is a spot.
et encerche bien tot, et le cure si com il covient, tant qu’il soit sanez parfaitement.	 And search thoroughly, and heal as it should be, until perfectly healthy again.
des nous	From us
Maintes manieres de nous sont, dont je dirai toutes les semblances;	 Many ways we have, of which I will tell all the similarities;
et or covient que je die toute la difference qui est entre nout et issue.	 And here one must say all the differences that exist between us and dislocation.
Je dis que issue est chalors et fievre tenans, tant que li ebulicions est passee, et est acomplie li porriture;	 I say that dislocation is heat and fever-ridden, as long as the boiling has not ceased, and the decay is complete.
adonques repose li fievre et li chalor.	 Then rests the fever and warmth.
Avec lou nout n’a ne chalor ne fievre ne dolor, et contient I syfac, qui est ses propres sac et est selonc la color dou cors, et encomence ausi com une jaisse, et devient gros;	 With ours there is no warmth or fever and pain, and it contains pus, which is its own sack and follows the color of the body, beginning as a jet, and becoming thickened.
et sont selonc II semblances, ou grais, ou moiste, et mout de color sont si com j’ai dit en la division.	 And it resembles in its appearance, either fatty or moist substance, with colors as I have described in the classification.
Il covient, quant tu viens a la cure dou nout, que tu esprueves et l’enquier premierement a tout l’estrument qui est apelez «entromissoire», selonc ce que sa forme venra ou chapistre qui est aprés.	When attending to the patient's wound, first examine and question with all the instrument called "intermitted," according to its form or procedure which is afterwards.
Et li maniere de l’inquisicion des apostemes des nous est que tu preignes ou plus moiste leu que tu trueves en l’aposteme, et torne tes dois poc et poc, tant que tu saiches que li estrumens ait perciet le keur, puis que ce soit selonc la grandor de l’aposteme;	 And the manner of inquiring into boils among us is that you grasp or find more moisture there than in the boil, and turn your fingers occasionally, until you know that the pus has pierced the skin, then according to the size of the boil.
puis estrai l’entromissoire, et pren garde en ceu que saut fuer.	 Then extract the interosseous, and take care so it does not bleed.
Se moistor corrans cort, queil color elle ait, si le fent si com j’ai dit des autres apostemes;	 If moisture runs through the vein, if it has any color as I have said of other abscesses;
et se aprés l’entromissoire nen vient moistor, saiches qu’il est gras, si le fent donques en croix, et le prent as pinceures, et l’escorche legierement de chescune part et warde la cotte ou il gist que tu la traies saine avec le nout;	 And after extracting the interosseous vein, if no moisture comes out, assume it is fatty, then incise in a cross pattern, and take pinchers to lightly scrape from each side, and cover the coat where it lies with a clean dressing.
et se tu ne la pues traire saine, si la trai par pieces si qu’il n’i demoure rien.	 And if you cannot cleanse it thoroughly, then cut into pieces so that nothing remains.
Car s’il i demoure rien, si revient li nous par maintes fois;	 Because if anything remains, it will return to us many times;
et s’il en demore un poc, et li sans te grieve, si emple la plaie d’aucunes poudres corrosives agues, et estraint la plaie, et met sus choses apaisans aposteme chaut, et le cure d’autres cures tant qu’il soit sanez;	 And if any remains and it does not hurt him, apply the wound with some corrosive powders, tighten the wound, and put on soothing substances for other remedies until it is healthy.
et se li nous est grans, si cout les II levres de la plaie, et le cure de ceu qui enjanre char.	 If it is severe, then cut the edges of the wound, and treat as if there were a festering sore.
et se li voine batans t’est contraire ou autre si te haste et emple le leu de vitriole broiet, et lou laisse liiet II jors ou III, tant que li plaie porrisse, et repose li ebulicion dou sanc;	 And if the boil appears contrary or other, apply vinegar and leave it on for two or three days until the wound heals, and allow rest to relieve blood congestion.
puis revien au coper ceu que i est demoreit dou nout.	 Then return to the previously mentioned treatment that was delayed in use.
Vez ci les formes des estrumens entromissoires, et sont de III manieres:	 Behold these forms of intruding sores, and there are three kinds:
grans et moien et petit;	 large and medium and small;
et s’en i a III quarrez qui sont apelez «albaret», et I qui est apelez «breb», et s’en i a de III manieres:	 And there are three types that are called "albaret", and one that is called "breb", and there are again three kinds;
grant, moien, et petit, por encerchier les apostemes de fistule;	 large, medium, and small to address abscesses of a fistula.
et sont ausi com les aguilles dont on cout les sorceles, et sont d’arain citrin, ou de fer, ou d’argent, et mues valent cil qui sont jaune, et sont plus esprovez de plonc noir por encerchier les corbeures de fistule;	 These are like the needles used in sorcery, made of brass, iron, or silver, and turning ones made of yellow color are more effective, and they are especially tried for finding haemorrhoids from a fistula.
et sont de III manieres:	 There are three kinds:
grans, moiens, et petis, selonc la quantiteit de la largesce des pertus.	 large, medium, and small, according to the size of their openings.
Les formes des oncines sont de mout de semblances, si com tu vois ci:	 The shapes of tumors are most similar to what you see here:
grans, moiens, et petis;	 large, medium, and small;
et si a oncines qui ont II corbeures de III manieres ausi;	 and if there are tumors that have hemorrhoids of three kinds as well;
et si a oncines qui ont III corbeures, et sont ausi de III manieres;	 and if there are tumors with three types of hemorrhoids, just like the sizes.
et si a oncines qui ont II corbeures, et oncines d’une corbeure soulement, et sont de III manieres;	 and if there are tumors that have two kinds of hemorrhoids, or only one kind, they too come in three sizes.
et tuit cist sont necessaire en lor leu.	 And all of these are necessary in their place.
Li chief de ces a coi on fent sont trenchant, et de telz i a qui ne taillent mie fuer que d’une part, dont on escorche les nous, por ceu c’on ne cope la voine ne le nerf;	 The primary tools used for these purposes are sharp ones, and among them there are those that do not cut at all but only scrape the skin, hence one does not sever the vein or nerve.
et de ces intromissoires sont les alemeles reponues en mainches, si que li malaide ne s’en persoivent a l’overture des apostemes;	 and among these instruments are those used to remove scabs, such that the patient does not feel them during the incision of abscesses.
et sont de III manieres:	 And there are three ways:
grant, petit, et moien, si com tu vois;	 large, small, and medium, as you see;
et n’en use on mie fuer que en leu charnut, si com jambes, et bras, et mameles, et as angres, et en semblans leus;	 And they are used only where the flesh is toughened, such as legs, arms, cheeks, and elbows, and other similar places.
et aucune fois fait on I autre estrument petit, semblant a escorces de fistices, selonc ceste forme, a coi on estainche sanc:	 And never is any other small instrument used, resembling the scrapers of lancet wounds, according to this form, which causes bleeding.
et le met on aucune fois au leu qui saine a copement des voines, et as arteres, et aucune fois reont selonc ceste grant forme:	And at no time is one placed in such a way that it touches the veins for copulation, and arteries, and again according to this great method:
Aucune fois enflent les mameles d’aucuns homes quant cil encomencent estre corrumput, tant qu’eles semblent mameles de feme;	 Never do the breasts of any men swell when they begin to be corrupted, until they appear like women's breasts.
et demorent laides et enflees, et qui les vuet curer, si le covient soier selonc ceste forme des ceste ligne .b. jusques a .g.:	 and remain ugly and swolled, and whoever wishes to heal them should do so according to the following form of this line... until b: g
puis escorche la graisse, et emple la plaie de medicine enjanrant char, puis assemble les II levres de la plaie a costure, et la cure tant qu’ele soit sanee;	 then scrape the fat, and apply medicinal pitch to the wound, then sew together the two edges of the wound with stitches, until it is cleaned.
et se li mamele cline aval, et est amolie por sa grandor si com il avient as femmes, si la fent en II costelz desus, par II semblans fendures;	 and the breast falls forward, and becomes soft due to its size like in women, making it into two rib-like folds above, with two similar splits.
de coi l’une soit tenans a l’autre a la fin de l’une et de l’autre, si que li plus grans ligne conteigne la menor selonc ceste forme, des ceste ligne .b. jusc’a la ligne .g.;	 to the point where one is held against the other at the end of each, so that the larger contains the smaller according to this form... from line b: up to line g.
puis escorche le cuir qui est entre les II levres, et oste la graisse, et i amenistre ceu que nos avons dit de costure et de poudres, et ceu qui est necessaire en la cure, tant qu’il soit sanez;	 Then scrape the skin between the two lips and remove the fat, then treat as we have mentioned with stitching and powders, and everything necessary for healing until it is clean.
et s’il n’est sanez, ou li incision n’est mie toute faite, por ceu que li malaides ne vuet reposer, ou por le decorrement de sanc, si covient que tu emplisses la plaie de coton moilliet en oignement corrosif;	 And if it is not clean, or the incision has not fully healed because the patient does not want to rest, or due to blood loss, then you must fill the wound with a pliable cotton ball soaked in corrosive ointment.
et le laisse tant qu’il menjuce le remenant et la graisse, puis le cure tant qu’il soit saneis.	 and leave it to heal until all remaining tissue and fat are gone, then cleanse it thoroughly until it is healthy again.
des apostemes des asselles	Of abscesses on the elbows
Cist apostemes que vienent desoz les asseles sont manieres de scrophules dures ou il ait cotes, et s’en i a que contienent moistor.	And often it is found in places or any swelling of, and are from them that the oment wherein lest.
Cil donques qui contienent moistor covient qu’il soient copez selonc ceste forme, des la ligne .b. jusc’a la ligne .g.:	 Those which contain moisture must be cut according to this form, from line b up to line g:
Et quant toute li bowe qui est en l’aposteme est vuidie, si emple la plaie de viel coton, et la laisse jusc’a l’autre jor, puis oste tout le coton, et cure d’oignement avenant a ceu tant qu’il soit sanez.	And when all the bowel that is in an abscess is emptied, fill the wound with old cotton and leave it until the next day, then remove all the cotton, and apply ointment until it heals.
Et se li apostemes est de semblances de scrophules, si le fent si com nos avons dit en fendures des scrophules, et se li plaie rent bowe, si amenistre cautere si com nos avons dit devant.	And if the abscess resembles like scrofula, treat it as we have described for the incisions of scrofula, and if the wound fills with bowels, prepare a fire cautery as we have described before.
de la routure de l’artere	Of the procedure of the artery
Quant li artere est route, et li cuir est soudez qui est sus, si en vient maintes fois apostemes, et tout aussi avient il a la voine enflee et aposteme;	 When the vein is exposed and the skin above it swells, thus there are often abscesses occurring multiple times, and similarly occurs an outbreak of gouty joints and ulcers.
et si le conoist on ensi quant c’est por l’artere, si est li apostemes lons em parfont;	 And if it is discovered at this stage for an artery, then there are large abscesses near.
et quant tu le sens a tes dois, si sens I estraignement;	 And when you feel it in your shoulders, you sense straining severely;
et quant c’est por la voine, si est reons defuer aparans;	 And if it is for the vein, then there are visible signs of insufficiency appearing.
et c’est folie de coper cest aposteme, et meismement quant il est desoz les asseles et as angres et ou col et em mout d’autres leus, et est mout grans.	 It is foolish to treat this abscess, and especially when it arises from joints and nerves and neck and involves many others, making it very large.
Il covient donques eschuir la cure de fer, et celui qui est a chief covient eschuir ausi, et en celui qui est d’enfleure d’artere fent par desus le cuir dou lonc;	 Therefore one must avoid the iron treatment, and for those at risk of head injury it is also avoided, as well as in cases where artery pressure occurs above long skin.
puis oevre la taille as oncines, et depart bellement l’artere des toiles, tant qu’ele soit descoverte;	 Then work the groin glands, and carefully remove the blood vessels from the sinews until they are exposed;
puis boute desoz li une aguille, et la fai percier jusc’a l’autre costeit, et estraint l’artere d’un fil double en II leus, selonc ceu que je t’ai ensigniet en l’estraction des II arteres qui sont en temples;	 Then insert a needle on one side and pierce until the opposite rib, and tie off the artery with a double thread for two fingers, as I have shown you in the extraction of the two arteries that are behind the ears.
puis point le leu qui est entre les II liens d’un intromissoire tant que li sans en isse qui i est, et soit deliiez li aposteme;	 Then pinpoint the joint which is between the two threads of a trocar until no blood flows out from it, and then open the abscess.
puis amenistre la cure que enjanre bowe, tant que li liien chient;	 Then perform the suturing as required by the wound, while ensuring that the ligature bites.
puis cure ceu d’oignement avenant a ceu, tant qu’il soit sanez;	 Then apply appropriate ointment for this matter until it is cleaned.
et se li apostemes est por la taille de la voinne, si covient que tu teignes a ta main ceu que tu pues de l’aposteme a tout le cuir, puis boute l’aguille desoz le leu que tu tiens a ta main, et la fai percier, et i ait I fil double, si que tu le trais de l’autre costeit;	 And if the abscess is large in size for the vein, it is necessary to treat your hand as you would the entire skin of the abscess with an ointment, then insert a needle on one side that you hold in your hand and pierce until the opposite rib, and tie off with a double thread.
puis lie l’aposteme, si com je t’ai dit, ou liien de l’une de II pars as II chiés dou fil;	 Then treat the abscess as I have told you, or if it lies between one part of the two shoulders.
et se tu doutes que li filz n’isse fuer, si i reboute une autre aguille a tout I fil desoz tout l’aposteme a l’incision de la premiere aguille, et estraint les filz en IIII leus;	 And if you doubt that the threads are not all gone, then it pushes another needle through all the threads from underneath the abscess to the incision of the first needle, and pulls the threads in four directions.
puis cope l’aposteme tant que li superfluitez en isse, puis cope la superfluiteit dou keur et laisse ceu qui est liiez;	 Then excise the abscess until no excess tissue remains, then cut away any remaining pus and leave what is attached.
puis met sus I drapeil moilliet en vin et en oile, puis li amenistre cures de tentes et d’oignemens tant qu’il soit sanez.	 Then apply a compress of wool soaked in wine and oil, then treat with bandages and salves until it is healed.
des apostemes des ners	Of abscesses of veins
Ausi com aposteme vienent en l’artere et en la voine, vienent aposteme as ners quant il sont ferut, ou par trop grant travail, et semblans choses.	Similarly, abscesses come from the artery and vein; they form in the nerves when struck or due to excessive strain, and similar occurrences.
Et ceu avient plus sovent as adjutoires et as dois et en toz leus ou il ait jointures, et c’est I grief apostemes, et sa color semble la color dou cors, et est em plusors dispositions sens dolor;	 And this occurs more often in shoulders and arms with all the joints, and it is severe abscesses, and its appearance resembles that of the body, causing pain in various ways.
et quant on l’estraint forment, si sent li malaides dolor, et n’est mie em parfont dou cors, mais desoz lou keur;	 And when it is strongly held back, the patient feels great pain, and it is not throughout the whole body, but from below the head.
et muet bien de toutes pars, et ne va ne avant ne arrier, ne desoz ne desus, et celui qui est en jointures ne covient mie coper par fer:	 And he moves badly all over, and cannot go forward or backward, nor up nor down, and those who are in the joints do not need to be bound with iron.
par aventure i vanroit contraction;	 there may well be spasms;
et cil qui est ou chief ou ou front, fent le cuir au spatumile.	 and those who have it at the head or forehead cause swelling in the temple area.
Se li apostemes est petis, si le tien a unes tenailles, et le cope en sa racine;	 If the abscess is small, then treat it with tweezeboots and bandage at its base;
et s’il est grans, si le sospent a l’oncine, et l’escorche, puis l’oste et assemble la plaie a la costure, et lou cure tant qu’il soit sanez.	 And if it is large, then drain it with a hook, scrape away the dead tissue, then stitch up the wound and dress it until healed.
des grosses boces pendans	Heavy hanging mouths
Aucune fois avient en ventres et ne mie autre part thelul, et est une maladie qui est apelee «funge» par la semblance d’aus, et est li racine subtilz, et li chiez gros;	 Never occurs in wombs or elsewhere, and it is an illness called "fungus" due to its appearance, and the roots are subtle, but the stems are thick.
et en i a de petis et de mout grans;	 And there are both small and very large ones.
et je vis I home qui en avoit II ou ventre qui estoient plus semblans a funges que ai autre chose, et n’i avoit point de difference, et estoient blanc, et avoient menue racine, et estoient jai fendut, et en corroit adés moistor.	 I have seen patients with two wombs that appeared more like fungi than anything else, without any difference; they were white, had fine roots, and were cracked, containing moisture within.
Je les copai et trovai en l’un XVIII onces pesant, et en l’autre VI З., et li ovraiges en l’incision si est que tu regardes se li malaides est moistes, et li color de l’artelul est blainche et moiste et de subtil racine;	 I weighed them and found the first to be eighteen ounces, and the other six pounds, and upon incision one observes if the patient is moist, with the arterial color being pale and wet and of a subtle root.
si le cope au spatumile large, et soient en ta presence li cautere au feu.	 If the cloth at the thigh is wide, and have the fire cautery in your presence.

et se les racines sont grosses, si a paour au coper meismement por le ventre, mais tu em pues bien coper la moitiet, puis le cauterize qu’il ne reviegne;	 And if the roots are large and you fear for the abdomen, but adequately cover most of it with a cup then cauterize so that it does not return.

Car c’est uns apostemes enchancrez, et je venrai a la cure de chancre ci aprés.	For it is an advanced syphilis, and I will treat the chancroid hereafter.
quant li boude ist fuer	When the mouth jaw is injured
Se li apparance de la boude vient par cautere de plaie ou de fendure de syfac, et est sus le ventre et en ist aucuns des bouez, si com il avient en autres routures, ou de sanc qui cort de voines ou d’arteres selonc ceu qui est devant, ou de ventositeit;	 If the appearance of gangrene comes from a wound or incision infection, and it is on the belly with none elsewhere as occurs in other regions, where blood flows from veins or arteries depending on what is seen before, or swelling.
et se c’est par la routure dou syfac et par l’issue dou bouel, si est li color de l’aposteme semblans a la color dou cors, et est legiere chose sens dolor, et apert de diverse issue.	 And if it is from the infection of the gum and by the exit of pus, then its appearance is similar to that of normal skin color, feels like a minor thing with little pain, and has various issues arising from it.
Et se c’est por l’issue de l’intestine, adonques est il plus divers, et quant on le presse a ses dois si se repont, et puis revient, et par aventure si est sarrez, et agrandist mout a l’entree dou bain et por fort travail.	If it is due to an intestinal issue, then it becomes more diverse, and when pressed at its limits, it rebounds, and then returns, and by chance it may be swollen, and greatly enlarges the entrance to the bath and for vigorous work.
Et se c’est por moistor, c’est legiere chose, et apert bien quant tu le presses a ta main, ne ne constraint mie;	 And if it is due to moisture, it is a minor thing, and appears normal when you press it with your hand, do not restrict movement.
et se c’est por sanc, si apert par ces signes li apostemes gros et dur, et est fichiez selonc une quantiteit;	 And if it is for blood, when large and hard abscesses are opened by these signs, they grow and become embedded in accordance with the quantity.
et se c’est por ventositeit, si est souef au tochier, et li ovraiges si est que tu regarde se li apparance est por le sanc de l’artere, ou de la voine, ou ventositeit.	 And if it is for inflammation, when tender upon touching, and the appearance of the wound seems to be related to arterial blood or vein or inflamm ization.
Si covient que tu laisses la cure.	 If it is necessary to leave the wound open for healing.
Car il en a doutance et paor, si com je t’ai dit ou chapistre des apostemes, por l’artere et por la voine.	 For there may be doubt and fear, as I have described in the chapter on abscesses, concerning arteries and veins.
Et se li apparance est por l’intestine ou lou boueil, si covient que tu comandes au malaide qu’il teigne son alaine, et soit estendus tout drois, puis seigne d’enche tout entor la boude;	 And if the appearance is of intestines or bowels, then you command the patient to stretch out his legs and extend them straight, then encircle him entirely with a belt.

puis oevre la moitiet de l’aposteme estendut sus le liien, et i boute ton doit indice, et quier l’intestine;	 Then work on extending a portion of the abscess over the joint, and insert your instrument, piercing it into the intestines.
se tu le trueves pris dou liien, si le deslie, et boute l’intestine au defuer dou ventre;	 If you find the joint captured, detach it, and push the intestine back through to its original position in the abdomen.
et se tu trueves le boueil, si le prent a l’oncine, et en cope la superfluiteit;	 And if there is a boil, grasp it with forceps, and remove any excess material.
et se li artere te fait contraire, ou li voine, si vai belement entor, puis revien a ton ovraige et pren II aguilles, et i boute II fors filz, et boute les II aguilles entor ceu que tu as fait en crois que tu feis percier;	 And if the artery is in an unfavorable position or bleeding profusely, then return to your work and take two needles. Bore through them with a threaded cord and place the two needles around where you have previously made a cross incision for piercing.
puis estrain l’aposteme en IIII leus sus les aguilles, et se tu vues, oste les aguilles, et laisse lou leu tant qu’il porrisse, et chiece li char morte par soi;	 Then strain the abscess into four layers beneath the needles, and if you see it, remove the needles, and let the place rest until it heals, and extract the dead tissue by yourself.
ou tu la cope quant elle iert subtiliie et porrie, puis le cure de ceu qu’il covient, et cheve l’aposteme si com nos avons dit;	 Then you shall bind it if it is thin and suitable, then treat as necessary, and remove the abscess as we have said.
et estrai le sanc ou la moistor que tu trueves, puis cure le leu de ceu qu’il couvient, et soude le leu.	 And extract any blood or pus that you find, then treat the place as necessary, and close the wound.
dou chancre	On the ulceration

de ydropisie	And for dropsy, which means edema due to fluid retention in the body, causing swelling: apply a concoction of rosen with roses and ointment and pour on l'estuin, et les eaux; puis giete li detergens le morsel de l'eau-lui.

si est eclites soulement;	 If it only oozes;

c’est a savoir, tympanites et yposarche, car c’est mortelz chose;	 That is to say, tympanitis and hyposarca, for it is a deadly thing. - Tympanitis refers to inflammation of the eardrum (tympanic membrane), while hyposarca might be referring to
donques quant tu medicines ceste semblance de ydropisie qui est apelee «eclites» de medicines, et li cure ne profite, si regarde se li malaides est foibles, ou s’il ait autre maladie que ydropisie, si com toust et solution de ventre et semblans choses;	 Therefore when you treat this resemblance of dropsy called "oozing" with medicines and the treatment does not help, check if the patient is weak or has another disease besides dropseris, such as constipation and similar things. - Here, it's discussing how to approach a case that initially presents like dropsy (a condition characterized by an accumulation of fluid in tissues) but doesn't respond to standard treatments for the illness. si n’i touchier de fer, car il i a doutance;	 If you do not touch it with iron, for there is doubt;

de la circoncision	Regarding circumcision
Circoncision n’est mie desliemens de continuation si com les autres plaies;	 Circumcision is not an ongoing disjunction like other wounds;
toutevoie quant nos faison ceste oevre de nostre volenteit, et proprement as enfans, si est mestier que nos faisiens la millor oevre, et la plus legiere a salut.	 However, if we do this work of our own accord, and properly for children, it is necessary that we make the best possible work, and the easiest to health.
Je dis que li ancien ne dirent mie la circoncision de lor enfans, car il n’en usent mie en lor loi, et n’en avons mais que ceu que nos avons aquis par experiment.	I say that the ancients did not practice childhood circumcision, for it is not done in their law, and we have only what we have gained through experience.
Car j’ai veut la plus grant partie des maistres et des sainors qui faisoient circumcision entor I dal, et as forces, et a tout une novacule;	 Because I have observed most masters and healers performing circumcision in the dawning light, at times of force, and on any occasion.

dou retenement de l’urine	Regarding urine retention
Li retenue de l’urine si est d’opilation de piere, ou de sanc congeleit, ou de bowe, ou de char nee, ou de semblans choses, que nos avons dit en la division;	 The retention of urine is due to the compression of stones, or frozen blood, or arrows, or nettles, or similar things as we have said in that section.

des maladies de la vessie	diseases of the bladder
Quant escorcheures ou sanc vient en la vessie, ou porriture i est assemblee, et tu i vues distiller aigues et medicines, si fai a tout l’estrument qui est apellé «clepsedre», et c’est li forme:	When scrapes or blood enters the bladder, or putrefaction is present therein, and you see to distill waters and medicines, make use of the entire instrument called "clyster," which is thus formed:
