II d’une part, et I d’autre, si com tu vois;	 On one hand, and on the other, as you see;
et li leus chevez par coi li medicine cort soit telz qu’il estoupe bien la verge sens adition, si c’on em puisse traire la moistor, et bouter quant mestier est;	 And the roots from which the medicinal paste is such that it well fills the member without addition, and if one can draw out the moisture, and do so as needed.
et quant tu vues giter tes medicines en la vessie, met le chief dou keusteur en la moistor, et trai au traiant qui est ens;	 And when you see to apply your medicines in the bladder, place the scorching stick where there is moisture, and draw out what can be drawn.
si trairas la moistor au kesteur, et puis reboute fort le traiant ens;	 If you draw out the moisture with the burning stick, and then strongly reshape it as possible.
si entrera li moistors ens, et venra a la vessie maintenant, si que li malaides la sentira;	 If there is entry of moisture there, and comes to the bladder now, so that the patient will feel it.
et c’est li forme dou clistere subtil dont on clisterize la vessie:	 And this is the form of the subtle cleansing for which we cleanse the bladder:
si est ci:	 If it occurs thusly:
Et est d’argent ou d’archaut, et est li chiés plus haut;	 And it is of silver or copper, and the head is higher.
et desoz a I sein ou li liiens chiet;	 and from under the neck where the ligaments tear;
puis pren une vessie de mouton et i met la moistor dont tu vues clisterizer la vessie, puis la lie entre les II seins forment d’un boin fil double, et chaufe I poc celle moistor sus le feu;	 then take a sheep bladder and put the moisture inside that you wish to use for an enema on the bladder, then tie it between the two nipples with a strong double thread, and heat the moisture over fire.
puis boute le chief dou clistere en la verge, puis estrain ta main sus la vessie a tout la moistor avenanment, tant que li malaides sente que celle moistor est jai venue a la vessie;	 then insert the head into the enema, and press your hand against the bladaderly moisture as soon as it reaches the bladder.
et se tu n’as la vessie, si pren une piece de parchemin, et en fai I cercle, et le perce rondement entor;	 and if you do not have a bladder, take a piece of parchment, make it into a circle, and pierce it roundly through.
puis boute I fil fort en ces pertus, puis assemble le cercle si com on assemble I dal, et met dedens ceu que tu vues d’oile et de moistor et d’aigue, et le lie en l’estrument;	 Then blow a strong thread through these perforations, then form the circle as you would with a peg and hole, and fill inside what you see of oil, moisture, and water, and bind it in the instrument.
et fai si com tu as fait de la vessie, de presser a ta main tant que li moistor veigne a la vessie.	 And do so as you did with the bladder, pressing until the moisture reaches the bladder.
de la piere	Of the stone
Nos avons jai dit en la division les manieres de piere, et l’estraction ensamble medicines;	 We have already described in this section methods of stone removal and extracting arrows collectively with remedies;
et ai dit la difference entre la piere enjanree as rains, et toz les signes, et en queil piere on doit ovrer de taille;	 And I have explained the difference between stones inward of rain and all other signs, and where stone you must work by cutting.
et en la vessie, et en la verge;	 And in the bladder, and in the penis;
et je le vos dirai apertement et briément.	 And I will tell it openly and briefly.
Je dis que li piere qui est enjanree en la vessie si avient plus sovent as enfans, et c’est signe que li aigue saut de la vessie semblans a aigue en sa subtiliteit;	 I say that stones lodged within the bladder occur more often in children, and this is a sign that water springs from the bladard like to a watery subtlety.
et i apert harene, et graite li malaides sa verge, et li pent maintes fois, et puis enroidist;	 And he has bare skin, and grieves the patient greatly with his rod, and strikes him many times, then immobilizes.
et a mout de ces saut li fondemens;	 and it is part of these blows that shakes the foundation;
et est legiere li sanation des enfans jusqu’il ont IIII ans, et est mout grief en viellars, et est as jones moiene, a ces qui sont entre jonesce et viellece;	 and it is lightly healing for children up to four years old, but very severe in the elderly, and moderate for those who are between youth and old age.
et est li cure plus legiere de ces qui ont la piere grans, que de ces qui l’ont petite.	 and it is a lighter treatment for those with large stones than for those with small ones.
Et quant nos venons a la cure, si couvient premier mundifier le malaide per clistere, por traire tout le fiens qui est as intestines.	 And when we come to treatment, it is necessary first to cleanse the patient by enema, in order to expel all feces from within the intestines.
Car il encombre aucune fois a querir la piere.	 For sometimes it may obstruct the stone.
Puis prenez le malaide par les piez, et lou deboutez et movez au desoz, si que li piere dessende au parfont de la vessie, et saille aucune fois dou leu haut;	 Then take the patient by the feet and stand them up, bending backwards so that the stone descends to the front of the bladwock, without any sign of blood coming out from the back.
puis le fai seoir entre tes mains appareilliet, et ses mains soient desoz ses cuisses, si que li vessie soit toute declinans aval;	 Then make them sit between your hands spread apart, with their hands behind their thighs, so that the bladder slopes downwards.
puis la quier et la touche dedens;	 Then grasp and touch within; 
se tu sens la piere en l’espaice, si te haste maintenant de taillier sus la piere.	 If you feel the stone in the space, quickly cut near the stone.
Et s’elle ne chiet au touchier dou tout, si moille ton doi indice d’oile de la main senestre, se li malaides est enfes, ou ton doi moien, se li malaides est jovencelz acomplis;	 And if it does not pass with the probe at all, grease your index finger of the left hand with oil, if the patient is a child or an adult.
et le boute en son fondement, et quier la piere, et quant tu la sens a ton doi, si l’amoine au col de la vessie;	 and place it at its base, then press on the stone, and when you feel it in your finger, amputate near the bladder neck.
puis presse sus a ton doi, et la boute au defuer lai ou tu vues taillier.	 then press with your finger, and remove the residual part where you see cut.
Et comande au ministre qu’il presse la vessie a sa main, et li comande qu’il estende a sa main destre les coions en haut, et a sa main senestre oste le cuir qui est desoz les coions en la partie ou on fait la taille;	 And instruct the minister to press the bladres with his hand, and command him to extend upwards with his right hand the loins, and with his left hand remove the skin that is below the loins at the part where you make the cut.
puis i boute le spatumile copant, de coi ce est li forme:	 Then apply the splinting bandage so this is its shape:
Et fent entre ceu qui est entre les coions et le fondement, ne mie em mileu mais au costeit de la naige senestre;	 And make it between those who are between the joints and the foundation, not in the middle but to the left of the navel.
et soit drois sus la piere, et tes dois soit adés ou fondement, et soit li taille dou traver si qu’ele soit large par defuer, et dedens estroite, selonc la quantiteit de la piere, ne mie trop grans;	 And it should be straight above the stone, and your hands should touch either its top or base, and extend the rope as wide as needed if broad, and dense within, according to the quantity of the stone, not too large.
par aventure la presse si li dois qui est ou fondement, qu’elle saut fuer sens travail;	 In case you press the hand that is either on top or at the base, so it moves without effort.
et saiches qu’il i a teil piere ou il a angles, et marges:	 And know if there are any pieces of stone or edges and borders:
si est griés a issir;	 If they are stuck in trying to remove them;
et si a teil qui est souez, semblans a une glant, et reonde, dont li issue est legiere.	 And if there is any part that resembles a slit, round, and whose removal is easy.
A celi donques ou il a angles et marge, fai la taille plus grant;	 When you encounter joints with edges and margins, make the incision larger.
et s’elle ne saut, si covient que tu estraignes sus as tenailles qui sont ausi com une lime au chief, por mues estraindre la piere si qu’elle n’eschaipe;	 And if it does not yield, then you must use forceps similar to a file on the head, to extract the stone so that it doesn't escape.
ou tu boute desoz li I estrument subtil corbé au chief;	 or you insert an instrument with a subtle hooked end underneath;
et se tu ne la pues engignier ensi, si eslarge I poc lou pertus, et se li sans decort, si l’estrainche de vitriole;	 and if you cannot achieve it this way, slightly widen the opening, and if the stone is thickened, then extract with vinegar.
et s’il i a plus d’une piere, si boute premier la plus grant au col de la vessie, puis cope sus, puis le trai fuer, et les petites aprés s’il en i a plusors.	 and if there are multiple stones, first extract the largest from the bladder neck, then remove it with your fingers, and afterwards crush it, and do the same for any smaller ones that remain.
Et s’elle est mout grans, si la covient soier, et faire plus grant plaie.	 And if it is very large, one must soften it, causing a larger wound.
Car II choses avienent au malaide:	 For two things occur in patients:
ou il muert, ou li urine vient adés par lai que li leus ne puet souder;	 When he dies or the urine flows again through the part where the flesh cannot join.
mais toutevoie t’efforce dou traire, ou dou debrisier as tenailles, tant que tu la traies par pieces;	 Nonetheless, strive to drain with a syringe or debridement using pincers until you have treated it in pieces.
et quant tu as acomplit ton oevre, si emple la plaie d’encens et d’aloe et de sanc de dragon, et l’estraint, et met par sus I drapeil moilliet en oile et en vin, ou en oile et en aigue rose et aigue froide, por apaisier l’aposteme chaut;	 And once you have completed your work, apply the wound with incense and aloe and dragon's blood, and bandages, and place moistened cloths soaked in oil and wine, or oil and pink and cold water to cool the hot sore.
puis resovine le malaide sus son col, et ne desliier lou lien jusc’au tier jor.	 Then wrap the patient's neck with bandages without untying them until the next day.
Et quant tu le desliies, si arose mout bien lou leu d’oile et d’aigue, puis le cure d’oignement dyafinicon et d’oignement basilicon, tant qu’il soit sanez.	When you reset it, raise the area well with oil and water, then treat with the ointment diafiniticum and basilicon until healed.
Et se apostemes chaus vient en la plaie et corrosions, et congelemens de sanc en la vessie, et soit par ceu retenue li urine, qui est conue en teil maniere que sans saut avec l’urine:	 And if the sore is present in the wound and tissue deterioration occurs, with blood clotting in the bladder causing it to be unable to pass urine as seen by a lack of stream.
boutes donques ton doi en la plaie, et estrai celui sanc, car s’il i remaint, si corront la vessie, et la porrit;	 Therefore bend your elbow into the wound, and extract that blood, for if it remains, then blisters and pus will form.
puis leve la plaie d’aigue et d’aisil et de seil, et li aide en toutes les manieres que tu seis, tant qu’il soit sanez;	 Then lift the wound from water and filth and wind, and treat it in all ways you know of until it is healed.
et covient que toutes les oures que tu le cures, que tu li lie les II cuisses, et assemble les medicines sus le leu.	 And it is necessary that for all wounds you treat, bind him with two leg wraps and apply the ointments on site.
Et se li piere est petite, et ele est ou conduit de la verge, et fichie ens, et li urine ne puet issir;	 And if the stone is small and it comes from the penis and protrudes out, and he cannot urinate.
si le cure de ceu que je dis ainsois, que tu lou tailles maintes fois, est on escusez de la taille per ceste cure.	 If you treat as I say hereafter, do the procedure many times, ensuring to unwind the scrotum with this treatment.
Je ai ja ce proveit ensi.	 I have also experienced this thus.
Pren .i. foret de fer selonc ceste forme et soit a .iij. angles fichiees en .i. tison:	Take an iron bar in the following shape and make it at three sharp points like stakes:
puis pren I fil et lou lie entor la verge desoz la piere, si qu’ele ne puist venir arrier en la vessie;	 Then take a thread around the shaft below the head so that it cannot come back into the bladder.
puis boute le foret en la verge legierement, tant qu’il viegne a la piere;	 Then insert the probe gently into the shaft until it reaches the head.
et torne le foret a ta main en la piere poc et poc, tant que tu puisses percier la piere d’autre part;	 And turn the probe towards your hand in the head slowly and slowly, as you can pierce through to the other side of the stone.
si venra tantost li urine, puis presse ta main sus ceu qui est demorez de la piere qui est dedens la verge.	 The urine will come out soon, then press your hand on what remains lodged in the head within the shaft.
Si est tantost brisie, et saut fuer avec l’urine, et est garis li malaides;	 If it is broken quickly and comes out with the urine, and the patient is relieved.
et se tu ne pues ce faire por aucune chose qui le deffent, si lie I fil desoz la piere et I autre desus, puis fent la verge endroit la piere entre les II liiens, puis l’estrai fuer, et deslie lou liien, et mundifie lou sanc congeleit qui est en la plaie;	 And if you cannot do it for any reason that prevents it, then tie a thread below the head and another above, then break the shaft at the place between the two threads, extract it forcefully, loosen the ligatures, and cleanse the congealed blood in the wound.
et le cure tant qu’il soit sanez.	 And treat until it becomes healthy again.
de la piere des femmes	From the stones of women (referring to uterine stones or fibroids)
Poc avient que piere soit enjanree en femmes, et s’il avient aucune fois, si est li cure grief, et est deffendut por III choses:	 Occasionally a stone may be found in women, and if it occurs once, then the treatment is serious, and there are three things to avoid.
l’une est que per aventure li femme est vierge;	 One is that perhaps the woman might be a virgin;
et li seconde est c’on ne puet trover femme bien saichant qui se descuevre as mires, meismement quant elle est caste.	 and the second is that one cannot find a wise woman who knows how to undress in front of strangers, especially if she is chaste.
Et li tierce maniere si est que par aventure on ne puet trover femme bien saichant en cest art de mains;	 And the third way is that perhaps one cannot find a knowledgeable woman in this art of hands;
et li quarte maniere si est que li piere de la femme si est plus em parfont que li piere de l’ome, por coi il i couvient faire plus parfonde taille, et grant paour i a. Et se necessitez semont a ceu, si covient que tu preignes une mieresse bien sachant, et a poines la trueve on, et se tu n’en trueves, point si quier I caste mire subtil;	 and the fourth way is that the stone in the woman's body is more embedded than in men, so it requires deeper cutting, and there is much fear involved. And if necessary, one must find a very knowledgeable midwife, and carefully seek her out, and if you do not find such, then no matter how chaste she may be, she must have subtle skills;
et li presente une baile bien saige en la vie des femmes, ou une femme qui saiche une partie de l’art, et li comande qu’ele faice ceu que tu li comandes de l’inquisicion de la piere;	 And this presents a skilled hand in women's lives, or a woman who knows part of the art, and he commands that she performs what you command regarding the stone examination.
et regarde mout bien se li femme est vierge:	 And look very carefully if the woman is a virgin.
adonques li covient bouter son doit ou fondement et querir la piere;	 Then it is necessary to apply a bandage or foundation and seek the stone.
et s’ele la trueve, si la constraigne desoz son doit, et li recomande qu’elle boute son doit ou con la malaide, et quiere et presse sa main senestre sus la vessie forment.	 And if it bleeds, then bind it below the bandage and instruct that they apply a new bandage or hold it with their left hand over the swollen vein, wanting to press it.
S’elle la trueve, si covient qu’elle la mueve de greit en greit des l’entree de la vessie jusque desoz, tant qu’elle viegne a la racine de la cuisse;	 If it bleeds, then they should move it gradually from the entrance of the vein to below, until it reaches the root of the thigh.
puis cope sus la piere en la racine de la cuisse encontre le mileu dou con, lai ou il est mues apparilliet, et sent la piere en celle partie;	 then push against the stone at the root of the thigh towards the middle part where it is protruding, and feel for the stone in that area.
et ne mueve son doi desus la piere ou desoz, et soit li taille au premier petite;	 and do not move his finger over or under the stone, and be sure to grasp at the first small part.
puis boute lou rait en la taille, se tu sens la piere si acroi la plaie tant que li piere puisse issir fuer, et saiches que maintes manieres de pieres sont:	 Then insert the staff into the waist; if you feel the stone within, believe in the wound so that the stone may be removed forcefully, and know that there are many ways to deal with stones.
c’est a savoir, petites et grans et aspres et souez, longes et reondes, et qui ont rains.	 This is known: small and large and sharp and smooth, elongated and round, and that have veins.
si saiches les semblances por savoir l’issue.	 If you examine similar cases to know the outcome.
Et se li sans te vaint, si met au leu vitriole broiet, et li tien une houre tant que li sans soit estainchiez;	 And if the stone does not yield, then apply a poultice of white lead powder, and hold it there until the stone is expelled.
puis revien a ton ovraige, tant que li piere soit fuer, et aies des estrumens que je t’ai dit en l’estraction de la piere as homes por toi aidier en ton oevre;	 Then return to your work, until the stone is loose, and have the remedies I told you about for stone extraction at home to help you in your work.
et se li sans te vaint, et c’est de l’artere qui est copee, si met la poudre sus le leu et l’estrain de tentes et de bendelz, et ne rencomencier plus ceu, et laisse la piere et ne la traire mie, que par aventure morroit li malaide;	 And if the stone does not yield, and it is from an artery that has burst, then apply powder on the site and wrap tightly with bandages and ties, and do not repeat this method again, and let the stone pass without traction unless by chance the patient faints.
puis cure la plaie.	 Then treat the wound.
Et quant li chalor dou sanc est apaisie, et li leus porrist, si revien a ton ovraige, tant que li piere soit fuer.	And when the fever of blood is calmed and the limb restored, return to your work until the bone is strong.
de hernie carnouse	Of a groin hernia
Ramice aquouse n’est autre chose que assemblee de moistor ou blanc syfac, qui est desoz lou keur des coions, que contient l’uef;	 Next, pus is nothing but a gathering of moisture or scabs, which are under the skin near the joints, contained in the blister.
et est apelez «syfac», et aucune fois est proprement en la toile de l’uef, si c’on cuide que ce soit I autre oef;	 and is called "scab," and it is never properly within the skin of the blister, if one thinks it is something else.
et c’est li cuir dou coion entre lou blanc syfac que nos avons dit;	 and this is the leather-like tissue between the scabs that we have mentioned;
et ceu n’avient se poc non.	 And this does not happen often.
Et li generation de cest ramice si est de foibleteit que vient as coions, et est espandue celle matiere.	And the formation of this pus is due to weakness in the joints, and it spreads that material.
Et aucune fois si vient de percussion sus les coions, et ceste moistor si a maintes colors:	 And at no time if it comes from striking upon the joints, and this moisture is of many kinds:
ou c’est color declinans a jaunice, ou c’est sans rouge, ou noir, ou aquous blans, et ce avient plus;	 or its color wanes to jaundice, or it lacks redness, or turns black, or becomes watery white, and this occurs more frequently.
et ce sont li signe de conoistre ceste assemblee, car s’elle est ou blanc syfac que nos avons dit, si est li apostemes reons, I poc lonc si com li figure d’un oef, et n’apert mie li coions, car il a moistor tout entor.	 and these are the signs of recognizing this assembly, for if it is or becomes white as we have mentioned, then the abscesses reopen, they do not remain long like an egg's shape, and do not pierce the joints because there is moisture all around.
Et s’il a moistor en la propre toile, si est li apostemes reons avec une partie de l’uef, et por ceu pense on que c’est uns autres oef;	 And if it has moisture in its own tissue, then the abscesses reopen with part of the egg, and for this reason one thinks it is another egg.
et se li moistor est entre le cuir des coions et le blanc syfac, si le sent om bien;	 And if there is moisture between the skin of the elbows and the shiny saddle bone, it feels quite well.
donques quant tu vues savoir la color de la moistor, si esprueve a tout l’intromissoire quarreit, de coi li forme est ci devant.	 Therefore, when you see to know the color of the moisture, if it spreads over all the surrounding area, that is why there are marks beforehand.
Selonc ceu donques qui vient aprés l’intromissoire, juge de ceu qui est dedens.	According to what follows after the intermission, judge according to what is within.
Et quant nos la curons par fer, si covient que li malaides soit sainiez selonc som pooir et la repletion de son cors;	 And when we cauterize with iron, it is necessary for the patient to be healthy according to their ability and fullness of body.
puis le sovine sus son dos, sus une chose un poc haute, et met desoz lui mout de drapelz;	 Then you heat on his back, upon something slightly raised, and place a lot of linens under him.
puis sié sus sa senestre, et comande au ministre qu’il sié a destre, et estende la verge a l’un des II costelz dou keur des coions;	 Then sit on his left side, and command the assistant to sit to your right, and extend the rod towards one of the two ribs below the elbow joint.
puis pren le spatumile leit, et cope le cuir des coions parmi leu dou lonc jusque delez lou poignil, et soit ta fendure toute droite en devisant le cuir des coions jusc’a syfac blanc, et l’escorche subtilment selonc tom pooir;	 Then take the spatula and cut the skin of the elbangs along their length up to the wrist, and make your incision straight while turning the skin towards the shiny saddle bone, and peel it delicately as far as possible.
puis perce lou syfac plain d’aigue a I large pertus, et estrai toute l’aigue, et puis met tes oncines, et estent lou syfac amont;	 Then pierce the sack full of water through its wide opening, and extract all the water, and then apply linen bandages, and elevate the sack.
et ne touchier le keur des coions, mais que le syfac soulement;	 and do not touch the edge of the wound, but only the sack itself;
cope tout ou par pieces meismement le costeit de lui subtil, que se tu ne le copes bien saigement, si revenra li aigue;	 cut very finely along its edges, such that if you do not cut it neatly and cleanly, the water will return.
et se l’uef saut fuer a ton oevre, si le ramoinne en son leu quant tu avras acomplit l’uevre dou syfac;	 and if the egg springs forth from your work, then reset the limb in its place when you have completed the task with the sack.
puis assemble les II leivres dou keur des coions a une costure, puis le cure si com les autres plaies, tant qu’il soit sanez.	 Then sew together the two edges of the wound securely, then treat it as you would other injuries until it is healed.
Et se tu trueves l’uef corromput d’autre maladie, si covient que tu lies les vasselz que sont suspensoire, en doutant le decorrement de sanc;	 And if you find the egg to be spoiled by another disease, it is necessary that you tie up the vessels that are swollen, fearing bleeding.
puis cope le coion a tout le suspensoire, et estrai l’uef, et le cure si com nos avons dit.	 Then cut away any excess sinew, remove the bone splinter, and treat it as we have said.
Et se aigue est assemblee en II parties ensamble, saiches que ce sont II ramices;	 And if an artery is split into two parts together, ensure that they are two branches.
si cope l’autre partie si com tu as fait la premiere igalment, puis essue lou sanc, et met en la plaie lainne moillie en oile roset;	 Cut the other part just as you did the first equally, then stop the bleeding, and place a cloth soaked in rose oil into the wound.
et met defuer autre laine moillie en vin et en oile, et met sus les II coions, et met desus drapelz doublés, et le lie sus a tout le liien qui est selonc ceste forme:	 And apply another cloth soaked in wine and oil on top of it, place cloths over the two joints, then cover with doubled sheets, and bind everything as described by this method.
Puis pren II drapelz, et les emple de laine charpie selonc ceste semblance et soient assemblez par cousture en la gorle des braies, et li uns des chiés preigne sus le fondement jusc’au dos, et li autres a la partie dou poignil;	 Then take two more sheets and place them with shredded cloth as shown here, sewn together at the waistband, and one sheet should be pulled up to the back from the foundation, while the other is placed on the part near the wrist.
et li autre dui chief sus les II angres, et soit toute assemblee li restreinture en la boucle dou braier;	 And the other two heads above the shoulders, and it is fully secured within the loop of the shirt.
et aucune fois est medicinee ceste ramice de cautere en leu de taille de fer, et est que tu preignes I cautere cultellaire subtil, et cope le cuir des coions, et soit eschaufez si com nos avons dit, si que li syfac blanc que contient l’aigue est descovers;	 And this method of cautery is akin to iron bandaging in size and type, with the use of a delicate knife-like cauterizer, covering the leather straps, ensuring they are sufficiently heated as we have described, so that the white sap which contains water is revealed.
si pren lou cautere selonc ceste forme, et perce celui syfac as oncines, et l’escorche a cest subtil cautere chaut:	 If you take the cautery in this manner and pierce that sap with thorns, and scrape off using this hot delicate cauterizer.
Et lou cope en toutes les manieres que tu pues, tant que tu esraiches tout;	 And scrape it in all ways you can, until everything is scraped off;
et garde que li feus ne touche l’uef;	 and ensure that the fire does not touch the egg;
et saiches que ceste oevre est plus salve;	 And you must believe this work to be more healing;
et mues gardans de decorrement de sanc, et muedres que li ovraiges de taille;	 and with caution avoiding blood loss, and ensuring the actions of cutting are done correctly.
et se nulle chose te fait contraire, ou aposteme chaus ou decorremens de sanc ou autre chose, si cure ce qui te fait contraire, selonc ceu qui est devant dit.	 and if anything opposes you, or an abscess appears or blood loss occurs or something else happens, then treat what is against you according to what has been previously mentioned.

des hermofrodites	Hermaphrodites are individuals who possess both male and female reproductive organs or traits. This condition can be referred to as true hermaphroditism when an individual has ovarian and testicular tissues, which may be separate or combined in a gonad known as an ovotestis. False hermaphroditism occurs when there is the presence of only one type of reproductive organ along with secondary characteristics of the other sex.
Hermofrodie est selonc II manieres as homes:	 Hermaphroditism occurs in two ways among men:
l’une si est que entre les II coions apert ausi com li figure de la nature d’une femme, ou il ait poil, et aucunes fois en cort li urine.	 The one is such that between the two testes they look as if naturally of a woman's shape, and it may have hair, or occasionally urinates from there.
Et li autre maniere si est en femmes, et ait sus lou poignil ausi com une verge et II coions.	 And the other method is for women, with swelling as much like a rod and two knots.
Et li cure de l’ome et de la fame si est que tu copes les chars ajostees toutes, et les cure si com autres plaies;	 And the treatment of man and woman is such that you bandage all swollen joints, and treat them as other wounds.
en la seconde maniere, des homes dont li urine saut par lou cuir des coions, si n’a point de cure.	 In the second way, for men whose urine flows without control from their scrotum, there is no remedy.

des emorroides	Emotions often involve feelings of discomfort or distress related to situations affecting one's internal state and external conditions; in the case of hemorrhoids, it concerns painful swelling around the anus due to vein inflammation.
Emorroydes sont overtures de voines dont sans cort acostumeement, et quant les emorroydes sont vielles si devienent thelul;	 Effusions are veins that overflow without usual habituation, and when effusions are old they become tumorous.
et nos avons jai dit en la division les semblances d’aus, et les signes, et je dirai ci celles qui resoivent curation.	 And we have observed similarities to those mentioned before, and signs, and I will now say which ones receive treatment.
Je di que les emorroides et li thelul, quant il sont em parfont en la marris, et il n’aperent au sentir, si n’est mie li cure par fer.	 I say that morbus and hardening when fully in the arm, they do not appear to touch, except by curing with iron.
Cil qui sont a la bouche de la marris, c’on puet sentir, sont cil c’on puet curer.	 Those who are at the beginning of the arm, which can be felt, these can be treated.
Il covient donques que tu mettes la femme en une maison froide, puis estent l’altelul as tenailles, et le cope en ses racines, puis poudre sus medicines restraignans sanc, si com acaice et sanc de dragon et encens, et semblans choses;	 Therefore, you must place the woman in a cold house, then stretch the bone with tongs, and wrap it at its roots, then apply powders of restraining medicines such as those made from hawthorn berries and dragon's blood resin and incense.
puis boute ses piez a la paroit une houre, puis la met en aigue froide;	 Then bind her feet to the wall for an hour, then place them in cold water.
et se decorremens de sanc i vient, si la fai seoir en une decoction de sumac et d’escorce de pomes grenates et de gales et de semblans choses, et puis pren farine d’orge, et la confis avec miel et aisil, et en fai I emplaustre sus son dos.	 And if bleeding persists, make her sit in a concoction of sumac and the bark of pomegranate trees and hawthorn berries and elderberries along with similar things, then take wheat flour, mix it with honey and onion juice, and place an embalming cloth over her back.
Et se il estainche, c’est boin.	 And if it becomes inflamed, that is good.
Se ceu non, se li fai aerdre ventouses au dos et as mameles sens ferir;	 If not, apply heated cups to the back and avoid touching the nipples.
puis pren lainne, et la moille en jus de plantain ou en jus d’aglentier avec vin viel, et fai aerdre au leu.	 Then take linen, and the hair in juice of plantain or elderberry with wine vinegar, and apply to the area.

des apostemes de la marris	Abscesses of the rectum
Maintes manieres d’aposteme vienent en la marris, si com chancre et aposteme pierous et herpes et estiomenes et fistules et emorroides et aposteme chaut, et plusors autres maladies que j’ai dit en la division. et se tu vues savoir l’ovraige de fer, si regarde se li apostemes est agus en l’encomencement de sa venue, et plain de chalor et de fievre, et s’il devient rouge se tu le pues veoir. et se li estrumens est plus grans, si covient covrir la parfondesce de la marris de drapelz, si que li estrumens ne li grieve;	 And if the fractures are larger, it is necessary to cover the depth of the fracture with cloths so that the fragments do not harm.

de l’enfantement	Of childbirth
