et s’il ne puet soder, si rencomence la rasure plus fort que devant, tant qu’il saine mout, et soit escorchiez;	 And if it cannot be made whole again, resume the removal more strongly than before until it is fully healed and scraped clean.
puis le cure tant qu’il soit sanez.	 Then treat until it is healed thoroughly.
dou fremit	By a sudden blow
Formice est une petite apparance fautree antor le cors, et va mout em parfont;	 A mouse is a small creature appearing on the body, moving much.
et aucune fois la trueve li frois, et le sent on ausi comme mort de fremit, et vient en tout le cors, et plus as mains que autre part.	 and it never brings coldness to the joints, feeling similar to death from fear, affecting all over the body, especially in the hands than elsewhere.
Et li cure si est que tu pren une cainne d’une penne d’oie, ou une penne de vultul fort, et met celle caine sus le fremit, tant que li cercles porpreigne le fremit tot entor;	 And the treatment is to take a feather from a goose pen or a strong vulture wing and place it on the shaking, until the purple circle completely envelops the trembling.
puis torne ta main a tout la cainne tant que tu copes tout entor le fremit, et le met em parfont, et esraiche le fremit de ses racines.	 then turn your hand around the feather until you cover all the shaking, moving it freely, and uproot the trembling from its roots.
Et se tu vues, si fai ceu d’une caine d’arain ou de fer selonc ceste forme, et soit subtilz desoz et traians desus:	And if you see it, make a splint from either wax or iron as shown here, and be subtle below and transparent above.
ne mie perciet, por mues tenir au doi, et mues presser.	 do not feel, to hold with both hands, and press together.
Et se tu vues, si cauterize lou fremit, si com il est devant ou chapistre de cautere.	 And if you see it, then cauterize the trembling, as it is in front or by fire cautery method.
de la forme dou clistere	by pa l’sul:d sir toug. Et so ou n'estra;
Aucune fois fait on clistere d’argent ou d’archaut, ou d’arain fondut ou mailliet;	 Never is one made a silver or lead clister, or of melted brass or pewter.
et aucune fois fait on de ces estrumens petis et grans, selonc ces a cui il sont amenistrez.	 And never are such small and large suppositories made, according to the one for whom they are prepared.
Cil donques c’on amenistre en la cure des enfans et qui sont foible et dolorous, sont petis.	Thus in the care of children who are weak and painful, they are small [suppositories].
Li forme dou clistere petit et grant si est desus large, ou li ventres est liiez selonc ceste maniere:	The form of enema small or large is as follows: the belly being tied in this manner.
et i ait une desevrance ou li ventres soit liiez, si com tu vois, et li chiez soit dedens perciez;	 and there is a distension or the belly is bound, as you see, and the head is pierced inside;
et ait a l’un des costez II pertus, et en l’autre I;	 and to one side it has a hole, and on the other it does.
et soit li ventres ou om met les medicines d’une vessie de beste ou de parchemin, et soit perciez tout entor de menus pertus, et ait entre chescun pertus I doit d’espaice, puis boute en ces pertus I fil fort de fil crut tort en X ou enqui entor, et assemble le ventre si com est une chievre;	 and the belly or his arm has medicines from a beast's bladder or parchment, and it is pierced all around small holes, and between each hole there should be space, then put in these holes a strong thread of twisted linen, X times on both sides, and gather the belly as if it were a goat.
et quant li medicine est dedens, si la lie a l’estrument devant d’un fil fort, puis clisterize;	 When the medication is inserted, tie it to the instrument with a strong thread, then enema.
et c’est li forme dou cercle:	 and here is the shape of the circle:
Et soit li medicine ne trop chaude ne trop froide, et oint le chief dou clistere d’oile ou d’aubun d’uef, ou de semblant chose, puis le boute ens legierement;	 And let the medication not be too hot or too cold, and apply the substance of the enema with oil or goat's butter or similar substance, then administer it gently.
puis l’espreigne li ministres a ses II mains ensamble, tant qu’il soit toz vuis, puis estrai lou clistere, et lieve li malaides ses jambes a la paroit, et se li medicine vuet issir, si la teigne tant com il puet;	 then the minister inserts it with both hands together until full, then withdraws the enema, and lifts the patient's legs to the bedside, allowing the medication to exit as much as possible.
et s’il dort une nuit atot, si est plus grans aide.	 and if he sleeps through the entire night, it provides greater relief.
Et se tu le clisterizes em maladie de decorrement de ventre, et li medicine se haste d’issir, si le rencomence tant qu’il soit sanez.	And if you administer an enema in the case of intestinal issues, and the patient's health improves, as long as it remains so.
Et se li emorroide sont ou fondement, ou aposteme, si soit li clistere ausi subtilz com por I enfant;	 And if the hemorrhoids are at their foundation or abscessed, make the enema as subtle as for a child.
et c’est li forme dou clistere subtil sus coi li cuir soit estraint:	 And this is the form of a subtle suppository through which the body is restrained.
des plaies	M, even you give them:
Nos avons jai dit en la division la cure des plaies;	 We have said in that section on wound care;
or vos dirons les cures de mains et de medicine, selonc l’acomplissement.	 Or we shall speak of hand treatments and medicines, according to their completion.
Je dis que les plaies sont diverses selonc ceu qu’elles sont faites, et selonc les leus ou les plaies sont faites, et de coi elles sont faites.	I say that wounds are diverse depending on how they are made, and according to the locations or the ways in which they are made, and why they are made.
Les choses par coi plaies sont faites sont par gitement de piere, et taille d’espee et de couteil, ou de lance ou de fust ou de siette, ou de semblans choses;	 The things by which wounds are made include the thrust of a spear, cutting with a sword and knife, or of a lance, club, arrow, or similar items.
ou que sont faites selonc les leus dou cors, si com plaie que chiet sus le col, ou sus le chief, ou le peis, ou le ventre, ou le foie, et semblans membres;	 Or those that are made depending on the wounds of the body, as a gash upon the neck, or head, or thighs, abdomen, liver, and similar limbs.
et je vos dirai la cure de chescune plaie, et encomencerai as plaies dou chief simples, car li remenbrance venra en son chapistre.	 And I will tell you the treatment for each wound, beginning with simple head wounds, because memory will come to mind in its chapter.
Je dis que quant simple plaie vient ou chief, et li os n’est brisiez, si pren garde se c’est de gitement de piere ou de semblans choses, et li cuir est toutevoie rompus et est li plaie grans, et tu doutes levement d’aposteme chaut:	 When a simple wound occurs or the bone is not broken, be cautious if it's from a stone fall or similar things, and the skin is always torn and the wound is large, so you suspect hot abscess.
si le fai tantost sainier de la cephalique meismement s’il vient poc de sanc de la plaie, et soit li sainie au contraire de la partie navree;	 If a coldness quickly appears on the head if there is little blood from the wound, and it is opposite to the affected part.
et eschuisse li malaides repletion de vin et de viandes grosses.	 And remove the patient's excess fluids with wine and large meats.
Et s’il ne vuet sainier, si soit amenuisie sa viande, et ne boive point de vin, ne ne menjuce point de char;	 And if it does not cool down, reduce his meat intake, and do not drink wine or eat fatty foods.
et met sor la plaie, se apostemes chaus i vient, coton moilliet en oile roset soulement, ou en vin stiptice;	 And apply soothing herbs to the wound if abscess occurs there, use a soft-cotton oil or astringent wine.
et s’il n’i a aposteme chaut, si met sus la plaie, s’elle est fresche a tout son sanc, et elle n’est muee par l’air, poudre, que je dirai un poc ci aprés;	 If there is no abscess present, place it on the fresh wound where all its blood remains, and it has not moved from air or powder, which I will say something more about shortly.
et se li ars l’ait muee, si met sus aucuns oignemens, tant qu’il soit sanez.	 If the wound has moved due to motion, apply some ointment until it is healed.
Et se li plaie est grans si com de tailleure d’espee et de semblans, et les levres ne se pueent assembler par tentes, si les assemble par cousture, si com je dirai as plaies dou ventre, de la costure.	And if the wound is large like a sword cut and similar to it, and the lips cannot be joined by stitches, join them with sutures as I will describe for abdominal wounds in stitching.
Se li plaie est descoverte de l’os, et pent, et ne tient mais que a un poc, si le cope;	 If the wound exposes bone, and persists, clings only slightly with flesh, you must cover it.
puis cure la plaie de medicine, et restoure char dure en leu de cuir, et comande au malaide a mengier grosses viandes, si com testes et froment cuit, ausi com poulz, et semblans choses.	 Then treat the wound with medicine and restore its firmness by applying tanned leather, instructing the patient to eat hearty meats as you have tested wheat and cooked barley, likewise fish and similar things.
Et se tu trueves ou cuir porriture, et il n’aert a l’os, si cope lou porrit tot, et giete fuer, puis le cure;	 And if you find or feel softening of the flesh, not reaching to the bone, cover it completely with fat and then treat it.
et se il ait artere en la plaie ou voine, dont sans cort, et il ne puet estainchier par medicines, si quier l’artere, et se tu la trueves desloie, si la lie d’un fil;	 And if there is an artery in the wound or vein, without bark, and it cannot be stopped by medicines, you may tie off the artery, and if you find it dislocated, bind it with a thread.
et se ceu ne profite mie, si la cauterize.	 And if this does not help at all, then cauterize it.
Et se ces plaies sont petites et simples, si est li cure legiere:	 And if these wounds are small and simple, there is a light treatment:
et est que tu mettes ens ceste poudre qui soude ainsois que li ars l’ait muee.	 And you should apply this powder which sticks as the arrow moves it.
Et li maniere de la poudre si est:	 The manner of using the powder is as follows:
pren encens une partie;	 Take incense one part;
sanc de dragon II parties;	 Blood of a dragon, two parts;
chalz vive III parties, et le poudre subtilment, et emple la plaie, et l’estraint forment, tant qu’elle s’aerse bien et se joigne a tout son sanc;	 Wax alive three parts, and the powder delicately sprinkled, apply to the wound, and gently bind it, until it dries well and rejoins all its blood.
et puis la lie bien, et la laisse sens desliier, s’elle n’enfle;	 And then securely bandage it, allowing for some loosening unless it swells;
car on n’oste la madicine tant qu’ele soit sanee.	 Because the medicine is not removed until it is healed.
Et aucune fois fait on ceu de chalz soulement, quant on n’ait l’encens ne lou sanc de dragon, mais que li ars n’ait muee la plaie.	And this should not be done by fire alone unless you have the incense or blood of a dragon; but that the art must heal the wound.
Et se li ars ait mueit la plaie, meismement en esteit, si n’i met om mie ceste poudre;	 And if the wound has moved or shifted in its place, particularly during sleep, do not reapply this powder.
mais met sus aucuns oignemens digestis, ou poulz de farine d’orge faites d’aigue et de miel, tant qu’ele giete bowe;	 But apply some digested ointments or ground barley flour made of water and honey, until it heals.
puis le cure d’autres cures tant qu’il soit sanez.	 Then use other remedies until it is fully healed.
Et se li brisure d’os vient avec la plaie, et elle est petite, si l’estrai as pinceures subtilz;	 And if there is a small bone fracture with the wound, extract it using fine tweezers;
et je vos dirai ci aprés les brisures dou chief.	 and I will tell you about this regarding head fractures afterwards.
de la plaie dou col	From a wound of the neck
Se plaie vient ou col et elle est simple, si n’a point de difference entre li et celi dou chief, mais se li ners dou col ou li artere est copee.	If the wound comes from the neck and is simple, without a difference between it and that of the head, but if the veins or the artery are severed in the neck.
Se c’est li ners, si n’i a autre engien que laissier la cure, et n’i mettre nulle chose restraignant, car il nuit as ners et les fait retraire;	 If it's the veins, there is no other option but to let them clot, and do not apply anything constricting, for it harms the veins and causes them to recede.
et ne mettre sus la plaie rien froit, car li substance des ners est froide, et li continuation d’aus si est avec le cerveil, qui est li plus haus membres;	 and do not apply anything cold to the wound, because the nature of the veins is cold, and their continuation lies with the brain, which are the highest members.
mais soit li medicine souez, si com chalz lavee en aigue douce, et mellee avec oile roset, et cucie lavee ausi en aigue douce, et autres pieres de mine selonc ceste maniere, et oignemens moistes.	 but use the medicine applied with warm water softened by salt, and mixed with rose oil, and boil it in water softened similarly, and other remed cupping according to this manner, and moist salves.
Et se li plaie est grans, si la cout et lie de bendes, puis la cure tant qu’il soit sanez.	And if the wound is large, then stitch it and bind with bandages, then care for it until it is healed.
Et se les plaies sont parfondes et ele est chevee et pleinne de bowe, si la perce ou plus bas leu;	 If wounds are deep and swollen with pus, puncture or drain below them.
et se li artere est copee, et decorremens de sanc en vient, si la desoivre, et la loie, et la cauterize se mestier est;	 If the arrow is embedded and blood flows inwardly, open it, extract it, and if necessary, cauterize.
et se li espinee de la gorge est copee, ou li keurs, et li conduiz est gardez, par coi la viande va, si cout le keur sus la cainne de la gorge, et ne touchier la gorge mais la remet selonc sa figure naturel;	 If the spine of the throat is embedded or the kidney, and urination is obstructed, causing tissue to protrude, if possible cut near the base of the throat, but do not touch the throat itself, replace it according to its natural shape.
et puis l’estraint avenanment, et le laisse aucuns jors, puis le cure d’oignemens desechans tant qu’il soit sanez;	 And then bind securely, leave untouched for some time, and treat with washed ointments until it heals.
et se li plaie a fait empression en l’os, si la quier;	 If the wound is pressing on bone, you must address it.
et s’il i a pieces d’os, si les trai fuers toz se tu pues, et ces que tu ne pues avoir, si laisse tant que li plaie porrisse, et soit desevree et aligie li issue;	 And if there are bone fragments, pull out all you can, and those that you cannot retrieve, leave them so the wound may heal over, and then cleanse and align the edges.
et se li plaie est fresche, si poudre sus la poudre que j’ai dit.	 And if the wound is fresh, apply powder as I have instructed.
Et s’il a en la plaie os et il i a fistule, si la cure ensi com j’ai dit en son chapistre.	If there are bones within the wound and it has a fistula, then treat it as I have described in its chapter.
de la plaie de lance ou de coutel	From the wound caused by a spear or knife
Se c’est cop de lance ou de coutel, et li plaie est parfonde, si regarde se de la plaie saut ventositez cant li malaides alainne:	 If it's a puncture from a spear or knife, and the wound is deep, observe if there are signs of venom which may afflict the patient:
saiches adonques que li plaie est mortelz;	 Recognize then that the wound is fatal:
et s’elle n’est parfonde, et elle est fresche a tout son sanc, si n’i mettre mie a la premiere houre la poudre, ne ne la liier mie por le sanc que ne demorse em parfont, et reviegne au cuer, et ocie lou malaide;	 And if it is not deep, and the wound is fresh with all its blood, do not apply the powder at once, nor use it to stop bleeding from within, as this could harm the patient:
mais i met oignement atractif, et le lie II fois le jor;	 But apply an attracting balm, and bind it for two days.
et se tu n’as oignement, si met en la plaie viel coton por succier fuers la moistor, et fai dormir le malaide sus la plaie III jors, ou IIII, ou plusors;	 And if you do not have a balm, place woolen cotton in the old wound to absorb moisture, and make the patient sleep with the injury exposed for three days or more.
si n’i venra mie spasme, ne tremor male de cuer n’estraingnemens d’alainne;	 If this does not cause muscle spasm or severe body shaking;
et quant tu vois les bones dispositions, si saiches que li plaie est sauve.	 And when you see the bone properly aligned, know that the wound is healed.
Cure la donques de tentes et d’autres cures, tant qu’il soit sanez;	 Treat with tent and other remedies until it is healthy again;
et s’elle ne puet saner, et oevre, adés saiches que il i a fistule;	 And if it cannot heal or function properly, then understand that there is an abscess.
si la cure si com on doit.	 If the treatment is as described.
Et se li plaie est d’incision d’espee ou de coutel, et elle est simple, ou pis ou au dos, si la cure de ceu qui est devant;	 And if the wound is from a sword or knife cut, whether it's on top or bottom, treat as described for such injuries.
s’elle est grans, de cousture;	 If it is large, with stitches;
et s’elle est petite, de poudre, et s’elle est empressee en l’os, et en a copeit pieces, si quier la plaie, et les trai fuers s’il sont desevrez;	 If it is small, with powder, and if it is embedded in the bone, and there are broken pieces, then you must address the wound and pull out any splinters if needed.
et s’il ne sont desevrez, si laisse porrir la plaie, si aligera li estractions;	 And if they are not embedded, let the wound heal naturally, and lighten the extractions;
et des autres plaies as autres membres est li jugemens si com nos avons dit.	 And for other wounds on other limbs, apply our judgement as we have said.
dou derrompement dou ventre	And rupture of the abdomen
Li derompemens dou ventre est grans et moiens et petis;	 The protrusions of the abdomen are large and medium and small;
de la grant plaie saut aucune fois li intestine, ou li ners des intestines, par coi li intromission d’aus;	 From a large wound, never does it occur that the intestines or their nerves are affected, resulting in contamination from outside;
et li costure est plus malaisie, et aucune fois vaut pis li petite plaie que li grans, por ceu c’on remet plus a poinnes les intestines en, s’on ne les i remet de chaut en chaut;	 And the stitching is easier to manage, and never is the small wound worse than the large one because it allows for more frequent handling of the intestines when not reset piece by piece;
por ce que li intestine enflent tantost qu’il sentent le froit, si rentrent plus a poinnes, et por ceu vaut mues li moieinne plaie, por ceu c’on ramoine mues l’intestine a son leu que as autres II.	 Because the intestines swell so soon when they feel cold, thus become more painful, and therefore move the wound inward, since it is necessary to reset the intestines to their place among the others.
Et saiches que li routure dou ventre est selonc IIII manieres:	 And know that there are four ways of treating abdominal issues.
les II costures communes avienent en la costure dou ventre, et li costure des autres plaies dou cors et II autres costures propres sont communes as autres plaies;	 The two common sutures occur in the stomach's incision, and the sutures for other body wounds and two other specific types are common to other injuries.
et toutevoie elles sont plus propres avec la costure dou ventre, et je dirai une chescune et declairerai.	 Also, they are more suitable with the stomach's sutures, and I will describe each one and declare them.
Je di que quant li plaie est petite, et aucune chose de l’intestine ist fuer, et griés chose est dou remettre, ceu est par l’une des II manieres:	 I say that when the wound is small and nothing from the intestines protrudes, this is by one of the four ways mentioned.
ou por la petitece de la plaie, si com nos avons dit, ou por ce que li intestine est enflez por le froit.	 Or for the smallness of the wound, as we have said, or because the intestines are swoln by cold.
Et quant il est frois, eschaufez lou en teil maniere:	 And when it is cooled, warm it in a certain manner:
moillie une esponge ou I mol drapeil en aigue tede soulement, ou tu cuis en aigue squinant et cipre et spique, et arose l’intestine tant que li enfleure soit ostee;	 Dabble an apron or cloth in hot water only, and boil it with salt and pepper, and heat the intestines until inflammation is gone.
et aucune fois fait ce vins restraingnans, et est muedre que awe soule por desenfler.	 And never do this that constricts blood flow, and ensure it is loosened to deflate.
Et quant tu vois l’enfleure departir, si amoiste l’intestine d’aigue ou altee et malves soient cuites, car par ceu est aligie li entree a poc de chose;	 And when you see inflammation subsiding, moisten the intestines with water or wine, but cook them sparingly as their passage is facilitated by little food.
et s’il n’i puet entrer, si fent un poc la plaie a l’estrument de coi on cope les emorroydes;	 If it cannot enter, make a small incision with the instrument used to treat bunions.
et li premiere cure est muedre que li taille, que nus n’i doit taillier sens grant necessiteit n’i ait;	 And the first remedy is to move it that no one should cut without great necessity or need.
et c’est li estrumens por le fendre:	 And this is for splitting:
si trenche dedens en la corbeure et defuer non, et vez ci la forme:	 If a split occurs in the arch and does not heal properly, then apply this method:
Et quant li plaie est enlargie, et li intestine saut fuer, si le remet arer selonc la forme naturel en son leu propre, se tu en as pooir, car ce vaut mues.	 When the wound is large and the intestines protrude, if you can reset it to its natural place in its proper location, because movement aids healing.
Quant li plaie est large, et elle est en la partie desoz lou ventre, si covient que tu faices gesir lou malaide sus son dos, et met ses jambes plus haut que son chief;	 When the wound is wide and located below the belly, it is appropriate to place the patient on their back with legs raised higher than their head.
et s’elle est en la partie desoz le ventre, si met le chief et le pis plus haut que les parties desoz, et ausi se li routure dou ventre est en l’une des II parties si met t’entente en ceu que li partie navree soit plus haute que li autre;	 And if it is located below the belly but above the legs, raise the head and groin higher than the lower parts. If the wound in the abdominal area is on one side, balance them so that the affected part is higher than the other.
et ensi covient amenistrer ceu que je dis en plaies grans et moienes.	 Thus, one must treat as I have instructed on large wounds and small ones.
Es plaies petites met ceu que t’est apparilliet, puis aies entre tes mains I ministre pitous ki teigne toute la routure a sa main, et assemble les levres;	 For small wounds do this as you have learned, then take the pus in your hand and place it between your fingers to mix thoroughly, and bring together the edges.
et c’est la maniere commune de costures, et est que tu preignes une aguille ou plusors, selonc la quantiteit de la largesce de la plaie, puis laisse des le chief de la plaie I doi d’espaice, et i fiche une aguille ou il ait I boin fil fort;	 And this is the common way for sutures, and you should take a needle or several according to the quantity of the width of the wound, then leave space at the top edge of the wound, and insert a needle with strong thread.
et perce les II chiés dou cuir avec les II chiés dou siphac, qui est desoz le cuir dedens, tant que tu la faices percier de celle partie, et assemble les II chief dou siphac les IIII ensamble;	 And pierce the two sides with the two sides of sinew, which is underne.the skin close to the deep layer until you have separated that part, and bring together the top edges of both sinews as one.
puis l’estrain d’un fil double entor l’aguille de II pars, puis assemble les II chiés de la plaie avenanment, et puis laisse I doi d’espaice, et i fiche une autre aguille;	 Then strain a double thread around the arrowhead on both sides, then immediately reassemble the two heads of the wound, and leave some space, and insert another arrow.
puis la lie dou fil si com tu as fait la premiere aguille, et ne cesser de ceu faire selonc ceu que tu as mestier des aguilles, tant que toute li plaie soit restrainte;	 Then tie the thread again as you did with the first arrow, and continue doing so according to how many more arrows are needed until all wounds are secured.
et soient les aguilles moienes, entre subtilz et grosses, car les aguilles subtilz copent toute la char, et les trop grosses si ne pueent mie bien entrer:	 and let the arrows be medium-sized, between fine and large, because fine arrows can securely hold together, and overly large ones may not enter properly.
por ceu covient qu’elles soient moienes;	 therefore it is necessary that they are medium-sized.
et ne covient mie bouter les aguilles trop au defuer de la char et dou cuir, k’elles ne copent et oevrent la plaie devant la soudure;	 and do not place the arrows too far from the wound or the skin, so they can properly secure and function at the site of stitching.
et puis cope les chiés des aguilles, qu’elles ne blecent lou malaide au dormir, et i met tentes ou drapelz au chiés des aguilles por mues tenir, et les laisse tant que li plaie soit soudee;	 Then wrap the head of the arrows so they do not bend and cause pain to the patient while sleeping, and place pads or cloths on the arrowheads for movement, allowing them to remain until the wound is healed.
et ceste maniere de costure as aguilles est plus covenauble en petites plaies, car il i soffist une aguille ou II.	 And this manner of suturing arrows is more convenient in small wounds, for there may be a single arrow or two used.
Li seconde costure si est commune, et est que tu assemble les II chiés dou cuir et les II chiés dou syfac ensamble a une aguille ou il ait I fort fil moien;	 The second method of suturing is common and involves joining the two heads of the bone with one arrowhead at a time, using an iron wire.
et quant tu avras perciez ces chiez toz IIII ensamble, si ramoinne l’aguille a la partie ou tu as encomenciet, en la maniere c’on cout les dras;	 And once you have pierced all four heads together, reset the arrow at the part where you began, similar to how one fastens cloths.
et met d’espaice entre chescune costure la grossece d’un menor doi;	 And place space between each stitch, the size of a small finger.
ceste costure sevent li home, et je cousi une plaie c’uns hons avoit ou ventre, qui estoit navrez d’un coutel, et estoit li plaie plus d’une palme de grant, et issoit des intestines bien II palmes de grant, et estoit li plaie enmi le ventre.	 These stitches close the wound, and I sewed a wound that a man had on his belly, which was troubled by a knife, and the wound was wider than one palm wide, and it involved intestines more than two palms wide, and the wound was in the abdomen.
Je li ramenai l’intestine puis k’il ot esteit XXIIII houres fuer, et fut li plaie soudee jusc’a XV jors, et le curai, et fut sanez.	 I brought back the intestines as it had been XXIV hours since, and healed the wound until day fifteen, and treated him, and he was well again.
Et li mire l’avoient jugiet qu’il morroit, et ce fut miracle;	 And the physician judged that he would die, but it was a miracle.
et ne le curai mie d’oignement, car je estoie en I leu ou on n’en trovoit point, ne nule medicines;	 and did not treat him with ointment because I was in the place where there were none to be found, nor any medicine.
et metoie sens plus sus la plaie coton viel II fois le jor, et le lavoie d’aigue de miel tant qu’il fut sanez.	 and applied clean cloth over it twice a day, and washed the wound with honey water until it healed.
Or vos dirai les II propres manieres de cousture:	 Now I will tell you two proper ways of dressing:
pren l’aguille, et la boute des la partie defuers jusc’a celi dedens;	 Take the needle and thread up to that part inside.
quant elle a perciet le keur de droit en droit, si lai le chief dou siphac ou cousteit ou tu as bouteit l’aguille, et la fai percier d’autre part des la partie dedens jusc’a celi defuer;	 When it has pierced the core straight on, then insert the needle head or thread through where you have passed the needle, and make another cut inside to that far-off part.
et li entendemens de ceste costure si est que tu cous ausi com li peletier font les pelz, et que tu laisses une fois le syfac d’une part, et le reprent d’autre, tant que li costure soit toute acomplie.	 And the understanding of this stitching is that you sew as the furrier does with furs, and leave once the skin from one side, and then return to the other, until the dressing is completely finished.
Li seconde maniere de costure, que Galiens dist proprement, si est si com aucun font, qui assemblent les II parties ensamble naturelment, et apploient l’un des chief dou syfac a l’autre chief, en teil maniere:	 The second way of stitching, which Galien properly calls it, is as any join together naturally, and apply one head of the skin to the other head, in such a manner:
fiche une aguille ou chief dou mirach prochiene, et fai percier celui leu soulement, et laisse les II chiés dou syfac;	 Insert a needle or pin near the next vein, and make an incision at that location only, leaving the two heads of the suture.
puis torne l’aguille, et la fai percier des la partie defuers jusc’a celi dedens, as II chiés dou syfac;	 Then turn the needle, and pierce it through to that depth with both ends of the suture.
puis fai percier l’un et l’autre des la partie defuers jusc’a celi dedens, en II autres chiés dou mirach que sont on l’autre costeit;	 Then pierce each one through to that depth with two other veins near it.
et c’est li muedre maniere de costure et li plus commune.	 And this is the proper manner of suturing, and the most common method.
Galiens si dist ceste parolle, et aucun le tesmoignent, c’on doit coudre le ventre a II aguilles, ou il ait fil en chescune;	 Galen said this word, but no one can attest to it, that you must sew the belly with two needles, having thread in each.
et doit on bouter l’une aguille d’une part, et l’autre d’autre, en la maniere de ces qui cousent corroies;	 And one needle should be inserted from one side and the other from the opposite, as those who sew belts.
et saiches que quant li routure est enmi lou ventre, si est li cousture plus griez que des autres leus dou ventre.	 And say that when the rupture is within the belly, then the suture is more difficult than with other parts of the belly.
Li jugemens de la plaie si est telz com li jugemens des autres plaies:	 The judgments of the wound are such as the judgments of other wounds.
et est que quant tu trueves la plaie fresche a tout son sanc, ainsois que li ars l’ait muee, si remet arer l’intestine, et lou cout;	 and it is such that when you find the fresh wound with all its blood, as also the arrow has moved it, reset the intestines and the spleen.
puis met sus la poudre enjanrant char, et se li ars l’ait muee, si met sus aucun oignement que soit present, tant que li plaie bowe;	 then apply powdered antidote with charcoal, and if the arrow has moved it, put on any salve that is available, until the wound heals.
et chicent li fil, et soient soudez li sifac, et li mirach;	 and cleanse the thread, secure the knot, and the needle.
puis cure la plaie si com les autres, tant qu’il soit sanez;	 Then treat the wound as you would others, until it is healthy again.
et se tu n’as medicines, si met sus, tantost qu’ele comance a giter bowe, coton viel, et le remue II fois le jor tant k’il soit sanez.	 And if you have no medicine, apply it directly, as soon as it begins to swell slightly, using wool or old cloth and move it twice a day until it is healthy again.
Car tu n’as mestier d’autre medicine en plusors dispositions cant les plaies sont simples;	 For in most cases you do not need any other medicines for simple wounds;
et se tu doutes que li plaie ne faice communiteit as membres principelz, si covient ke tu moilles lainne legiere en oile de tempree chalor, ou en oile roset, et la met entor les angres, et desoz les asselles;	 and if you suspect that the wound is infecting the main limbs, it is necessary to grind linen with heated oil or rose oil, and place it around the joints and under the elbps.
et s’il sent dolor ou porriture en bouelz, et maintes fois avient, si les clisterize de vin noir tede, et meismement se li porriture vient jusc’a l’intestine;	 and if it causes pain or swelling in large amounts, and often occurs, then apply black wine enemas, especially if the swelling reaches the intestines.
et le perce dedens, et saiches que quant c’est li gros intestines, si est plus legier a saner que li petis.	 And it penetrates within, instructing that when it is the large intestines, then it is easier to heal than the small ones.
Li intestine qui est apelez «jeun» ne puet saner quant il est navrez, et c’est por la planteit des voinnes que i sont, et por la subtiliteit de tout le cors, et l’aprochement de sa nature des ners.	 The intestines called "jeun" cannot heal when they are in distress due to the size of the veins and their presence throughout the entire body, as well as the subtlety of all the organs and the proximity of its connection with the nerves.
Et si li zirbe saut de la plaie, si le remet arrier ausi com l’intestine, tandis qu’il est fres;	 And if the spleen protrudes from the wound, reset it as before like the intestines while fresh.
et s’il est vielz et devenus vers ou noir, si covient que tu lies le leu qui est noir, que decorremens de sanc n’i viegne, car il i a voinnes et arteres;	 and if it is old and has become black or blue, you must remove the dead tissue where bleeding vessels may arise.
puis cope ceu qui est entre le liien, et met les II chiés pendans des la partie desoz la plaie jusque defuer por aligier l’estraction quant li zirbes chiet, et li plaie bowe.	 then cut out what is between the ligaments and place two fingers hanging from below the wound edge to facilitate arrow extraction, and the wound bowing.
de la routure dou boueil	From the treatment of the eyelid
Quant li intestine est rons, et li plaie est petite, si la puet on restorer en aucuns homes, por ceu que je vis que uns hons fut navrez ou ventre d’une lance;	 When the intestine is torn and the wound is small, it can be restored in some cases because I have seen a man wounded by a lances' belly.
et estoit li plaie au destre de l’estomac, et fut envillie et devint fistule, et en issoit li egestion et li ventositez;	 And it was the wound on the right side of the abdomen, and became infected and turned into a fistula, and from which there were excretions and flatulence.
je i mis cure selonc ceu que je poi, et ne cessai de subtilier tant qu’il fut sanez, et li leus soudez.	 I provided treatment according to what seemed best, and did not stop probing until it was healed, resulting in suppuration of the pus.
Et quant je le vis souder, je doutai que li malaides n’eust mal en son ventre;	 And when I saw that it had stopped seeping, I doubted whether the patient did not have a problem in his stomach;
et il n’i ot point de mal, mais demora en millors dispositions, et menjans et bevans;	 and there was no illness present, but he remained in better conditions, eating and drinking.
et dirent aucun experimentors que quant il a petite plaie en l’intestine, qu’il doit estre liiez en teil maniere:	 and several experienced physicians stated that when there is a small wound within the intestines, it must be tied in a certain way:
pren fremis a grans testes, puis assemble les levres de la plaie, et quant li fremis ait overte la bouche, si la met sus les II levres, si qu’elle estraigne sa bouche sus;	 take fine thread and gather the edges of the wound, then when it opens up like a mouth, place it between the two lips and stretch its mouth out.
et puis li cope la teste, et ce se tient si qu’il ne puet desliier, puis met I autre fremit aprés en celle maniere que devant, tant que li plaie soit toute porprise;	 And then wrap the head, and hold it so that it cannot dislocate again, then apply another force afterwards in the same manner as before, until the wound is fully healed.
et cout la plaie.	 and cover the wound.
Cil chief si s’aerdent en l’intestine, et ne vient nulle nuisance au malaide, et se puet on liier l’intestine d’un fil subtil qui est copez de l’intestine d’une beste, en teil maniere:	 If the head enters the intestines and causes no harm to the patient, one can tie the intestines with a fine thread cut from an animal's intestine in such a manner:
pren le chief de cest fil d’intestine que soit mout descharnez, et puis lie au chief de cest fil I fil de lin subtil tort, puis boute le fil en l’aguille, et en cout l’intestine, et le ramoinne en la routure;	 Take the head of this intestinal thread that is mostly cleaned and then tie it with a fine flax thread twisted, sew the intestine with the needle, and stitch up the wound.
et ceste maniere de costure de fremis nen est fuers que selonc la voie de fiance et d’esperance;	 And this method of suturing is only effective if done in accordance with trust and hope;
et se li plaie est grans et large, meismement quant elle est en l’un des grailes intestines, si n’i a engien ne santeit, fuer que subtiliteit.	 And if the wound is large and wide, especially when it is in one of the internal organs, there is no remedy or health, only subtlety required.
de fistule ou qu’ele soit	Regarding a fistula, or wherever it may be
Saiches que toute plaie ou aposteme, quant il enveillist, si est apelee universement «fistule», et meismement quant elle est chevee et rent bowe.	 Every wound or abscess, when it becomes ulcerated, is universally called "fistula", especially when it grows and becomes bowed back.
Et fistule est selonc la verteit nodation fautree dure et blainche, ou on ne sent dolor, et est ausi chevee com li penne d’un oiseil;	 And a fistula is the result of improper tissue hardening and bruising, where there is no pain felt, and it appears as swollen as the feather of a bird.
et aucune fois en saut clere bowe, et autre fois espesse;	 and at times clear like glass, and other times thickened;
aucune fois poc, et autre fois assez;	 At no time too much, and at other times enough;
et je en ai jai parleit en la division des plaies, que toute plaie que n’est sanee, et il n’i a char, ce n’est fuers que par une des VIIII causes:	 And I have spoken in the section on wounds, that any untreated wound is not closed, for it is through only one of the nine causes.
c’est a savoir, par la petitece dou sanc ou cors;	 It means, by the smallness of blood or body parts;
ou por sa malice;	 Or due to its evil nature;
ou por ceu qu’il i a char dure dedens, et sus les levres, que n’i laisse naistre char;	 Or because there is internal hardness and above the lips, where no blood should flow.
ou il i a trop de bowe;	 Or because there is too much flesh;
ou li leus est porris, et li matiere est de male qualiteit;	 Or the wound heals poorly, and the material is of bad quality;
ou li medicine n’est mie bone en la cure;	 Or the medicine used for treatment is not good.
ou por ceu que li corruption est maniere de pestilence;	 Or because it is a form of plague infection.
ou por la proprieteit en la region est tardive li digestion, et tarde li santeit, et enflee par nature;	 Or due to the property of the area being slow at digestion and health restoration, fleeing by nature.
ou il i a voinnes ou os:	 When there are veins or bones.
et j’ai ja mostreit toutes ces causes, et les signes, et les cures de medicines en la division.	 And I have already shown all these causes, signs, and treatments with herbs in the section.
Or covient que je te faice a savoir la cure de fistule qui est faite par oevre de mains.	Now it is necessary for me to inform you about the treatment of a fistula made by handiwork.
Saiches que fistule avient en tous membres dou cors;	 Seams that a fistula occurs in all members of the body;
car il i a fistules que vienent as grans voines, et as arteres, et as ners, ou au syfac, ou a l’intestine, ou a la vessie, ou a aucunes des costes, ou a l’espinee dou dos, ou a aucune jointe des mains ou des piez;	 Because there are fistulas that come from large veins and arteries, nerves, or the liver, intestines, bladder, some ribs, the spinal column of the back, or any joint in hands or feet.
et si a teil que vient a la proprieteit dou membre principeil, et as semblans leus.	 and if there is one that comes to the principal part of the limb and others.
Et toutes les fistules que sont de ceste maniere sont de grief sanation, et n’i a fors que labour, et ignorance;	 And all such fistulas are difficult to heal, with only hard work and ignorance being involved.
et se il i a aucune fistule que ne veigne mie jusc’a leu que j’ai dit, et tu as fiance de la cure, et tu la vues conoistre, si pren une tente d’arain ou de fer, se li fistule est droite, si la quier;	 And if there is any fistula that does not reach to the place I have said, and you trust in its healing, and observe it becoming known, then take a tent of wool or iron, if the fistula is straight, use it.
et se li fistule est torte, si la cerche d’une subtil tente de plonc, car li plons se ploie mues entor la tortuositeit;	 And if the fistula is twisted, search for a delicate tent of linen, because the linens bend easily around the twisting.
et se li fistule a mains pertus et tu ne la pues mie bien cerchier par tentes, si la clisterize par l’un des pertus, car la moistors si cort d’un pertus a autre, et la mundifie;	 And if the fistula has many openings and you cannot well search it with tents, clysterize it through one of the openings, because moisture quickly moves from one opening to another, and cleanses it.
puis la quier saigement a ton pooir, que tu conoisses s’il i a os ou nerf, et est chevee em parfont, et demande bien au malaide de la dolor qu’il sent au presser de ta main, et le leu ou il la sent;	 Then choose it carefully with your strength so that you know if there are bones or nerves present and they are inflamed at the front, and ask the patient well about the pain he feels when pressed by your hand and where it is located.
et quant tu savras vraiement le leu ou elle est, et s’elle est loing de jointure, ou de nerf, ou d’artere ou de voine, ou en aucuns des leus que je t’ai dit, si la cope selonc ceu que je t’ai dit, et oste fuer la fautreure et les chars corrumpues que sont dedens;	 And when you know truly the place where it is, and if it is far from a joint or nerve, or an artery or vein, or in any of the cases I have told you, then follow the procedure as I have instructed, and remove the other part and the corrupted bones within;
et puis la cure tant qu’elle soit sanee, et se li fistule est bien parfonde de droit endroit, si covient que tu copes em parfont, tant com tu pues, puis i met tentes moillies en medicine ague, et les boute jusc’au chief de la fistule, tant que li medicine corrode la superfluiteit qui est demoree au fons;	 and then treat it until it is cleaned, and if the fistula is well placed in the right location, if you should cut into it fully as you can see, then afterward apply bandages soaked in medicinal water, and let them reach up to the top of the fistula, until the medicine corrodes the excess that remains at the bottom;
et puis i met oignemens enjanrans sainne char, tant qu’il soit sanez;	 and then apply compresses with medicinal salve, until it is healed;
et s’il n’est sanez par ceu, si le cauterize si com nos avons dit, et se li os est corrompus de la fistule, si le cope.	 If it cannot be reduced by this method, then cauterize as we have said, and if the bone is corrupted by the fistula, treat with a poultice.
Se voinne ou ners ne te greve ou membres principelz, si com nos avons dit;	 If neither veins nor principal limbs are afflicted as we have said;
et se li os est descovers, et il i a corruption et noiror, si lou reis tant que li corruption soit toute ostee, puis le cure de choses enjanrans char tant qu’il soit sanez;	 And if the bone is exposed and there is corruption and darkness, reign it until the entire corruption of bone is healed, then treat with various remedies until it is clean.
et s’il n’est sanez, et rent bowe si com devant, saiches que tu n’es mie alez jusc’a font:	 If it remains unclean, reopen as before, be sure not to go past the extent of:
si descuevre et quier tant que tu soies au fons, et oste toute la corruption, puis restore le leu;	 And open and scrape until you reach the bottom, then remove all corruption, and return it to its place.
et s’il est ensi sanez, c’est bien.	 And if he is thus whole, that is well.
Se ceu non, saiches que la corruption est trop en parfont, que tu n’i pues avenir;	 If not, know that the putrefaction is too advanced, you cannot go near it;
si n’i a autre engien que dou lassier a nature;	 if there is no other remedy than the poultice of nature.
et s’il i a i petit os corrumput, et tu le pues traire as tenailles, si l’estrai a I estrument covenauble a ceu, et s’il i a maint os, si les trai trestoz, ne n’en laissier nes un;	 and if there is a small piece of corrupted bone that you can extract with tongs, use the appropriate instrument for this, and if there are many bones, extract all of them without leaving any.
et se li moistor te fait contraire, et il n’i a error ne paour, si cope et moistor et char, et delivre les os.	 and if the moisture causes difficulty, with no mistake or fear, cover it, dry it, and remove the bones.
Et se tu ne les pues oster a une houre, si met sus la plaie chose enjanrant porriture, et laisse tant que li leus soit porris entor les os, et adonc si avront plus legierement les os;	 And if you cannot remove them at once, apply something to the wound that prevents putrefaction, and let it be in place until the flesh grows around the bones, and then they will more easily extract the bones.
et se c’est uns grans os, si com de jambe ou de cuisse, si reis tant soulement la corruption tant que li noiror soit toute ostee, puis restoure la plaie;	 If it is a large bone, such as of the leg or thigh, return so much that the darkening has become all bone, then restore the wound.
et s’il en i a grant partie dou corrumput, et vient jusc’a mole de l’os;	 If there is significant portion of it rotten, and it reaches near to molten bone;
si le covient soier et coper tout jusc’a la corruption, et puis le cure tant qu’il soit soudez;	 if the matter must be scraped away and covered up to the rotting, then heal it until it is sealed.
et je te dirai d’une fistule qui avint I home en sa jambe, si que tu i preignes exemple et aide en ton ovraige.	 And I will tell you of an abscess that occurred in the man's leg; take it as an example and guidance for your work.
Il fut I jovencelz entor XXX ans, qui ot une dolor en sa jambe d’une cause que vint dedens le cors, tant que les matieres vinrent a la jambe, et fut enflee d’un gros aposteme, et n’ot point de cause defuer por ovrir;	 He was a young boy of under thirty years, who had pain in his leg from a cause that came from within the body until materials reached the leg, and it developed into a large abscess, and there was no reason to open.
mais li mire par lor folie ovrerent tant sus que li apostemes ovri, et en corroient mout de matieres, et devint fistule, et i vint mout de pertus que tuit gitoient bowe et moistor dou cors;	 But the surgeons, due to their folly, worked so much on the abscess that it burst, and consumed a great deal of materials, becoming an ulcer, and brought about many discharges causing wetness throughout the body.
et maint mire i mirent cure entor II ans, et n’i ot nul saige en l’art de mains, tant que je i fui apelez, et vi sa jambe et les medicines dont on le curoit, et ceu que corroit par les pertus a grant cors;	 and many surgeons attempted to heal it for two years, without any skilled hand in the art of surgery, until I was called upon, and saw the leg and the remedies used on him, and what flowed through discharges into his body.
et devenoit rouges li cors dou jouvenceil, et avoit color citrine.	 and it became red on the youth's body, with a citrine hue.
Je boutai une tente en l’un de ces pertus, et puis cerchai toz les pertus, et trovai que li uns venoit encontre l’autre de toutes les parties de la jambe.	 I built a tent on one of these points, and then searched all the points, finding that each comes in opposition from all parts of the leg.
Je me hastai donques, et copai en l’un des pertus tant que je descovri une partie de l’os, et le trovai corrumput et perciet, et venoit li corruption jusc’a l’os dedens;	 So I proceeded, and examined one of the discharges until I discovered a part of the bone, which found it corroded and pierced, with infection reaching up to the inner bone.
je soiai ceu qui m’aparissoit de l’os corrumput, et cuidai qu’il n’i eust autre corruption, fuer que celi que je ostai;	 I knew those that appeared from the rotten bone, and thought there was no other decay except for what I removed.
et comensai a restourer la plaie de medicines sodans par lonc tens, et ne pot souder;	 And began to heal the wound with strong medicines over long periods, but could not close it up.
et puis rencomensai, et descovri l’os si com devant, et trovai la corruption continuee en l’os, et la soiai, et puis l’ostai, et me penai de souder le leu;	 Then I resumed my efforts and found the bone as before, discovered continuous decay in the bone, treated it again, removed more of it, and struggled to close up the wound.
mais je ne pou tant que je copai entor une palme de l’os, et le traï fuer a tout son mole, puis le restourai de medicines;	 But I could not completely remove even an inch of bone, and it betrayed me entirely in its depths, so I then reattempted with medicines.
et il fut sanez et soudez hastanment, et ne covint plus rencomencier l’ovraige fors por la foibleté dou malaide, qui ne pooit soffrir, et por la paour de mort que je avoie de lui.	 And it became safe and closed quickly, and I did not resume the treatment except due to the frailty of the patient who could not endure more, and out of fear for his impending death that I had for him.
Car por l’evacuation sanglotoit sovent, mais il fut sanez entierement, et nasquit en leu de l’os une char dure, et fut de bone disposition et n’ot point de nuisement ne de contraire dou tout en tout, ne a l’aleir ne a venir.	 For often the evacuation of blood was bloody, but he recovered completely, and in place of the bone there arose a hard cartilage, which was well-shaped and had no harm or drawback at all, neither on arrival nor departure.
Et se li os est brisiez en aucun leu dou cors, si le covient soier en ceste maniere:	 And if a bone is broken in any part of the body, it must thus be treated as follows:
pren I liien, et l’estrain au chief de l’os qui apert, et comande aucun k’il l’estende en haut;	 Take hold of the ligament, and stretch to the top of the broken bone shaft, and command that it be extended upwards.
et met I autre lien de lainne plus gros dou premier liien, et le lie sus la char qui est desor l’os, et estent le chief, si que tu traies la char corrumpue au desoz, et descuevre la char sus le leu ou tu vues soier, que li soie ne blece la char;	 And place another thicker ligament than the first, and tie it to the skin above the bone, then extend the shaft. As you pull the damaged cartilage away from below, expose the cartilage at the level where you aim to heal, so that it does not move with the tissue.
et met I tison ou une tauble desoz l’os por mues coper la char corrumpue;	 And place a needle or a small tablet below the bone to help move the damaged cartilage.
et covient tant soier com on puet veoir et sentir la corruption, et soier ancor autre fois.	 And you must treat until as much as can be seen and felt is healed, continuing treatment further if needed.
Et se li os est corrumpus, et n’apert mie, et li corruptions est en mileu ou en une partie, si descuevre la char toute;	 If the bone is corrupted and does not open, and the corruption is in a joint or part, then expose the entire fracture.
puis met I tison desoz, et puis soie des l’une partie a l’autre la corruption, et soit li soieure dou lonc de la corruption I poc, si com nos avons dit;	 Then place a heating pad on it and then move it from one part of the corruption to another, and let the stronger side be longer than the other end of the corruption, as we have said.
et se li corruptions est en la jointure, si cope la jointure corrumpue, et soie l’os ou elle contient de l’autre part;	 And if the corruption is in a joint, cut out the corrupted joint, and move the bone or its contents to another part.
et se li corruptions est en la continuation des II jointes, si n’i a autre angien que dou coper;	 If the corruption continues through two joints, there is no other remedy but double cutting.
et se li corruptions est ou poignil de la main, ou ou poignil dou piet, si est mout fort celle chose, mais toutevoie il covient que tu enquieres celle corrosion, coment elle t’apert;	 If the corruption is at a finger or toe joint, it may be quite severe, but you must inquire about that corruption and how it opens.
et la mundifie en toutes les manieres que tu pues, mais que li voine ou li nerf ne te faicent contraire;	 And clean it in all ways you can, but let neither vein nor nerve oppose you.
et saiches que li incisoire et les soies por coper ces os sont maintes, selonc l’assise des os et l’aparance d’ous, et lor grossece et lor subtiliteit, et lor grandor et lor petitece, et lor duresce;	 And choose the incisions and sutures for healing these bones are many, according to the position of the bones and their appearance, as well as their thickness and fineness, their size and smallness, and their hardness.
et por ceu covient il apareillier a chescune semblance d’ovraige son estrument;	 And therefore one must equip each type of procedure with its instrument.
et saiches que l’uevre te moustrera l’estrument dont tu avras mestier, selonc la conissance de cest art, et le tesmoignaige des manieres des maladies;	 And know that the work will show you the instrument of which you need, according to your knowledge of this art, and its guidance on the ways of diseases.
si porpense l’estrument dont tu as mestier selonc ceu qu’il le covient.	 If you consider the instrument you need, choose it according to what is fitting for it.
dou feu	By fire
Li chiés porrissent ou par cause dedens, ou par cause defuer;	 The head may dislocate or due to internal causes, or external factors.
et quant tu avras medicinee celle corrosion par la cure des medicines, et il ne profitent mie, si covient coper celui membre jusques au leu ou li corrosion vient, si que li malaides eschaipe par ceu de la mort, ou par la malice, qui est plus grans, de la defaute dou membre;	 And when you have administered the medicine for combating corrosion through medicinal treatment, and it proves ineffective, then cover that limb up to its original place where the corrosion occurs. So the patient may escape either by death or a worse fate due to the failure of the limb.
et li signes si est que li membres devient noir, si qu’il semble qu’il soit ars dou feu, et porrist aprés la noiror, pues va celle corrosions de membre em membre, et prent par tout le cors;	 And the signs are that the limb becomes black and appears as though it were scorched by fire. Afterwards, from this darkness follows the limb's corroding in one member to another throughout the body.
si te haste dou coper, et se c’est par la percussion d’aucunes venimouses bestes, si com scorpion de mer et wivre et semblans, se li corrosion est au chief dou doi, si le cope, et ne li doner mie espaice de venir jusc’a la main.	 If you quickly dress the wound, and if it is from a sting of venomous creatures such as scorpions, snakes, etc., and if the corrosion reaches the head of the elbow, then wrap it and do not give any space for it to reach up to the hand.

et s’elle vient au bras, si le cope au coute;	 And if it reaches the arm, then bind above the knee;
et s’elle passe le coute, c’est li mors, et n’i vaut amenistremens fuers que li quantitez de sa vertut;	 And if it passes below the knee, that's fatal, and no remedies can be effective other than in accordance with the extent of its power.
et tot ensi fai quant li corrosion vient ou piet:	 Do this as such whenever the corrosion appears or erupts:
s’elle vient en la premiere jointe, si la cope aprés l’autre jointe;	 If it occurs at the first joint, then proceed to the following joint.
et s’elle vient ou piet, si cope tout le piet;	 And if it comes near or on the arm, reset the entire arm.

et s’elle vient desus le genoil, si n’i a autre engien que dou lassier le malaide a mort;	 And if it comes over the groin, there is no other remedy but to behead the patient.

et je te conterai k’il avint a I home en som piet:	 And I will tell you what happened at a certain place in times past:
il li avint une noiror qui sembloit arsure de feu, et celle corrosion vint premier en son doi dou piet, tant qu’elle porprist tout le piet;	 It happened one night that it seemed like the glow of fire, and this corrosion began first in his right foot, so much so that it affected the entire foot.
